// Graph show/hide toggle (mobile)
var _graphHidden=false;
function toggleGraph(){
  _graphHidden=!_graphHidden;
  var mc=Q("main-content");
  var btn=Q("graph-toggle");
  if(_graphHidden){
    mc.classList.add("graph-hidden");
    if(btn)btn.textContent="Show Graph";
  }else{
    mc.classList.remove("graph-hidden");
    if(btn)btn.textContent="Hide Graph";
    setTimeout(function(){drawRelMap()},300);
  }
}

// Gateway uptime tracking
function updateGatewayDetails(){
  var det=Q("gw-details");if(!det)return;
  var gw=D.gateway||{};
  var gs=D.gatewayStatus||{};
  var host=gw.bind==="loopback"?"127.0.0.1":(gw.bind||"0.0.0.0");
  var ip=gs.host||gs.ip||gs.address||window.location.hostname||host;
  var port=gw.port||gs.port||window.location.port||"—";
  var ac=(D.agents||[]).length;
  // Preserve health warnings span content across rebuilds
  var existingHealth=det.querySelector("#gw-health-warns");
  det.innerHTML='<span>'+esc(ip)+':'+esc(port)+'</span><span>'+ac+' agent'+(ac!==1?'s':'')+'</span>';
}

// ── API key health check ──
var _healthIssues=[];
var _healthCheckTimer=null;
var _dismissedHealthFingerprint=""; // fingerprint of issues the user dismissed
try{_dismissedHealthFingerprint=sessionStorage.getItem("oc_dismissed_health")||""}catch(e){}
function _runHealthCheck(){
  api("health",{_quiet:true}).then(function(d){
    _healthIssues=d.issues||[];
    _renderHealthStatus();
    // Schedule next check in 5 minutes
    if(_healthCheckTimer)clearTimeout(_healthCheckTimer);
    _healthCheckTimer=setTimeout(_runHealthCheck,300000);
  }).catch(function(){});
}
function _renderHealthStatus(){
  if(!_healthIssues||_healthIssues.length===0){
    _hideKeyIssueBanner();
    return;
  }
  var invalid=_healthIssues.filter(function(i){return i.status==="invalid"});
  var limited=_healthIssues.filter(function(i){return i.status==="rate_limited"});
  var expired=_healthIssues.filter(function(i){return i.status==="expired"});
  var errors=_healthIssues.filter(function(i){return i.status==="error"&&i.provider!=="gateway"});

  // Show banner for invalid keys, expired tokens, or rate limits
  if(invalid.length>0||limited.length>0||expired.length>0){
    _showKeyIssueBanner(_healthIssues);
  }

  // Trigger model limit banner for rate limits
  if(limited.length>0&&!_modelLimitActive){
    var msgs=limited.map(function(i){return i.provider+": "+i.error});
    _showModelLimitBanner(msgs.join("; "));
  }
}
function _showKeyIssueBanner(issues){
  var existing=Q("key-issue-banner");
  if(existing)existing.remove();
  var invalid=issues.filter(function(i){return i.status==="invalid"});
  var limited=issues.filter(function(i){return i.status==="rate_limited"});
  var expired=issues.filter(function(i){return i.status==="expired"});
  if(invalid.length===0&&limited.length===0&&expired.length===0)return;

  // Build fingerprint of current issues — skip if user already dismissed this exact set
  var fp=issues.map(function(i){return i.provider+":"+i.status}).sort().join("|");
  if(fp===_dismissedHealthFingerprint)return;

  var b=document.createElement("div");b.id="key-issue-banner";
  b.className="oc-banner bottom warn-bg";
  var msgs=[];
  invalid.forEach(function(i){msgs.push('<span class="health-err">'+esc(i.provider)+': '+esc(i.error)+'</span>')});
  expired.forEach(function(i){msgs.push('<span class="health-warn">'+esc(i.provider)+': '+esc(i.error)+'</span>')});
  limited.forEach(function(i){msgs.push('<span class="health-warn">'+esc(i.provider)+': '+esc(i.error)+'</span>')});
  b.innerHTML='<div class="oc-banner-body">⚠ '+msgs.join(" · ")+'</div>'
    +'<div class="oc-banner-actions">'
    +'<button class="btn-banner primary" onclick="showProviderStatus()">View Details</button>'
    +'<button class="btn-banner ghost" onclick="_hideKeyIssueBanner()">Dismiss</button>'
    +'</div>';
  document.body.appendChild(b);
}
function _hideKeyIssueBanner(){
  var el=Q("key-issue-banner");
  if(el)el.remove();
  if(_healthIssues&&_healthIssues.length>0){
    _dismissedHealthFingerprint=_healthIssues.map(function(i){return i.provider+":"+i.status}).sort().join("|");
    try{sessionStorage.setItem("oc_dismissed_health",_dismissedHealthFingerprint)}catch(e){}
  }
}

// Responsive chart: re-render on resize so it scales and centers
var _resizeTimer=null;
window.addEventListener("resize",function(){
  clearTimeout(_resizeTimer);
  _resizeTimer=setTimeout(function(){
    if(D.agents&&D.agents.length>0&&!drawerAgent){drawRelMap()}
  },200);
});

var _apiInFlight=0;
function api(p,o){
  o=o||{};
  var quiet=o._quiet;delete o._quiet;
  if(!quiet){_apiInFlight++;_showProgress()}
  return fetch("/api/"+p,{headers:Object.assign({"Content-Type":"application/json"},o.headers||{}),method:o.method||"GET",body:o.body||undefined})
    .then(function(r){
      if(!quiet){_apiInFlight--;if(_apiInFlight<=0){_apiInFlight=0;_hideProgress()}}
      if(!r.ok)return r.json().catch(function(){return{}}).then(function(e){throw new Error(e.error||r.statusText)});
      return r.json();
    })
    .catch(function(e){
      if(!quiet){_apiInFlight--;if(_apiInFlight<=0){_apiInFlight=0;_hideProgress()}}
      throw e;
    });
}
function toast(m,t){t=t||"info";var e=document.createElement("div");e.className="toast toast-"+t;e.textContent=m;document.getElementById("toasts").appendChild(e);setTimeout(function(){e.remove()},3500)}
function esc(s){if(s==null)return"";var d=document.createElement("div");d.textContent=String(s);return d.innerHTML}
function openModal(t,h){document.getElementById("modal-title").textContent=t;document.getElementById("modal-body").innerHTML=h;document.getElementById("modal-bg").classList.add("open")}
function closeModal(){document.getElementById("modal-bg").classList.remove("open");var modalEl=document.querySelector("#modal-bg .modal");if(modalEl)modalEl.style.maxWidth="";_chatSessionKey=null;_cancelAllPollTimers()}

  var pp=document.getElementById("page-panel");
  var pb=document.getElementById("page-panel-body");
  var pt=document.getElementById("page-panel-title");
  var bk=document.getElementById("page-panel-backdrop");
  if(!pp||!pb||!pt)return;
  pt.textContent=title;
  pb.innerHTML=h;
  pp.classList.add("open");
  if(bk)bk.classList.add("open");
}
function closePagePanel(){
  var pp=document.getElementById("page-panel");
  var bk=document.getElementById("page-panel-backdrop");
  if(pp)pp.classList.remove("open");
  if(bk)bk.classList.remove("open");
  if(location.hash)history.replaceState(null,"",location.pathname);
}
function fmtDate(d){if(!d)return"N/A";try{return new Date(d).toLocaleString()}catch(e){return String(d)}}
function fmtTime(d){if(!d)return"";try{var dt=new Date(d);var now=new Date();var sameDay=dt.toDateString()===now.toDateString();return sameDay?dt.toLocaleTimeString([],{hour:"2-digit",minute:"2-digit"}):dt.toLocaleDateString([],{month:"short",day:"numeric"})+" "+dt.toLocaleTimeString([],{hour:"2-digit",minute:"2-digit"})}catch(e){return""}}
function getModel(a){if(!a.model)return"";if(typeof a.model==="string")return a.model;return a.model.primary||""}
function getFallbacks(a){if(!a.model||typeof a.model==="string")return[];return a.model.fallbacks||[]}
function getSubs(a){return(a.subagents&&a.subagents.allowAgents)||[]}
function getPeers(a){var t=D.config&&D.config.tools&&D.config.tools.agentToAgent;return(t&&t.allow)||[]}
function getToolProfile(a){return(a.tools&&a.tools.profile)||""}
function getToolAlso(a){var t=a.tools||{};return t.alsoAllow||t.allow||[]}
function getToolDeny(a){return(a.tools&&a.tools.deny)||[]}
function Q(id){return document.getElementById(id)}
function V(id){var e=Q(id);return e?e.value:""}
function CK(id){var e=Q(id);return e?e.checked:false}
function agentColor(agentId){
  var ids=(D.agents||[]).map(function(a){return a.id});
  var idx=ids.indexOf(agentId);
  return AGENT_COLORS[idx%AGENT_COLORS.length];
}
function agentToneClass(agentId){
  var ids=(D.agents||[]).map(function(a){return a.id});
  var idx=ids.indexOf(agentId);
  if(idx<0)idx=0;
  return "agent-tone-"+(idx%AGENT_COLORS.length);
}
// Returns list of defined model aliases from agents.defaults.models
function getModelAliases(){
  var m=D.config&&D.config.agents&&D.config.agents.defaults&&D.config.agents.defaults.models;
  if(!m)return[];
  return Object.values(m).map(function(v){return v.alias}).filter(Boolean);
}
// Returns map of alias -> "provider/modelId"
function getModelAliasMap(){
  var m=D.config&&D.config.agents&&D.config.agents.defaults&&D.config.agents.defaults.models;
  if(!m)return{};
  var out={};
  Object.keys(m).forEach(function(k){if(m[k].alias)out[m[k].alias]=k});
  return out;
}
// Tooltip helper: renders a label with an info icon
function tip(labelText,tipText){
  return '<label class="lbl">'+esc(labelText)
    +'<i class="tip-icon" data-tip="'+esc(tipText)+'">?</i>'
    +'</label>';
}
// Model select: shows defined aliases + free-text fallback
// Also fetches available providers/models from API status for discovery
var _providerModels=null; // cached {provider:[model1,model2,...]}
var _providerModelsFetching=false;
function fetchProviderModels(cb){
  if(_providerModels){if(cb)cb(_providerModels);return}
  if(_providerModelsFetching)return;
  _providerModelsFetching=true;
  api("models/status").then(function(d){
    var pm={};
    (d.providers||[]).forEach(function(p){
      var name=(p.provider||"").toLowerCase().replace(/\s+/g,"-");
      if(name&&p.status==="ok")pm[name]=(p.models||[]).slice();
    });
    (d.oauth||[]).forEach(function(c){
      if(c.status!=="connected")return;
      var name=(c.name||"").toLowerCase().replace(/\s+/g,"-");
      if(!pm[name])pm[name]=[];
      var qm=c.quota&&(c.quota.models||c.quota.localModels)||[];
      qm.forEach(function(m){if(pm[name].indexOf(m)<0)pm[name].push(m)});
    });
    _providerModels=pm;
    _providerModelsFetching=false;
    if(cb)cb(pm);
  }).catch(function(){_providerModelsFetching=false;if(cb)cb({})});
}
function modelSelect(id,currentVal,placeholder){
  var aliases=getModelAliases();
  var aliasMap=getModelAliasMap();
  // Parse current value: could be alias or "provider/model"
  var curAlias="",curProvider="",curModel="";
  if(currentVal){
    if(aliases.indexOf(currentVal)>=0){
      curAlias=currentVal;
      var full=aliasMap[currentVal]||"";
      if(full.indexOf("/")>-1){curProvider=full.split("/")[0];curModel=full.split("/").slice(1).join("/")}
    }else if(currentVal.indexOf("/")>-1){
      curProvider=currentVal.split("/")[0];curModel=currentVal.split("/").slice(1).join("/");
    }else{
      curAlias=currentVal;
    }
  }
  var h='<div class="model-sel-wrap" id="'+id+'-wrap">';
  // Alias dropdown (if aliases exist)
  if(aliases.length>0){
    h+='<select id="'+id+'" onchange="onModelAliasChange(\''+id+'\')" class="model-alias-select">';
    h+='<option value="">— select alias —</option>';
    aliases.forEach(function(a){
      var full=aliasMap[a]||"";
      h+='<option value="'+esc(a)+'"'+(curAlias===a?" selected":"")+'>'+esc(a)+(full?' ('+esc(full)+')':'')+'</option>';
    });
    h+='<option value="__custom__"'+(currentVal&&!curAlias?" selected":"")+'>✏ custom provider/model…</option>';
    h+='</select>';
  }
  // Provider + Model dropdowns (shown when custom or no aliases)
  var showCustom=aliases.length===0||(currentVal&&!curAlias);
  h+='<div id="'+id+'-custom-row" class="model-custom-row'+(showCustom?'':' is-hidden')+'">';
  h+='<div class="model-custom-col"><label class="lbl mb-sm">Provider</label>';
  h+='<select id="'+id+'-provider" onchange="onProviderChange(\''+id+'\')">';
  h+='<option value="">Loading…</option>';
  h+='</select></div>';
  h+='<div class="model-custom-col"><label class="lbl mb-sm">Model</label>';
  h+='<select id="'+id+'-model" onchange="onModelSelectChange(\''+id+'\')">';
  h+='<option value="">Select provider first</option>';
  h+='</select>';
  h+='<input id="'+id+'-model-custom" placeholder="enter custom model ID" value="'+esc(curModel)+'" class="model-custom-input is-hidden" /></div>';
  h+='</div></div>';
  // Populate provider/model dropdowns after render
  setTimeout(function(){populateProviderDropdowns(id,curProvider,curModel)},0);
  return h;
}
function populateProviderDropdowns(id,curProvider,curModel){
  fetchProviderModels(function(pm){
    var provSel=Q(id+"-provider");
    if(!provSel)return;
    var providers=Object.keys(pm).sort();
    var h='<option value="">— select provider —</option>';
    providers.forEach(function(p){
      h+='<option value="'+esc(p)+'"'+(curProvider===p?" selected":"")+'>'+esc(p)+'</option>';
    });
    h+='<option value="__custom__"'+(curProvider&&providers.indexOf(curProvider)<0?" selected":"")+'>✏ custom…</option>';
    provSel.innerHTML=h;
    // If custom provider not in list, show it
    if(curProvider&&providers.indexOf(curProvider)<0){
      var wrap=provSel.parentNode;
      var existing=wrap.querySelector(".prov-custom-input");
      if(!existing){
        var inp=document.createElement("input");
        inp.id=id+"-provider-custom";inp.className="prov-custom-input";
        inp.value=curProvider;inp.placeholder="provider name";
        wrap.appendChild(inp);
      }
    }
    if(curProvider)onProviderChange(id,curModel);
  });
}
function onModelAliasChange(id){
  var sel=V(id);
  var row=Q(id+"-custom-row");
  if(!row)return;
  if(sel==="__custom__"){
    row.classList.remove("is-hidden");
  }else{
    row.classList.add("is-hidden");
  }
}
function onProviderChange(id,preselect){
  var provSel=Q(id+"-provider");
  var modelSel=Q(id+"-model");
  var modelCustom=Q(id+"-model-custom");
  if(!provSel||!modelSel)return;
  var prov=provSel.value;
  // Handle custom provider input
  var wrap=provSel.parentNode;
  var customInp=wrap.querySelector(".prov-custom-input");
  if(prov==="__custom__"){
    if(!customInp){
      customInp=document.createElement("input");
      customInp.id=id+"-provider-custom";customInp.className="prov-custom-input";
      customInp.placeholder="provider name";
      wrap.appendChild(customInp);
    }
    modelSel.innerHTML='<option value="">Type model ID below</option>';
    if(modelCustom){modelCustom.classList.remove("is-hidden");modelCustom.placeholder="enter custom model ID"}
    return;
  }else if(customInp){
    customInp.remove();
  }
  var pm=_providerModels||{};
  var models=pm[prov]||[];
  var pre=preselect||"";
  var h='<option value="">— select model —</option>';
  models.forEach(function(m){
    h+='<option value="'+esc(m)+'"'+(pre===m?" selected":"")+'>'+esc(m)+'</option>';
  });
  h+='<option value="__custom__">✏ other…</option>';
  modelSel.innerHTML=h;
  if(modelCustom){modelCustom.classList.add("is-hidden");modelCustom.value=""}
  // If preselect was set and not in list, show custom input
  if(pre&&models.indexOf(pre)<0){
    modelSel.value="__custom__";
    if(modelCustom){modelCustom.classList.remove("is-hidden");modelCustom.value=pre}
  }
}
function onModelSelectChange(id){
  var modelSel=Q(id+"-model");
  var modelCustom=Q(id+"-model-custom");
  if(!modelSel||!modelCustom)return;
  if(modelSel.value==="__custom__"){
    modelCustom.classList.remove("is-hidden");
    modelCustom.focus();
  }else{
    modelCustom.classList.add("is-hidden");
    modelCustom.value="";
  }
}
function getModelVal(id){
  var aliases=getModelAliases();
  // If alias dropdown exists and has a non-custom value, use it
  var aliasSel=Q(id);
  if(aliasSel&&aliasSel.tagName==="SELECT"){
    var sel=aliasSel.value;
    if(sel&&sel!=="__custom__")return sel;
  }
  // Custom: build provider/model
  var prov=V(id+"-provider");
  if(prov==="__custom__")prov=V(id+"-provider-custom").trim();
  var model=V(id+"-model");
  if(model==="__custom__")model="";
  var modelCustom=V(id+"-model-custom").trim();
  var finalModel=model||modelCustom;
  if(prov&&finalModel)return prov+"/"+finalModel;
  if(finalModel)return finalModel;
  if(prov)return prov;
  // Fallback: plain input (no aliases case)
  return V(id).trim();
}

// ── Graph caching layer ──
// Fingerprint agents+bindings+channels so we skip expensive graph re-render when nothing changed.
var _graphFingerprint="";
var _GRAPH_VERSION="v32"; // bump to invalidate localStorage graph cache after code changes
function _computeGraphFingerprint(agents,bindings,channels){
  // Deterministic JSON of the fields that affect the graph layout
  var pe=D.config&&D.config.plugins&&D.config.plugins.entries||{};
  var infraKey=Object.keys(pe).filter(function(k){return pe[k]&&pe[k].enabled!==false&&(k==="memory-lancedb"||k==="openclaw-mem0"||k==="mem0"||k==="lossless-claw")}).join(",");
  var data=_GRAPH_VERSION+infraKey+JSON.stringify({
    a:(agents||[]).map(function(a){return{id:a.id,name:a.name,icon:a.icon,"default":a["default"],model:a.model,hb:a.heartbeat,subs:getSubs(a),peers:getPeers(a),orch:getToolAlso(a).indexOf("run_task_flow")>-1}}),
    b:(bindings||[]).map(function(b){return{agentId:b.agentId,channel:b.match&&b.match.channel}}),
    c:channels||{}
  });
  // Simple djb2 hash — fast, good enough for change detection
  var h=5381;
  for(var i=0;i<data.length;i++){h=((h<<5)+h+data.charCodeAt(i))>>>0}
  return h.toString(36);
}
function _cacheGraph(){
  try{
    var canvas=Q("map-canvas");if(!canvas)return;
    var layer=Q("rel-layer");if(!layer)return;
    localStorage.setItem("oc_graph_html",layer.outerHTML);
    localStorage.setItem("oc_graph_fp",_graphFingerprint);
    localStorage.setItem("oc_graph_scale",String(mapScale));
    localStorage.setItem("oc_graph_ox",String(mapOffX));
    localStorage.setItem("oc_graph_oy",String(mapOffY));
  }catch(e){}
}
function _restoreGraphCache(){
  try{
    var cached=localStorage.getItem("oc_graph_html");
    var fp=localStorage.getItem("oc_graph_fp");
    if(!cached||!fp||fp!==_graphFingerprint)return false;
    var canvas=Q("map-canvas");if(!canvas)return false;
    var zc=Q("zoom-controls");
    canvas.innerHTML="";
    if(zc)canvas.appendChild(zc);
    var tmp=document.createElement("div");
    tmp.innerHTML=cached;
    var layer=tmp.firstChild;
    if(layer){
      canvas.appendChild(layer);
      mapScale=Math.min(1.1,parseFloat(localStorage.getItem("oc_graph_scale"))||1);
      mapOffX=parseFloat(localStorage.getItem("oc_graph_ox"))||0;
      mapOffY=parseFloat(localStorage.getItem("oc_graph_oy"))||0;
      // Re-attach event listeners (pan, click, hover) since innerHTML strips them
      setupMapPan(canvas);
      _reattachNodeListeners(canvas);
      var lbl=Q("zoom-label");if(lbl)lbl.textContent=Math.round(mapScale*100)+"%";
    }
    return true;
  }catch(e){return false}
}
function _reattachNodeListeners(canvas){
  // Agent nodes
  canvas.querySelectorAll(".rn").forEach(function(n){
    var id=n.getAttribute("data-id");
    var a=null;
    for(var i=0;i<(D.agents||[]).length;i++){if(D.agents[i].id===id){a=D.agents[i];break}}
    if(!a)return;
    var col=agentColor(id);
    var delBtn=n.querySelector(".rn-delete");
    if(delBtn){
      delBtn.addEventListener("click",function(e){
        e.preventDefault();
        e.stopPropagation();
        deleteAgent(a.id);
      });
    }
    n.addEventListener("mouseenter",function(){n.classList.add("hovered")});
    n.addEventListener("mouseleave",function(){n.classList.remove("hovered")});
    n.addEventListener("click",function(e){
      if(e.target&&e.target.closest&&e.target.closest(".rn-delete"))return;
      openDrawer(a,"sessions");
    });
  });
  // Channel nodes
  canvas.querySelectorAll(".chn-wrap").forEach(function(wrap){
    wrap.addEventListener("click",function(e){
      e.stopPropagation();
      if(wrap.classList.contains("infra-wrap"))showRawConfig();
      else showChannelsPage();
    });
  });
}

// Workflow cache removed — using custom SVG instead of mermaid
// Invalidate all caches and force re-render of main graph + current workflow
function _invalidateAndRedraw(){
  // Clear localStorage graph cache so drawRelMap renders fresh
  try{localStorage.removeItem("oc_graph_html");localStorage.removeItem("oc_graph_fp")}catch(e){}
  _graphFingerprint="";
  _graphFingerprint=_computeGraphFingerprint(D.agents,D.bindings,D.channels);
  drawRelMap();
  _cacheGraph();
  renderAgentList();
  // If a drawer is open, re-render the agent list
  if(drawerAgent){
    renderAgentList();
  }
}

function _refreshEffectiveUi(){
  var newFp=_computeGraphFingerprint(D.agents,D.bindings,D.channels);
  var fpChanged=newFp!==_graphFingerprint;
  _graphFingerprint=newFp;
  updateGatewayDetails();
  if(fpChanged){
    render();
    _cacheGraph();
  }
  if(Q("channels-body"))renderChannelsPage();
  if(drawerAgent&&drawerTab==="channels")renderDrawer();
}

function _setEffectiveConfig(config){
  D.config=config||{};
  D.channels=(D.config&&D.config.channels)||{};
}

function _loadEffectiveConfig(opts){
  opts=opts||{};
  return api("config",opts._quiet?{_quiet:true}:{}).then(function(r){
    if(r&&r.config)_setEffectiveConfig(r.config);
    return r&&r.config?r.config:null;
  });
}

function _getVisibleChannels(){
  var merged={};
  Object.keys(D.channels||{}).forEach(function(name){
    merged[name]=JSON.parse(JSON.stringify((D.channels||{})[name]||{}));
  });
  if(Object.keys(merged).length===0){
    (D.bindings||[]).forEach(function(b){
      var ch=b&&b.match&&b.match.channel;
      if(!ch)return;
      if(!merged[ch])merged[ch]={enabled:true,accounts:{}};
      if(!merged[ch].accounts)merged[ch].accounts={};
    });
  }
  return merged;
}

function _setEffectiveBindings(bindings){
  D.bindings=bindings||[];
}

var _initialLoadDone=false;
function load(opts){
  opts=opts||{};
  var fast=opts.fast;
  var quiet=opts._quiet;
  var endpoint=fast?"overview?fast=1":"overview";
  var myGen=++_loadGen;
  api(endpoint,quiet?{_quiet:true}:{}).then(function(d){
    if(myGen!==_loadGen)return; // stale response — newer load already in flight
    D=d;
    if(!D.channels)D.channels=(D.config&&D.config.channels)||{};
    _initialLoadDone=true;
    _enableNav();
    // Check for model limit errors in gateway status
    var gs=d.gatewayStatus||{};
    var gsErr=gs.error||gs.lastError||"";
    if(gsErr&&_isRateLimitError(gsErr)&&!_modelLimitActive){
      _showModelLimitBanner(gsErr);
    }
    if(!_modelLimitActive){
      Q("gw-status").className="gw-badge ok";
      Q("gw-status").textContent="\u25cf Gateway Online";
    }
    updateGatewayDetails();
    var newFp=_computeGraphFingerprint(d.agents,d.bindings,D.channels);
    var fpChanged=newFp!==_graphFingerprint;
    _graphFingerprint=newFp;
    if(!fpChanged&&_restoreGraphCache()){
      renderAgentList();
    }else{
      render();
      _cacheGraph();
    }
    if(drawerAgent){
      var fresh=null;
      for(var i=0;i<D.agents.length;i++){if(D.agents[i].id===drawerAgent.id){fresh=D.agents[i];break}}
      if(fresh)openDrawer(fresh,drawerTab);
    }
    if(Q("channels-body"))renderChannelsPage();
    // After fast load paints the UI, kick off deferred work
    if(fast){
      setTimeout(function(){
        fetchProviderModels();
        _loadToolRegistry(false);
        // Full load in background to get sessions, md files, gateway status
        load({_quiet:true});
        // Run health check after a short delay to not compete with the full load
        setTimeout(_runHealthCheck,2000);
        // Check for pending config changes
        _checkPendingOnLoad();
        // Restore page from URL hash on first load
        _restoreFromHash();
      },50);
    }else{
      fetchProviderModels();
      _loadToolRegistry(false);
    }
  }).catch(function(){
    if(myGen!==_loadGen)return; // stale response — newer load already in flight
    Q("gw-status").className="gw-badge err";
    Q("gw-status").textContent="\u25cb Gateway Error";
    var det=Q("gw-details");if(det)det.innerHTML="";
    D.agents=[];render();
    _initialLoadDone=true;
    _enableNav();
  });
}
function _disableNav(){
  var btns=document.querySelectorAll("#topbar .btn, .hamburger-btn");
  btns.forEach(function(b){b.setAttribute("disabled","true");b.classList.add("nav-disabled")});
  var items=document.querySelectorAll(".agent-list-item");
  items.forEach(function(i){i.classList.add("nav-disabled")});
}
function _enableNav(){
  var btns=document.querySelectorAll("#topbar .btn, .hamburger-btn");
  btns.forEach(function(b){b.removeAttribute("disabled");b.classList.remove("nav-disabled")});
  var items=document.querySelectorAll(".agent-list-item");
  items.forEach(function(i){i.classList.remove("nav-disabled")});
}

function showRawConfigForRepair(){
  api("config/raw").then(function(d){
    var raw=d.raw||"{}";
    openFsEditorDirect("Fix Configuration (Raw JSON)",raw,true,function(newVal){
      api("config?defer=1",{method:"PUT",body:JSON.stringify({raw:newVal})}).then(function(r){
        _closeFsOverlay();
        if(r.error){toast(r.error,"err");return}
        toast("Config saved — reloading…","ok");
        load();_deferRestart("Config saved");
      }).catch(function(e){_closeFsOverlay();toast(e.message,"err")});
    });
  }).catch(function(e){toast("Failed to load raw config: "+e.message,"err")});
}

function buildRelGraph(){
  var edges=[];
  // Delegation edges
  (D.agents||[]).forEach(function(a){
    getSubs(a).forEach(function(tid,idx){
      edges.push({from:a.id,to:tid,type:"delegates",label:"delegates",subIdx:idx});
    });
  });
  // A2A peer edges (global — bidirectional, only add once per pair)
  var peerSeen={};
  var globalPeers=getPeers();
  for(var pi=0;pi<globalPeers.length;pi++){
    for(var pj=pi+1;pj<globalPeers.length;pj++){
      var key=[globalPeers[pi],globalPeers[pj]].sort().join("||");
      if(!peerSeen[key]){
        peerSeen[key]=true;
        edges.push({from:globalPeers[pi],to:globalPeers[pj],type:"peer",label:"a2a peer"});
      }
    }
  }
  // Channel binding edges — agent → channel node (virtual node id = "ch:discord" etc)
  var bi=D.bindings||[];
  bi.forEach(function(b){
    if(!b.agentId||!b.match||!b.match.channel)return;
    var chId="ch:"+b.match.channel;
    // avoid duplicate edges for same agent+channel
    var exists=edges.some(function(e){return e.from===b.agentId&&e.to===chId});
    if(!exists)edges.push({from:b.agentId,to:chId,type:"channel",label:b.match.channel});
  });
  return edges;
}

// Returns virtual channel nodes derived from bindings
function buildChannelNodes(){
  var seen={};
  var CH_ICONS={whatsapp:"💬",telegram:"✈️",discord:"🎮",slack:"💼",signal:"🔒",matrix:"🔷",webchat:"🌐",irc:"📡"};
  (D.bindings||[]).forEach(function(b){
    if(!b.match||!b.match.channel)return;
    var ch=b.match.channel;
    if(!seen[ch])seen[ch]={id:"ch:"+ch,name:ch,icon:CH_ICONS[ch]||"📻",isChannel:true};
  });
  return Object.values(seen);
}


function render(){
  var m=Q("map-canvas");
  if(!m)return;
  if(!D.agents||D.agents.length===0){
    var zc0=Q("zoom-controls");
    m.innerHTML='<div class="empty map-empty-center"><div class="empty-icon">🦞</div>No agents configured.<br><span class="section-desc">Or refresh the page — connection to server may have been lost.</span><br><br><button class="btn btn-accent" onclick="showCreateAgent()">Create Agent</button></div>';
    if(zc0)m.appendChild(zc0);
    renderAgentList();
    return;
  }
  drawRelMap();
  renderAgentList();
}

function renderAgentList(){
  var body=Q("agent-list-body");if(!body)return;
  var agents=D.agents||[];
  if(agents.length===0){body.innerHTML='<div class="agent-list-empty">No agents</div>';return}
  var peers=getPeers();
  var h="";
  agents.forEach(function(a){
    var icon=agentIcon(a);
    var model=getModel(a);
    var isActive=drawerAgent&&drawerAgent.id===a.id;
    var isPeer=peers.indexOf(a.id)>-1;
    h+='<div class="agent-list-item'+(isActive?' active':'')+'" onclick="openDrawer(D.agents.find(function(x){return x.id===\''+esc(a.id)+'\'}),\'sessions\')">';
    h+='<span class="agent-list-icon">'+icon+'</span>';
    h+='<div class="agent-list-info">';
    h+='<div class="agent-list-name">'+esc(a.name||a.id)+'</div>';
    h+='<div class="agent-list-meta">'+(model?esc(model):'no model')+(a["default"]?' · default':'')+'</div>';
    h+='</div>';
    if(isPeer){
      h+='<div class="agent-list-dot peer" title="A2A Peer"></div>';
    }else{
      h+='<div class="agent-list-dot idle"></div>';
    }
    h+='</div>';
  });
  body.innerHTML=h;
}

// ── Zoom / Pan ──
function zoomMap(delta){
  mapScale=Math.max(0.25,Math.min(4,mapScale+delta));
  var lbl=Q("zoom-label");if(lbl)lbl.textContent=Math.round(mapScale*100)+"%";
  redrawMap();
}
function resetMapView(){mapScale=1;mapOffX=0;mapOffY=0;var lbl=Q("zoom-label");if(lbl)lbl.textContent="100%";drawRelMap();}
function refreshGraphCache(){try{localStorage.removeItem("oc_graph_html");localStorage.removeItem("oc_graph_fp")}catch(e){}_graphFingerprint="";drawRelMap();toast("Graph cache cleared","ok");}
function redrawMap(){
  var layer=Q("rel-layer");if(!layer)return;
  layer.style.transform="translate("+mapOffX+"px,"+mapOffY+"px) scale("+mapScale+")";
}
function setupMapPan(canvas){
  canvas.addEventListener("mousedown",function(e){
    if(e.target.closest&&(e.target.closest(".rn")||e.target.closest(".chn")))return;
    panStart={x:e.clientX-mapOffX,y:e.clientY-mapOffY};
    canvas.classList.add("panning");
    function onMove(ev){if(!panStart)return;mapOffX=ev.clientX-panStart.x;mapOffY=ev.clientY-panStart.y;redrawMap()}
    function onUp(){panStart=null;canvas.classList.remove("panning");document.removeEventListener("mousemove",onMove);document.removeEventListener("mouseup",onUp)}
    document.addEventListener("mousemove",onMove);document.addEventListener("mouseup",onUp);
  });
  // Touch pan support for mobile
  var _pinchStartDist=0,_pinchStartScale=1;
  canvas.addEventListener("touchstart",function(e){
    if(e.touches.length===2){
      // Pinch start
      var dx=e.touches[0].clientX-e.touches[1].clientX;
      var dy=e.touches[0].clientY-e.touches[1].clientY;
      _pinchStartDist=Math.sqrt(dx*dx+dy*dy);
      _pinchStartScale=mapScale;
      panStart=null;
      return;
    }
    if(e.touches.length!==1)return;
    var t=e.touches[0];
    if(e.target.closest&&(e.target.closest(".rn")||e.target.closest(".chn")))return;
    panStart={x:t.clientX-mapOffX,y:t.clientY-mapOffY};
    canvas.classList.add("panning");
  },{passive:true});
  canvas.addEventListener("touchmove",function(e){
    if(e.touches.length===2&&_pinchStartDist>0){
      // Pinch zoom
      e.preventDefault();
      var dx=e.touches[0].clientX-e.touches[1].clientX;
      var dy=e.touches[0].clientY-e.touches[1].clientY;
      var dist=Math.sqrt(dx*dx+dy*dy);
      var ratio=dist/_pinchStartDist;
      var prev=mapScale;
      mapScale=Math.max(0.2,Math.min(5,_pinchStartScale*ratio));
      // Zoom toward pinch center
      var cr=canvas.getBoundingClientRect();
      var cx=(e.touches[0].clientX+e.touches[1].clientX)/2-cr.left;
      var cy=(e.touches[0].clientY+e.touches[1].clientY)/2-cr.top;
      mapOffX=cx-(cx-mapOffX)*(mapScale/prev);
      mapOffY=cy-(cy-mapOffY)*(mapScale/prev);
      var lbl=Q("zoom-label");if(lbl)lbl.textContent=Math.round(mapScale*100)+"%";
      redrawMap();
      return;
    }
    if(!panStart||e.touches.length!==1)return;
    e.preventDefault();
    var t=e.touches[0];
    mapOffX=t.clientX-panStart.x;mapOffY=t.clientY-panStart.y;redrawMap();
  },{passive:false});
  canvas.addEventListener("touchend",function(e){
    if(e.touches.length<2)_pinchStartDist=0;
    if(e.touches.length===0){panStart=null;canvas.classList.remove("panning")}
  });
  canvas.addEventListener("wheel",function(e){
    e.preventDefault();
    // Scale factor proportional to current zoom (feels linear) and clamped for smoothness
    var raw=e.deltaY;
    var step=Math.min(Math.abs(raw),100)/100*0.08;
    var d=raw>0?-step:step;
    var cr=canvas.getBoundingClientRect();
    var mx=e.clientX-cr.left,my=e.clientY-cr.top,prev=mapScale;
    mapScale=Math.max(0.2,Math.min(5,mapScale*(1+d)));
    mapOffX=mx-(mx-mapOffX)*(mapScale/prev);
    mapOffY=my-(my-mapOffY)*(mapScale/prev);
    var lbl=Q("zoom-label");if(lbl)lbl.textContent=Math.round(mapScale*100)+"%";
    redrawMap();
  },{passive:false});
}

// Measure text width using a hidden canvas context
var _measureCtx=null;
function measureText(text,font){
  if(!_measureCtx){var c=document.createElement("canvas");_measureCtx=c.getContext("2d")}
  _measureCtx.font=font||graphFont(14,"700");
  return _measureCtx.measureText(text).width;
}

// Graph typography follows the shared token scale so canvas text tracks panel text.
var _graphTypography=null;
function _resolveGraphTypography(){
  var key=(window.innerWidth||0)+"x"+(window.innerHeight||0);
  if(_graphTypography&&_graphTypography._k===key)return _graphTypography;
  var fallback={name:14,model:13,channel:12,infra:13,peer:12,icon:16};
  if(!document.body)return fallback;
  var probe=document.createElement("span");
  probe.style.cssText="position:absolute;left:-9999px;top:-9999px;visibility:hidden;white-space:nowrap;pointer-events:none";
  probe.textContent="M";
  document.body.appendChild(probe);
  function px(cls){probe.className=cls;return parseFloat(getComputedStyle(probe).fontSize)||fallback.name;}
  _graphTypography={
    name:px("text-body-sm"),
    model:px("text-meta"),
    channel:px("text-badge"),
    infra:px("text-body-sm"),
    peer:px("text-meta"),
    icon:px("text-icon")
  };
  _graphTypography._k=key;
  probe.remove();
  return _graphTypography;
}
function graphFont(size,weight){return (weight||"600")+" "+size+"px -apple-system,BlinkMacSystemFont,sans-serif";}

// Agent icon helper — returns custom icon or default
function agentIcon(a){return a.icon||"🤖"}

function drawRelMap(){
  var canvas=Q("map-canvas");if(!canvas)return;
  var agents=D.agents||[],edges=buildRelGraph(),chNodes=buildChannelNodes();
  var W=Math.min(canvas.offsetWidth||window.innerWidth,window.innerWidth);
  var H=canvas.offsetHeight||400;
  var GT=_resolveGraphTypography();
  if(agents.length===0)return;

  // ── Constants ──
  var FONT_SIZE=GT.name,PAD_H=26,PAD_V=14,ICON_H=18,LINE_H=Math.max(16,Math.round(GT.model)+3);
  var CH_FONT=GT.channel,CH_PAD_H=22,CH_PAD_V=12,CH_H=Math.round(CH_FONT)+CH_PAD_V*2+4;
  var TITLE_FONT=graphFont(GT.name,"700");
  var HB_FONT=graphFont(GT.model,"400");
  var CH_FONT_STR=graphFont(CH_FONT,"600");
  var INFRA_FONT=graphFont(GT.infra,"600");
  var isMobileViewport=W<600;
  var PADX=50,PADY=60,MARGIN=isMobileViewport?16:40;

  // ── Measure nodes ──
  // Build agent → channel map for badge height calculation
  var agentChMap={};
  (D.bindings||[]).forEach(function(b){
    if(!b.agentId||!b.match||!b.match.channel)return;
    if(!agentChMap[b.agentId])agentChMap[b.agentId]={};
    agentChMap[b.agentId][b.match.channel]=true;
  });
  var nodeWidths={},nodeHeights={};
  agents.forEach(function(a){
    var label=a.name||a.id;
    var tw=measureText(label,TITLE_FONT);
    var nw=Math.max(120,Math.round(tw+PAD_H*2));
    // Widen card if heartbeat text is longer than the name
    var hb=a.heartbeat||{};
    if(hb.every){
      var hbText="♡ "+hb.every+(hb.model?" · "+hb.model:"");
      var hbW=measureText(hbText,HB_FONT);
      var maxHbW=280;// cap so cards don't get absurdly wide
      nw=Math.max(nw,Math.min(Math.round(hbW+PAD_H*2),maxHbW));
    }
    nodeWidths[a.id]=nw;
    var extraLines=0;
    if(getModel(a))extraLines++;
    if(a.heartbeat&&a.heartbeat.every)extraLines++;
    if(a["default"])extraLines++;
    if(agentChMap[a.id])extraLines++;// channel badge row
    nodeHeights[a.id]=ICON_H+FONT_SIZE+PAD_V*2+extraLines*(LINE_H+3)+16;
  });
  var NH=Math.max.apply(null,Object.values(nodeHeights).concat([70]));
  var chWidths={};
  chNodes.forEach(function(ch){
    var tw=measureText(ch.name,CH_FONT_STR);
    chWidths[ch.id]=Math.max(80,Math.round(tw+CH_PAD_H*2+28));
  });

  // ── Build edge index & detect bidirectional edges ──
  var peerSet={};
  getPeers().forEach(function(id){peerSet[id]=true});

  // Collect delegation edges, merging bidirectional into one
  var delEdges=[];
  var delMap={};
  edges.forEach(function(e){
    if(e.type!=="delegates")return;
    var fwd=e.from+"->"+e.to;
    var rev=e.to+"->"+e.from;
    if(delMap[rev]!==undefined){
      delEdges[delMap[rev]].bidir=true;
    }else{
      delMap[fwd]=delEdges.length;
      delEdges.push({from:e.from,to:e.to,bidir:false});
    }
  });

  // ── Hierarchical layering ──
  var children={},parents={};
  agents.forEach(function(a){children[a.id]=[];parents[a.id]=[]});
  delEdges.forEach(function(e){
    if(e.bidir)return;
    if(peerSet[e.from]&&peerSet[e.to])return;
    children[e.from].push(e.to);
    parents[e.to].push(e.from);
  });

  var layerOf={};
  var roots=agents.filter(function(a){return parents[a.id].length===0}).map(function(a){return a.id});
  if(!roots.length){
    var sorted=agents.slice().sort(function(a,b){return parents[a.id].length-parents[b.id].length});
    roots=[sorted[0].id];
  }
  var bfsQ=roots.slice();
  roots.forEach(function(id){layerOf[id]=0});
  var vis={};
  while(bfsQ.length){
    var cur=bfsQ.shift();
    if(vis[cur])continue;vis[cur]=true;
    (children[cur]||[]).forEach(function(c){
      if(vis[c])return;
      var nl=(layerOf[cur]||0)+1;
      if(layerOf[c]===undefined||layerOf[c]<nl)layerOf[c]=nl;
      bfsQ.push(c);
    });
  }
  agents.forEach(function(a){if(layerOf[a.id]===undefined)layerOf[a.id]=0});

  // Promote bidirectional partners to the same layer
  delEdges.forEach(function(e){
    if(!e.bidir)return;
    var minL=Math.min(layerOf[e.from],layerOf[e.to]);
    layerOf[e.from]=minL;layerOf[e.to]=minL;
  });

  // Compact layers
  var usedLayers={};
  agents.forEach(function(a){usedLayers[layerOf[a.id]]=true});
  var sortedLayers=Object.keys(usedLayers).map(Number).sort(function(a,b){return a-b});
  var layerRemap={};
  sortedLayers.forEach(function(l,i){layerRemap[l]=i});
  agents.forEach(function(a){layerOf[a.id]=layerRemap[layerOf[a.id]]});

  var maxL=0;agents.forEach(function(a){if(layerOf[a.id]>maxL)maxL=layerOf[a.id]});
  var tiers=[];for(var l=0;l<=maxL;l++)tiers.push([]);
  agents.forEach(function(a){tiers[layerOf[a.id]].push(a.id)});

  // Barycenter ordering (3 passes)
  for(var pass=0;pass<3;pass++){for(var li=1;li<=maxL;li++){var prev2={};tiers[li-1].forEach(function(id,i){prev2[id]=i});tiers[li].sort(function(a,b){var pa=parents[a]||[],pb=parents[b]||[];var ba=pa.length?pa.reduce(function(s,p){return s+(prev2[p]!==undefined?prev2[p]:0)},0)/pa.length:999;var bb=pb.length?pb.reduce(function(s,p){return s+(prev2[p]!==undefined?prev2[p]:0)},0)/pb.length:999;return ba-bb})}}

  // ── Position nodes ──
  // First, lay out all tiers normally
  var peerIds=Object.keys(peerSet).filter(function(id){
    return agents.some(function(a){return a.id===id});
  });
  var pos={};
  // Check if layer 0 has non-peer roots that need separation
  var tier0Peers=(tiers[0]||[]).filter(function(id){return peerSet[id]});
  var tier0NonPeers=(tiers[0]||[]).filter(function(id){return!peerSet[id]});
  var hasNonPeerRoots=tier0NonPeers.length>0&&tier0Peers.length>=2;

  // If we need to separate, add an extra visual row for non-peer roots
  var layerOffset=hasNonPeerRoots?1:0;

  // Position peer roots (layer 0)
  if(hasNonPeerRoots){
    var peerW=0;
    tier0Peers.forEach(function(id,ni){peerW+=nodeWidths[id]||120;if(ni<tier0Peers.length-1)peerW+=PADX});
    var cx=-peerW/2;
    tier0Peers.forEach(function(id){
      var nw=nodeWidths[id]||120;
      pos[id]={x:cx,y:0,w:nw,h:NH};
      cx+=nw+PADX;
    });
  }

  // Position all tiers (skip tier0 peers if already placed)
  tiers.forEach(function(tier,li){
    var items=tier;
    if(li===0&&hasNonPeerRoots){
      items=tier0NonPeers;// only position non-peers for tier 0
    }
    var actualY=(li+layerOffset)*(NH+PADY);
    if(li===0&&!hasNonPeerRoots)actualY=0;
    if(li===0&&hasNonPeerRoots)actualY=NH+PADY;// non-peer roots go on row 1

    var rowW=0;
    items.forEach(function(id,ni){rowW+=nodeWidths[id]||120;if(ni<items.length-1)rowW+=PADX});
    var cx=-rowW/2;
    items.forEach(function(id){
      if(pos[id])return;// already positioned (peer roots)
      var nw=nodeWidths[id]||120;
      pos[id]={x:cx,y:actualY,w:nw,h:NH};
      cx+=nw+PADX;
    });
  });

  // Center non-peer roots under their children
  if(hasNonPeerRoots){
    tier0NonPeers.forEach(function(id){
      var ch=children[id]||[];
      if(ch.length>0){
        var sum=0,cnt=0;
        ch.forEach(function(cid){if(pos[cid]){sum+=pos[cid].x+pos[cid].w/2;cnt++}});
        if(cnt>0)pos[id].x=sum/cnt-pos[id].w/2;
      }
    });
  }
  // Place channel nodes BELOW agents, centered under their bound agents
  if(chNodes.length>0){
    // Find the actual lowest agent Y
    var maxAgentY=0;
    agents.forEach(function(a){if(pos[a.id]&&pos[a.id].y+pos[a.id].h>maxAgentY)maxAgentY=pos[a.id].y+pos[a.id].h});
    var chY=maxAgentY+PADY;
    var chBindMap={};
    edges.forEach(function(e){
      if(e.type!=="channel")return;
      if(!chBindMap[e.to])chBindMap[e.to]=[];
      chBindMap[e.to].push(e.from);
    });
    chNodes.forEach(function(ch){
      var cw=chWidths[ch.id]||100;
      var boundAgents=chBindMap[ch.id]||[];
      var avgX=0;
      if(boundAgents.length>0){
        var sum=0,cnt=0;
        boundAgents.forEach(function(aid){var p=pos[aid];if(p){sum+=p.x+p.w/2;cnt++}});
        if(cnt>0)avgX=sum/cnt-cw/2;
      }
      pos[ch.id]={x:avgX,y:chY,w:cw,h:CH_H};
    });
  }

  // Place infrastructure nodes — driven by plugins.slots (role → pluginId)
  var infraNodes=[];
  var pe=D.config&&D.config.plugins&&D.config.plugins.entries||{};
  var slots=D.config&&D.config.plugins&&D.config.plugins.slots||{};
  var infraLines=[];
  var infraId="infra:embeddings";

  // Build a label for each active slot
  var slotLabels={"memory":"Memory","contextEngine":"Context Engine","embedding":"Embedding","vectorStore":"Vector Store","search":"Search"};
  Object.keys(slots).forEach(function(slotName){
    var pluginId=slots[slotName];
    if(!pluginId)return;
    var entry=pe[pluginId]||{};
    if(entry.enabled===false)return;
    var role=slotLabels[slotName]||slotName;
    infraLines.push(role+": "+pluginId);
  });

  // Fallback: if no slots defined, scan entries for known plugin kinds
  if(infraLines.length===0){
    Object.keys(pe).forEach(function(pluginId){
      var entry=pe[pluginId];
      if(!entry||entry.enabled===false)return;
      // Detect by plugin id patterns
      if(/memory|mem0|lancedb|qdrant/i.test(pluginId)){
        infraLines.push("Memory: "+pluginId);
      }else if(/lossless|context.*engine|compaction/i.test(pluginId)){
        infraLines.push("Context Engine: "+pluginId);
      }
    });
  }

  if(infraLines.length>0){
      var infraLabel=infraLines.join("\n");
      var longestLine=infraLines.reduce(function(a,b){return a.length>b.length?a:b},"");
      infraNodes.push({id:infraId,name:infraLabel,icon:"🧬"});
      var tw=measureText(longestLine,INFRA_FONT);
      var infraW=Math.max(120,Math.round(tw+40+44+44));
      var infraH=infraLines.length>1?CH_H+(infraLines.length-1)*18:CH_H;
      // Position to the right of channels, or centered if no channels
      var infraY=chNodes.length>0?pos[chNodes[0].id].y:((function(){var my=0;agents.forEach(function(a){if(pos[a.id]&&pos[a.id].y+pos[a.id].h>my)my=pos[a.id].y+pos[a.id].h});return my+PADY})());
      var allXs=Object.values(pos).map(function(p){return p.x+p.w/2});
      var maxPosX=allXs.length?Math.max.apply(null,allXs):0;
      var infraX=maxPosX+PADX;
      pos[infraId]={x:infraX,y:infraY,w:infraW,h:infraH};
  }
  var allP=Object.values(pos);
  var minX=Math.min.apply(null,allP.map(function(p){return p.x}));
  var maxX=Math.max.apply(null,allP.map(function(p){return p.x+p.w}));
  var minY=Math.min.apply(null,allP.map(function(p){return p.y}));
  var maxY=Math.max.apply(null,allP.map(function(p){return p.y+p.h}));
  // Expand bounds to include peer group box + label if peers exist
  var peerIds2=Object.keys(peerSet).filter(function(id){return!!pos[id]});
  if(peerIds2.length>=2){
    var pgPadBounds=isMobileViewport?16:24;
    var pgMinX=Infinity,pgMaxX=-Infinity,pgMinY=Infinity,pgMaxY=-Infinity;
    peerIds2.forEach(function(id){
      var p=pos[id];
      if(p.x<pgMinX)pgMinX=p.x;
      if(p.x+p.w>pgMaxX)pgMaxX=p.x+p.w;
      if(p.y<pgMinY)pgMinY=p.y;
      if(p.y+p.h>pgMaxY)pgMaxY=p.y+p.h;
    });
    // Expand overall bounds to include the peer group box + label
    if(pgMinX-pgPadBounds<minX)minX=pgMinX-pgPadBounds;
    if(pgMaxX+pgPadBounds>maxX)maxX=pgMaxX+pgPadBounds;
    if(pgMinY-pgPadBounds-22<minY)minY=pgMinY-pgPadBounds-22;
    if(pgMaxY+pgPadBounds>maxY)maxY=pgMaxY+pgPadBounds;
  }
  // Add space for the legend at the bottom
  var legendH=30;
  maxY=maxY+legendH;
  var cW=maxX-minX,cH=maxY-minY;
  // Fit the graph to the viewport — allow up to 1.4x zoom so it fills the space
  var fitSc=Math.min((W-MARGIN*2)/Math.max(cW,1),(H-MARGIN*2)/Math.max(cH,1));
  fitSc=Math.min(1.4,Math.max(isMobileViewport?0.3:0.5,fitSc));
  // On large viewports with few nodes, don't zoom past a comfortable level
  if(agents.length<=3)fitSc=Math.min(1.2,fitSc);
  var isMobile=isMobileViewport;
  var layerW=cW+MARGIN*2,layerH=cH+MARGIN*2+legendH;
  var uPos={};
  Object.keys(pos).forEach(function(id){
    uPos[id]={x:pos[id].x-minX+MARGIN,y:pos[id].y-minY+MARGIN,w:pos[id].w,h:pos[id].h};
  });
  // Center the layer in the canvas
  var scaledLayerW=layerW*fitSc;
  var scaledLayerH=layerH*fitSc;
  mapScale=fitSc;
  mapOffX=(W-scaledLayerW)/2;
  mapOffY=(H-scaledLayerH)/2;
  // On wide desktop with short graphs, bias toward upper third
  if(!isMobile&&W>1000&&scaledLayerH<H*0.6){
    mapOffY=H*0.08;
  }

  // ── Build DOM ──
  var zc=Q("zoom-controls");
  canvas.innerHTML="";
  if(zc)canvas.appendChild(zc);
  var domLayer=document.createElement("div");
  domLayer.id="rel-layer";
  var layerW=cW+MARGIN*2,layerH=cH+MARGIN*2+legendH;
  domLayer.className="rel-layer";domLayer.style.width=layerW+"px";domLayer.style.height=layerH+"px";
  domLayer.style.transform="translate("+mapOffX+"px,"+mapOffY+"px) scale("+mapScale+")";

  var ns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg";
  var svg=document.createElementNS(ns,"svg");
  svg.setAttribute("width",layerW);svg.setAttribute("height",layerH);
  svg.setAttribute("class","rel-svg");
  var defs=document.createElementNS(ns,"defs");
  // Arrowhead markers
  function addMarker(id,color,sz){
    var mk=document.createElementNS(ns,"marker");
    mk.setAttribute("id",id);mk.setAttribute("markerWidth",sz);mk.setAttribute("markerHeight",sz*0.75);
    mk.setAttribute("refX",sz-1);mk.setAttribute("refY",sz*0.375);
    mk.setAttribute("orient","auto");mk.setAttribute("markerUnits","strokeWidth");
    var p=document.createElementNS(ns,"path");
    p.setAttribute("d","M0,0.5 L"+(sz-1)+","+sz*0.375+" L0,"+(sz*0.75-0.5));
    p.setAttribute("fill","none");p.setAttribute("stroke",color);p.setAttribute("stroke-width","1.5");p.setAttribute("stroke-linejoin","round");
    mk.appendChild(p);defs.appendChild(mk);
  }
  addMarker("arr-del","#7c6cf0",8);
  addMarker("arr-ch","#3498db",6);
  // Reverse arrowhead for bidirectional
  var mkRev=document.createElementNS(ns,"marker");
  mkRev.setAttribute("id","arr-del-rev");mkRev.setAttribute("markerWidth","8");mkRev.setAttribute("markerHeight","6");
  mkRev.setAttribute("refX","1");mkRev.setAttribute("refY","3");
  mkRev.setAttribute("orient","auto");mkRev.setAttribute("markerUnits","strokeWidth");
  var pRev=document.createElementNS(ns,"path");
  pRev.setAttribute("d","M8,0.5 L1,3 L8,5.5");pRev.setAttribute("fill","none");
  pRev.setAttribute("stroke","#7c6cf0");pRev.setAttribute("stroke-width","1.5");pRev.setAttribute("stroke-linejoin","round");
  mkRev.appendChild(pRev);defs.appendChild(mkRev);
  svg.appendChild(defs);

  function edgePt(id,tx,ty){
    var p=uPos[id];if(!p)return{x:tx,y:ty};
    var cx=p.x+p.w/2,cy=p.y+p.h/2,dx=tx-cx,dy=ty-cy,len=Math.sqrt(dx*dx+dy*dy)||1;
    var ux=dx/len,uy=dy/len,t=Math.min(p.w/2/Math.abs(ux||1e-9),p.h/2/Math.abs(uy||1e-9));
    return{x:cx+ux*t,y:cy+uy*t};
  }

  // Draw delegation edges (merged bidirectional = single line with arrows on both ends)
  var peerSet2={};getPeers().forEach(function(id){peerSet2[id]=true});
  delEdges.forEach(function(e){
    if(peerSet2[e.from]&&peerSet2[e.to])return;
    var sp=uPos[e.from],dp=uPos[e.to];if(!sp||!dp)return;
    var sx=sp.x+sp.w/2,sy=sp.y+sp.h/2,dx=dp.x+dp.w/2,dy=dp.y+dp.h/2;
    var p1=edgePt(e.from,dx,dy),p2=edgePt(e.to,sx,sy);
    var mx=(p1.x+p2.x)/2,my=(p1.y+p2.y)/2;
    var nx=-(p2.y-p1.y)*0.1,ny=(p2.x-p1.x)*0.1;
    var path=document.createElementNS(ns,"path");
    path.setAttribute("d","M"+p1.x+","+p1.y+" Q"+(mx+nx)+","+(my+ny)+" "+p2.x+","+p2.y);
    path.setAttribute("fill","none");
    path.setAttribute("stroke","#7c6cf0");path.setAttribute("stroke-width","1.8");path.setAttribute("stroke-opacity","0.65");
    path.setAttribute("marker-end","url(#arr-del)");
    if(e.bidir)path.setAttribute("marker-start","url(#arr-del-rev)");
    svg.appendChild(path);
  });

  // Channel connections shown as badges on agent nodes instead of edges

  // Draw peer group box — rounded rect around all peer nodes
  var peerIds=Object.keys(peerSet).filter(function(id){return!!uPos[id]});
  if(peerIds.length>=2){
    var pgPad=isMobileViewport?14:20;
    var pgMinX=Infinity,pgMinY=Infinity,pgMaxX=-Infinity,pgMaxY=-Infinity;
    peerIds.forEach(function(id){
      var p=uPos[id];
      if(p.x<pgMinX)pgMinX=p.x;
      if(p.y<pgMinY)pgMinY=p.y;
      if(p.x+p.w>pgMaxX)pgMaxX=p.x+p.w;
      if(p.y+p.h>pgMaxY)pgMaxY=p.y+p.h;
    });
    var pgRect=document.createElementNS(ns,"rect");
    pgRect.setAttribute("x",pgMinX-pgPad);pgRect.setAttribute("y",pgMinY-pgPad-18);
    pgRect.setAttribute("width",pgMaxX-pgMinX+pgPad*2);pgRect.setAttribute("height",pgMaxY-pgMinY+pgPad*2+18);
    pgRect.setAttribute("rx","14");pgRect.setAttribute("ry","14");
    pgRect.setAttribute("fill","none");pgRect.setAttribute("stroke","#00bfa5");
    pgRect.setAttribute("stroke-width","1.5");pgRect.setAttribute("stroke-dasharray","6,4");
    pgRect.setAttribute("stroke-opacity","0.35");
    svg.appendChild(pgRect);
    // Label
    var pgLabel=document.createElementNS(ns,"text");
    pgLabel.setAttribute("x",pgMinX-pgPad+10);pgLabel.setAttribute("y",pgMinY-pgPad-4);
    pgLabel.setAttribute("fill","#00bfa5");pgLabel.setAttribute("font-size",String(GT.peer));
    pgLabel.setAttribute("font-family","-apple-system,BlinkMacSystemFont,sans-serif");
    pgLabel.setAttribute("font-weight","600");pgLabel.setAttribute("opacity","0.6");
    pgLabel.textContent="A2A Peer Group";
    svg.appendChild(pgLabel);
  }

  domLayer.appendChild(svg);

  // Build agent → channel map for badges
  var CH_ICONS={whatsapp:"💬",telegram:"✈️",discord:"🎮",slack:"💼",signal:"🔒",matrix:"🔷",webchat:"🌐",irc:"📡"};
  var agentChannels={};
  (D.bindings||[]).forEach(function(b){
    if(!b.agentId||!b.match||!b.match.channel)return;
    if(!agentChannels[b.agentId])agentChannels[b.agentId]={};
    agentChannels[b.agentId][b.match.channel]=true;
  });

    // Agent nodes
  agents.forEach(function(a){
    var p=uPos[a.id];if(!p)return;
    var n=document.createElement("div");
    n.className="rn";n.setAttribute("data-id",a.id);
    n.style.cssText="position:absolute;left:"+p.x+"px;top:"+p.y+"px;width:"+p.w+"px;height:"+p.h+"px;"
      +"background:#161622;border:1.5px solid #2a2a3e;border-radius:10px;cursor:pointer;"
      +"display:flex;flex-direction:column;align-items:center;justify-content:center;"
      +"user-select:none;transition:box-shadow .15s,border-color .15s;padding:8px 14px;box-sizing:border-box";
    var model=getModel(a);
    var hb=a.heartbeat||{};
    var html='<div class="rn-icon">'+(getToolAlso(a).indexOf("run_task_flow")>-1?'<span class="rn-crown">👑</span>':'')+agentIcon(a)+'</div>'
      +'<div class="rn-name">'+esc(a.name||a.id)+'</div>';
    if(model)html+='<div class="rn-model">'+esc(model)+'</div>';
    if(hb.every)html+='<div class="rn-heartbeat">♡ '+esc(hb.every)+(hb.model?' · '+esc(hb.model):'')+'</div>';
    if(a["default"])html+='<div class="rn-default">default</div>';
    // Channel badges
    var chMap=agentChannels[a.id];
    if(chMap){
      var chNames=Object.keys(chMap);
      html+='<div class="rn-channels">';
      chNames.forEach(function(ch){
        html+='<span class="rn-ch-badge">'+(CH_ICONS[ch]||"📡")+' '+esc(ch)+'</span>';
      });
      html+='</div>';
    }
    n.innerHTML=html;
    var delBtn=document.createElement("button");
    delBtn.className="rn-delete";
    delBtn.type="button";
    delBtn.title="Delete agent";
    delBtn.textContent="✕";
    delBtn.addEventListener("click",function(e){
      e.preventDefault();
      e.stopPropagation();
      deleteAgent(a.id);
    });
    n.appendChild(delBtn);
    n.addEventListener("mouseenter",function(){n.classList.add("hovered");n.classList.remove("inactive")});
    n.addEventListener("mouseleave",function(){n.classList.remove("hovered");if(drawerAgent&&drawerAgent.id===a.id){n.classList.add("active-node");n.classList.remove("inactive")}else{n.classList.add("inactive");n.classList.remove("active-node")}});
    n.addEventListener("click",function(e){
      if(e.target&&e.target.closest&&e.target.closest(".rn-delete"))return;
      openDrawer(a,"sessions");
    });
    domLayer.appendChild(n);
  });

  // Infrastructure nodes (embeddings/vector store)
  infraNodes.forEach(function(inf){
    var p=uPos[inf.id];if(!p)return;
    var wrap=document.createElement("div");
    wrap.className="chn-wrap infra-wrap";
    wrap.style.cssText="position:absolute;left:"+p.x+"px;top:"+p.y+"px;width:"+p.w+"px;height:"+p.h+"px;cursor:pointer";
    wrap.title="Click to open config";
    var n=document.createElement("div");
    n.className="chn";
    n.style.cssText="width:100%;height:100%;"
      +"background:#0d1520;border:1.5px dashed #6a5acd;border-radius:8px;"
      +"display:flex;flex-direction:row;align-items:center;justify-content:center;gap:8px;"
      +"user-select:none;opacity:0.85;padding:0 20px;box-sizing:border-box";
    n.innerHTML='<span class="rn-icon" style="font-size:'+GT.icon+'px">'+esc(inf.icon)+'</span>'
      +'<span class="ch-node-label infra">'+esc(inf.name).replace(/\n/g,"<br>")+'</span>';
    wrap.appendChild(n);
    wrap.addEventListener("click",function(e){e.stopPropagation();showRawConfig()});
    domLayer.appendChild(wrap);
  });

  // Legend — position below the lowest content, aligned right
  var leg=document.createElement("div");
  leg.className="graph-legend";
  var legendX=Math.max(MARGIN,(maxX-minX)+MARGIN-320);
  var legendY=(maxY-minY)+MARGIN+12;
  leg.style.left=legendX+"px";leg.style.top=legendY+"px";
  leg.innerHTML=''
    +'<span class="graph-legend-item"><svg width="20" height="8"><line x1="0" y1="4" x2="16" y2="4" stroke="#7c6cf0" stroke-width="1.5" opacity="0.65"/><polyline points="13,1.5 17,4 13,6.5" fill="none" stroke="#7c6cf0" stroke-width="1.2"/></svg>delegates</span>'
    +'<span class="graph-legend-item"><svg width="24" height="8"><polyline points="4,1.5 0,4 4,6.5" fill="none" stroke="#7c6cf0" stroke-width="1.2" opacity="0.65"/><line x1="0" y1="4" x2="20" y2="4" stroke="#7c6cf0" stroke-width="1.5" opacity="0.65"/><polyline points="17,1.5 21,4 17,6.5" fill="none" stroke="#7c6cf0" stroke-width="1.2" opacity="0.65"/></svg>mutual</span>'
    +'<span class="graph-legend-item"><svg width="16" height="12"><rect x="1" y="1" width="14" height="10" rx="3" fill="none" stroke="#00bfa5" stroke-width="1.2" stroke-dasharray="3,2" opacity="0.5"/></svg>a2a peers</span>'
    +(infraNodes.length>0?'<span class="graph-legend-item"><svg width="16" height="12"><rect x="1" y="1" width="14" height="10" rx="3" fill="none" stroke="#6a5acd" stroke-width="1.2" stroke-dasharray="3,2" opacity="0.5"/></svg>infra</span>':'');
  domLayer.appendChild(leg);

  canvas.appendChild(domLayer);
  setupMapPan(canvas);
  var lbl=Q("zoom-label");if(lbl)lbl.textContent=Math.round(mapScale*100)+"%";
  _cacheGraph();
}

// ── Agent Drawer ──
function openDrawer(a,tab){
  // Reset orchestrator flow state when switching to a different agent
  if(!drawerAgent||drawerAgent.id!==a.id){
    _orchFlow=null;
    _orchFlowLoadedFor=null;
  }
  drawerAgent=a;drawerTab=tab||"identity";
  var dr=Q("agent-drawer");
  var bk=Q("drawer-backdrop");
  dr.classList.add("open");
  if(bk)bk.classList.add("open");
  renderDrawer();
  renderAgentList();
  // Load orchestrator flow if opening on that tab
  if(drawerTab==="orchestrator"&&a){
    _loadOrchFlowForAgent(a.id);
  }
  // Fetch fresh agent data (file line counts etc.)
  api("agents/"+encodeURIComponent(a.id)).then(function(d){
    if(d.agent&&drawerAgent&&drawerAgent.id===a.id){
      // Update cached agent with fresh data
      drawerAgent=d.agent;
      for(var i=0;i<D.agents.length;i++){if(D.agents[i].id===a.id){D.agents[i]=d.agent;break}}
      renderDrawer();
    }
  }).catch(function(){});
  // Highlight active node in rel map
  var rl=Q("rel-layer");
  if(rl){
    rl.querySelectorAll(".rn").forEach(function(n){
      var id=n.getAttribute("data-id");
      if(id===a.id){n.classList.add("active-node");n.classList.remove("inactive")}
      else{n.classList.add("inactive");n.classList.remove("active-node")}
    });
  }
}
function closeDrawer(){
  drawerAgent=null;
  var dr=Q("agent-drawer");
  var bk=Q("drawer-backdrop");
  if(dr)dr.classList.remove("open");
  if(bk)bk.classList.remove("open");
  renderAgentList();
  // Clear highlights
  var rl=Q("rel-layer");
  if(rl)rl.querySelectorAll(".rn").forEach(function(n){n.classList.add("inactive");n.classList.remove("active-node","hovered")});
}

function renderDrawer(){
  if(!drawerAgent)return;
  var a=drawerAgent;
  var col=agentColor(a.id);
  var tabs=["sessions","identity","files","tools","channels","relationships","orchestrator","danger"];

  // ── Main panel only (no minimap) ──
  var main=Q("drawer-main");
  if(!main)return;
  var h='<div class="drawer-head" style="border-top:3px solid '+col+'">';
  h+='<div class="drawer-head-info">';
  h+='<div class="drawer-head-icon">'+agentIcon(a)+'</div>';
  h+='<div><div class="drawer-head-name">'+esc(a.name||a.id)+'</div>';
  h+='<div class="drawer-head-id">'+esc(a.id)+'</div></div></div>';
  h+='<button class="close-btn" onclick="closeDrawer()">×</button></div>';
  h+='<div class="drawer-tabs">';
  var TAB_LABELS={tools:"Tools / Skills"};
  tabs.forEach(function(t){var lbl=TAB_LABELS[t]||(t.charAt(0).toUpperCase()+t.slice(1));h+='<div class="dtab'+(drawerTab===t?" active":"")+'" data-tab="'+t+'" onclick="switchDrawerTab(\''+t+'\')">'+lbl+'</div>'});
  h+='</div>';
  h+='<div class="drawer-body" id="drawer-body">'+renderTab(a,drawerTab)+'</div>';
  main.innerHTML=h;
}
function switchDrawerAgent(agentId){
  var a=null;for(var i=0;i<D.agents.length;i++){if(D.agents[i].id===agentId){a=D.agents[i];break}}
  if(a)openDrawer(a,drawerTab);
}
function switchDrawerTab(tab){
  drawerTab=tab;
  var tabs=document.querySelectorAll(".dtab");
  for(var i=0;i<tabs.length;i++){
    if(tabs[i].getAttribute("data-tab")===tab)tabs[i].classList.add("active");
    else tabs[i].classList.remove("active");
  }
  var db=Q("drawer-body");
  if(db&&drawerAgent)db.innerHTML=renderTab(drawerAgent,tab);
  // Load existing flow definition when opening orchestrator tab
  if(tab==="orchestrator"&&drawerAgent){
    _loadOrchFlowForAgent(drawerAgent.id);
  }
}

function renderTab(a,tab){
  switch(tab){
    case "identity":return renderIdentity(a);
    case "files":return renderFiles(a);
    case "tools":return renderTools(a);
    case "channels":return renderChannels(a);
    case "sessions":return renderSessions(a);
    case "subagents":return renderSubagents(a);
    case "relationships":return renderSubagents(a);
    case "orchestrator":return renderOrchestrator(a);
    case "danger":return renderDanger(a);
    default:return"";
  }
}

// ── Fallback model tag-picker ──
function fbSelect(baseId,current){
  var aliases=getModelAliases();
  var hiddenId=baseId+"-hidden";
  var tagsId=baseId+"-tags";
  var dropId=baseId+"-drop";
  var customId=baseId+"-custom";

  var h='<div class="fb-picker" id="'+baseId+'-wrap">';
  // Hidden store
  h+='<input type="hidden" id="'+hiddenId+'" value="'+esc(current.join(","))+'" />';
  // Tag row
  h+='<div class="fb-tags" id="'+tagsId+'">';
  current.forEach(function(v){
    h+='<span class="fb-tag" data-val="'+esc(v)+'">'+esc(v)
      +'<button type="button" onclick="fbRemove(\''+baseId+'\',\''+esc(v)+'\')" class="fb-tag-x">×</button></span>';
  });
  h+='</div>';
  // Add row
  h+='<div class="fb-add-row">';
  if(aliases.length>0){
    h+='<select id="'+dropId+'" class="fb-drop">';
    h+='<option value="">+ add alias…</option>';
    aliases.forEach(function(a){h+='<option value="'+esc(a)+'">'+esc(a)+'</option>'});
    h+='<option value="__custom__">✏ custom…</option>';
    h+='</select>';
  }
  h+='<input id="'+customId+'" placeholder="custom alias…" class="fb-custom-input" style="'+(aliases.length>0?'display:none':'')+'" />';
  h+='<button type="button" class="btn btn-sm" onclick="fbAdd(\''+baseId+'\')">Add</button>';
  h+='</div></div>';

  // Wire up dropdown show/hide after render
  if(aliases.length>0){
    setTimeout(function(){
      var drop=document.getElementById(dropId);
      var custom=document.getElementById(customId);
      if(!drop||!custom)return;
      drop.addEventListener("change",function(){
        if(drop.value==="__custom__"){custom.style.display="";custom.focus()}
        else{custom.style.display="none"}
      });
    },0);
  }
  return h;
}
function fbAdd(baseId){
  var dropId=baseId+"-drop";
  var customId=baseId+"-custom";
  var drop=document.getElementById(dropId);
  var custom=document.getElementById(customId);
  var val="";
  if(drop&&drop.value&&drop.value!=="__custom__")val=drop.value.trim();
  else if(custom)val=custom.value.trim();
  if(!val)return;
  var hidden=document.getElementById(baseId+"-hidden");
  if(!hidden)return;
  var current=hidden.value?hidden.value.split(",").filter(Boolean):[];
  if(current.indexOf(val)>-1)return; // no dupes
  current.push(val);
  hidden.value=current.join(",");
  // Add tag chip
  var tags=document.getElementById(baseId+"-tags");
  if(tags){
    var span=document.createElement("span");
    span.className="fb-tag";span.setAttribute("data-val",val);
    span.innerHTML=esc(val)+'<button type="button" onclick="fbRemove(\''+baseId+'\',\''+esc(val)+'\')" class="fb-tag-x">×</button>';
    tags.appendChild(span);
  }
  // Reset inputs
  if(drop&&drop.value!=="__custom__")drop.value="";
  if(custom)custom.value="";
}
function fbRemove(baseId,val){
  var hidden=document.getElementById(baseId+"-hidden");
  if(!hidden)return;
  var current=hidden.value?hidden.value.split(",").filter(Boolean):[];
  var idx=current.indexOf(val);
  if(idx>-1)current.splice(idx,1);
  hidden.value=current.join(",");
  var tags=document.getElementById(baseId+"-tags");
  if(tags){
    var chips=tags.querySelectorAll(".fb-tag");
    chips.forEach(function(c){if(c.getAttribute("data-val")===val)c.remove()});
  }
}

// ── Identity Tab ──
function renderIdentity(a){
  var id=a.identity||{};var model=getModel(a);var fb=getFallbacks(a);
  var ICON_OPTIONS=["🤖","🧠","💻","🔧","📝","🎨","🔍","🛡️","📊","🚀","⚡","🌐","📡","🗂️","🧪","🐙","👑","🦊","🐺","🦅","🐉","🤹","🎯","💡","🔮","⚙️","🏗️","📦","🧩","🎭"];
  var curIcon=a.icon||"🤖";
  var iconOpts='<select id="ai-icon-'+a.id+'" class="icon-select">';
  ICON_OPTIONS.forEach(function(ic){iconOpts+='<option value="'+esc(ic)+'"'+(curIcon===ic?' selected':'')+'>'+ic+'</option>'});
  if(ICON_OPTIONS.indexOf(curIcon)<0)iconOpts+='<option value="'+esc(curIcon)+'" selected>'+esc(curIcon)+'</option>';
  iconOpts+='</select>';

  var h='<div class="fg-row3">';
  h+='<div class="fg">'+tip("Agent Name","The display name shown in the dashboard and used in logs.")+'<input id="ai-name-'+a.id+'" value="'+esc(a.name||a.id)+'" /></div>';
  h+='<div class="fg">'+tip("Icon","Emoji shown on the graph node and drawer header.")+iconOpts+'</div>';
  h+='<div class="fg">'+tip("Primary Model","The model alias this agent uses by default. Must match a key in the models section of openclaw.json.")+modelSelect("ai-model-"+a.id,model,"the-brain")+'</div></div>';
  h+='<div class="fg">'+tip("Fallback Models","Model aliases tried in order if the primary model fails. Add from your defined aliases or type a custom one.")+fbSelect("ai-fb-"+a.id,fb)+'</div>';
  h+='<div class="fg-row">';
  h+='<div class="fg">'+tip("Workspace","Absolute or ~ path to the directory containing this agent\'s MD files (SOUL.md, IDENTITY.md, etc.).")+'<input id="ai-ws-'+a.id+'" value="'+esc(a.workspace||"")+'" /></div>';
  h+='</div>';
  h+='<div class="fg">'+tip("Identity Name","The name the agent uses to refer to itself in conversations.")+'<input id="ai-idname-'+a.id+'" value="'+esc(id.name||"")+'" /></div>';
  var THINKING_LEVELS=["","off","minimal","low","medium","high","xhigh","adaptive"];
  var curThinking=a.thinkingDefault||"";
  var thinkOpts='<select id="ai-thinking-'+a.id+'">';
  THINKING_LEVELS.forEach(function(lv){thinkOpts+='<option value="'+esc(lv)+'"'+(curThinking===lv?' selected':'')+'>'+(lv||"(inherit)")+'</option>'});
  thinkOpts+='</select>';
  var REASONING_LEVELS=["","on","off","stream"];
  var curReasoning=a.reasoningDefault||"";
  var reasonOpts='<select id="ai-reasoning-'+a.id+'">';
  REASONING_LEVELS.forEach(function(lv){reasonOpts+='<option value="'+esc(lv)+'"'+(curReasoning===lv?' selected':'')+'>'+(lv||"(inherit)")+'</option>'});
  reasonOpts+='</select>';
  h+='<div class="fg-row">';
  h+='<div class="fg">'+tip("Thinking Level","Default thinking depth for this agent. Controls how much internal reasoning the model performs. Overrides the global agents.defaults.thinkingDefault.")+thinkOpts+'</div>';
  h+='<div class="fg">'+tip("Reasoning Visibility","Whether thinking/reasoning blocks are shown in replies. on = shown, stream = streamed (Telegram only), off = hidden.")+reasonOpts+'</div>';
  h+='</div>';
  var mp=(a.groupChat&&a.groupChat.mentionPatterns)||[];
  h+='<div class="fg">'+tip("Mention Patterns","Comma-separated patterns (e.g. @bot, /ask) that trigger this agent in group chats.")+'<input id="ai-mp-'+a.id+'" value="'+esc(mp.join(", "))+'" /></div>';
  var hb=a.heartbeat||{};
  h+='<div class="heartbeat-title">Heartbeat</div>';
  h+='<div class="heartbeat-desc">Keeps the agent alive by waking it periodically. Required for A2A peers. Leave empty to disable.</div>';
  h+='<div class="fg-row">';
  h+='<div class="fg">'+tip("Interval","How often the agent wakes up, e.g. 5m, 30m, 1h, 1200m. Leave empty to disable heartbeat.")+'<input id="ai-hb-every-'+a.id+'" value="'+esc(hb.every||"")+'" placeholder="e.g. 5m" /></div>';
  h+='<div class="fg">'+tip("Heartbeat Model","Model alias used for heartbeat tasks. Typically a cheap/fast model since heartbeats are lightweight.")+modelSelect("ai-hb-model-"+a.id,hb.model||"","cheap-fast")+'</div>';
  h+='</div>';
  h+='<div class="fg-row">';
  h+='<div class="fg"><label class="perm-item perm-item-auto"><input type="checkbox" id="ai-hb-light-'+a.id+'"'+(hb.lightContext?" checked":"")+' /> Light Context <i class="tip-icon" data-tip="Reduces token usage by sending a minimal context window to the heartbeat model instead of the full conversation history.">?</i></label></div>';
  h+='<div class="fg"><label class="perm-item perm-item-auto"><input type="checkbox" id="ai-hb-isolated-'+a.id+'"'+(hb.isolatedSession?" checked":"")+' /> Isolated Session <i class="tip-icon" data-tip="Runs the heartbeat in its own session so it doesn\'t pollute the main conversation context. Reduces token buildup over time.">?</i></label></div>';
  h+='</div>';
  h+='<div class="fg"><label class="perm-item perm-item-auto"><input type="checkbox" id="ai-def-'+a.id+'"'+(a["default"]?" checked":"")+' /> Default agent <i class="tip-icon" tabindex="0">?</i><span class="tip-text">The default agent handles messages that don\'t match any other routing rule.</span></label></div>';
  h+='<div class="save-row"><button class="btn btn-accent" onclick="saveIdentity(\''+a.id+'\')">Save Identity</button></div>';
  return h;
}
function saveIdentity(id){
  var name=V("ai-name-"+id).trim(),model=getModelVal("ai-model-"+id);
  var icon=V("ai-icon-"+id).trim();
  var fb=V("ai-fb-"+id+"-hidden").split(",").map(function(s){return s.trim()}).filter(Boolean);
  var ws=V("ai-ws-"+id).trim();
  var idName=V("ai-idname-"+id).trim();
  var mp=V("ai-mp-"+id).split(",").map(function(s){return s.trim()}).filter(Boolean);
  var isDef=CK("ai-def-"+id);
  var u={name:name};
  // Save icon to dashboard extension config (not openclaw.json)
  if(icon)api("dashboard/icons",{method:"PUT",body:JSON.stringify({agentId:id,icon:icon})}).catch(function(){});
  if(model){u.model={primary:model};if(fb.length>0)u.model.fallbacks=fb}
  if(ws)u.workspace=ws;
  if(idName)u.identity={name:idName};if(mp.length)u.groupChat={mentionPatterns:mp};
  var thinkVal=V("ai-thinking-"+id);
  if(thinkVal)u.thinkingDefault=thinkVal; else u.thinkingDefault=null;
  var reasonVal=V("ai-reasoning-"+id);
  if(reasonVal)u.reasoningDefault=reasonVal; else u.reasoningDefault=null;
  if(isDef)u["default"]=true;
  // Heartbeat
  var hbEvery=V("ai-hb-every-"+id).trim();
  var hbModel=getModelVal("ai-hb-model-"+id);
  var hbLight=CK("ai-hb-light-"+id);
  var hbIsolated=CK("ai-hb-isolated-"+id);
  if(hbEvery){
    u.heartbeat={every:hbEvery};
    if(hbModel)u.heartbeat.model=hbModel;
    if(hbLight)u.heartbeat.lightContext=true;
    if(hbIsolated)u.heartbeat.isolatedSession=true;
  }else{
    // Clear heartbeat if interval is empty
    u.heartbeat=null;
  }
  // Progress indicator
  var saveBtn=document.querySelector('#drawer-body .btn-accent[onclick*="saveIdentity"]');
  var origText="";
  if(saveBtn){origText=saveBtn.textContent;saveBtn.disabled=true;saveBtn.textContent="⏳ Saving…"}
  _showProgress();
  api(_deferParam("agents/"+encodeURIComponent(id)),{method:"PUT",body:JSON.stringify(u)}).then(function(r){
    _hideProgress();
    toast("Identity saved","ok");_deferRestart("Identity saved");
    if(saveBtn){saveBtn.textContent="✓ Saved";setTimeout(function(){if(saveBtn){saveBtn.disabled=false;saveBtn.textContent=origText}},1200)}
    // Update local agent data instead of full reload
    if(r.agent){
      for(var i=0;i<D.agents.length;i++){
        if(D.agents[i].id===id){
          // Remove properties that were deleted server-side (e.g. heartbeat cleared)
          if(u.heartbeat===null)delete D.agents[i].heartbeat;
          D.agents[i]=Object.assign(D.agents[i],r.agent);break}
      }
      if(drawerAgent&&drawerAgent.id===id){
        drawerAgent=D.agents.find(function(a){return a.id===id})||drawerAgent;
        renderDrawer();
      }
      renderAgentList();
      _invalidateAndRedraw();
    }
  }).catch(function(e){
    _hideProgress();
    toast(e.message,"err");
    if(saveBtn){saveBtn.disabled=false;saveBtn.textContent=origText}
  });
}

// ── Files Tab ──
function renderFiles(a){
  var model=getModel(a);
  var files=a.mdFiles||{};
  var extras=a.extraMdFiles||[];

  // If mdFiles hasn't been loaded yet (fast load), show loading state
  if(!a.mdFiles){
    return '<div class="loading-center"><span class="spin"></span> Loading files…</div>';
  }

  // Files now contain metadata objects {exists,lines,size} or null — not content strings
  var existingFiles=Object.keys(files).filter(function(f){return files[f]!=null});
  var allFiles=existingFiles.concat(extras.filter(function(f){return existingFiles.indexOf(f)<0}));

  var h='';
  // Generate-all section
  h+='<div class="gen-all-section">';
  h+='<div class="section-title-lg mb-sm">Generate All Files from Description</div>';
  h+='<div class="section-desc">Describe this agent\'s role and personality. The AI will write SOUL.md, IDENTITY.md, AGENTS.md, TOOLS.md and BOOTSTRAP.md.</div>';
  h+='<div class="gen-all-row">';
  h+='<div class="gen-all-model">'+tip("Model","Model alias to use for generation.")+modelSelect("gen-all-model-"+a.id,model,"the-brain")+'</div>';
  h+='<button class="btn btn-accent nowrap" id="gen-all-btn-'+a.id+'" onclick="doGenerateAll(\''+esc(a.id)+'\')">✨ Generate All</button>';
  h+='<span id="gen-all-status-'+a.id+'" class="gen-all-status"></span>';
  h+='</div>';
  h+='<div class="fg">'+tip("Description","Plain-language description of what this agent does, its personality, and how it should behave.")+mdToolbar("gen-all-desc-"+a.id)+'<textarea id="gen-all-desc-'+a.id+'" data-fs-title="Agent Description" style="min-height:80px;border-top-left-radius:0;border-top-right-radius:0" placeholder="e.g. A senior TypeScript developer who helps with code review and architecture. Communicates concisely. Specialises in Node.js and React."></textarea></div>';
  h+='</div>';

  // Add new file
  h+='<div class="files-header">';
  h+='<div class="section-title">Workspace Files</div>';
  h+='<button class="btn btn-sm btn-accent" onclick="addNewFile(\''+esc(a.id)+'\')">+ New File</button>';
  h+='</div>';

  if(allFiles.length===0){
    h+='<div class="no-files">No workspace files found at '+esc(a.workspace)+'</div>';
    return h;
  }

  allFiles.forEach(function(f){
    var meta=files[f];
    var lines=(meta&&meta.lines)?meta.lines:0;
    h+='<div class="file-row" id="frow-'+esc(a.id)+'-'+esc(f)+'">';
    h+='<div class="file-row-head">';
    h+='<span class="file-row-name">📄 '+esc(f)+'</span>';
    if(lines>0)h+='<span class="file-meta">'+lines+' lines</span>';
    else h+='<span class="file-meta empty">empty</span>';
    h+='<button class="btn btn-sm btn-accent" onclick="editFile(\''+esc(a.id)+'\',\''+esc(f)+'\')">✏ Edit</button>';
    h+='<button class="btn btn-sm btn-danger" onclick="deleteFile(\''+esc(a.id)+'\',\''+esc(f)+'\')">🗑</button>';
    h+='</div></div>';
  });
  return h;
}
function editFile(agentId,filename){
  api("agents/"+encodeURIComponent(agentId)+"/md/"+encodeURIComponent(filename)).then(function(d){
    var content=d.content||"";
    if(isMobileView()){
      openFsEditorDirect(filename,content,false,function(val){
        api("agents/"+encodeURIComponent(agentId)+"/md/"+encodeURIComponent(filename),{method:"PUT",body:JSON.stringify({content:val})})
          .then(function(){_closeFsOverlay();toast("Saved "+filename,"ok");if(drawerAgent)renderDrawer()}).catch(function(e){_closeFsOverlay();toast(e.message,"err")});
      });
      return;
    }
    var h=mdToolbar("mded-content")+'<textarea class="md-edit-ta" id="mded-content" data-fs-title="'+esc(filename)+'">'+esc(content)+'</textarea>'
      +'<div class="file-actions-row">'
      +'<button class="btn" onclick="closeModal()">Cancel</button>'
      +'<button class="btn btn-accent" onclick="saveEditedFile(\''+esc(agentId)+'\',\''+esc(filename)+'\')">💾 Save</button>'
      +'</div>';
    openModal(filename,h);
  }).catch(function(e){
    // File may not exist yet — open empty editor
    if(isMobileView()){
      openFsEditorDirect(filename,"",false,function(val){
        api("agents/"+encodeURIComponent(agentId)+"/md/"+encodeURIComponent(filename),{method:"PUT",body:JSON.stringify({content:val})})
          .then(function(){_closeFsOverlay();toast("Saved "+filename,"ok");if(drawerAgent)renderDrawer()}).catch(function(e2){_closeFsOverlay();toast(e2.message,"err")});
      });
      return;
    }
    var h=mdToolbar("mded-content")+'<textarea class="md-edit-ta" id="mded-content" data-fs-title="'+esc(filename)+'"></textarea>'
      +'<div class="file-actions-row">'
      +'<button class="btn" onclick="closeModal()">Cancel</button>'
      +'<button class="btn btn-accent" onclick="saveEditedFile(\''+esc(agentId)+'\',\''+esc(filename)+'\')">💾 Save</button>'
      +'</div>';
    openModal(filename,h);
  });
}
function saveEditedFile(agentId,filename){
  var ta=Q("mded-content");if(!ta)return;
  var content=ta.value;
  // Find save button and show progress
  var btns=document.querySelectorAll(".modal-body .btn-accent");
  var saveBtn=null;
  btns.forEach(function(b){if(b.textContent.indexOf("Save")>=0)saveBtn=b});
  var origText="";
  if(saveBtn){origText=saveBtn.textContent;saveBtn.disabled=true;saveBtn.textContent="⏳ Saving…"}
  api("agents/"+encodeURIComponent(agentId)+"/md/"+encodeURIComponent(filename),{method:"PUT",body:JSON.stringify({content:content})})
    .then(function(){toast("Saved "+filename,"ok");closeModal()}).catch(function(e){toast(e.message,"err");if(saveBtn){saveBtn.disabled=false;saveBtn.textContent=origText}});
}
function addNewFile(agentId){
  openModal("New File",
    '<div class="fg"><label>Filename (e.g. CUSTOM.md)</label><input id="nf-name" placeholder="CUSTOM.md" /></div>'
    +'<div class="file-actions-row">'
    +'<button class="btn" onclick="closeModal()">Cancel</button>'
    +'<button class="btn btn-accent" onclick="doAddNewFile(\''+esc(agentId)+'\')">Create</button></div>');
}
function doAddNewFile(agentId){
  var name=V("nf-name").trim();
  if(!name){toast("Enter a filename","err");return}
  if(!name.endsWith(".md"))name+=".md";
  api("agents/"+encodeURIComponent(agentId)+"/md/"+encodeURIComponent(name),{method:"PUT",body:JSON.stringify({content:""})})
    .then(function(){toast("File created","ok");closeModal();openFileIds[agentId+"/"+name]=true;if(drawerAgent)renderDrawer()}).catch(function(e){toast(e.message,"err")});
}
function deleteFile(agentId,filename){
  if(!confirm("Delete "+filename+"? This cannot be undone."))return;
  api("agents/"+encodeURIComponent(agentId)+"/md/"+encodeURIComponent(filename),{method:"DELETE"})
    .then(function(){toast("Deleted "+filename,"ok");if(drawerAgent)renderDrawer()}).catch(function(e){toast(e.message,"err")});
}
function doGenerateAll(agentId){
  var desc=V("gen-all-desc-"+agentId).trim();
  var model=getModelVal("gen-all-model-"+agentId);
  if(!desc){toast("Enter a description first","err");return}
  var btn=Q("gen-all-btn-"+agentId);
  var status=Q("gen-all-status-"+agentId);
  if(btn){btn.disabled=true;btn.textContent="Generating…"}
  if(status)status.textContent="This may take a minute…";
  api("agents/"+encodeURIComponent(agentId)+"/generate-all",{method:"POST",body:JSON.stringify({description:desc,model:model})})
    .then(function(d){
      toast("All files generated","ok");
      if(btn){btn.disabled=false;btn.textContent="✨ Generate All"}
      if(status){var ok=Object.values(d.results||{}).filter(function(v){return v==="ok"}).length;status.textContent=ok+" files updated"}
      load();
    }).catch(function(e){
      toast(e.message,"err");
      if(btn){btn.disabled=false;btn.textContent="✨ Generate All"}
      if(status)status.textContent="Error: "+e.message;
    });
}

// ── Tools Tab ──
var TOOL_PROFILES={
  "full":   {label:"Full",desc:"Every tool enabled — file system, shell, browser, messaging, memory, and all integrations.",tools:[]},
  "coding": {label:"Coding",desc:"Code-focused tools — file system, shell, browser, git, sessions, memory, and image. No messaging.",tools:[]},
  "minimal":{label:"Minimal",desc:"Read-only — session status only. No file access, no shell, no messaging.",tools:[]},
  "none":   {label:"None",desc:"No tools at all. Agent can only respond with text based on its context.",tools:[]}
};
var KNOWN_TOOLS=[];
var _toolRegistry=null;
var _toolRegistryLoading=false;

function _loadToolRegistry(force,cb){
  if(_toolRegistry&&!force){if(cb)cb(_toolRegistry);return}
  if(_toolRegistryLoading){if(cb)setTimeout(function(){_loadToolRegistry(false,cb)},200);return}
  _toolRegistryLoading=true;
  var method=force?"POST":"GET";
  api("tools/discover",{method:method}).then(function(d){
    _toolRegistry=d;
    _toolRegistryLoading=false;
    // Update profiles and known tools from registry
    if(d.profiles){
      Object.keys(d.profiles).forEach(function(k){
        TOOL_PROFILES[k]=d.profiles[k];
      });
    }
    if(d.tools&&d.tools.length>0){
