    .then(function(r){
      if(r.error){toast(r.error,"err");return}
      _onOrchSaveSuccess(agentId,toolId,flowDef);
      // Silently refresh agent's alsoAllow without re-rendering the drawer
      api("agents/"+encodeURIComponent(agentId)).then(function(agentData){
        if(agentData&&!agentData.error){
          for(var i=0;i<D.agents.length;i++){
            if(D.agents[i].id===agentId){
              if(agentData.tools)D.agents[i].tools=agentData.tools;
              if(drawerAgent&&drawerAgent.id===agentId)drawerAgent=D.agents[i];
              break;
            }
          }
        }
      }).catch(function(){});
    })
    .catch(function(e){
      toast(e.message||"Failed to save flow","err");
    });
}

function _onOrchSaveSuccess(agentId,toolId,flowDef){
  _orchFlowLoadedFromServer=true;
  toast("Task flow saved","ok");
  _deferRestart("Task flow saved");
  // Re-render to show persistent checklist
  var db=Q("drawer-body");
  if(db&&drawerAgent&&drawerTab==="orchestrator"){
    db.innerHTML=renderOrchestrator(drawerAgent);
    var cl=document.querySelector(".orch-setup-checklist");
    if(cl)cl.scrollIntoView({behavior:"smooth"});
  }
}

// ── Delete Flow ──
function deleteOrchFlow(agentId,flowName){
  if(!confirm("Delete the task flow \""+flowName+"\"? This stages removal for Apply & Restart and restores on Discard."))return;
  api("tasks/flows/definition/"+encodeURIComponent(agentId)+"/"+encodeURIComponent(flowName)+"?defer=1",{method:"DELETE"})
    .then(function(r){
      if(r.error){toast(r.error,"err");return}
      toast("Flow deleted","ok");
      _deferRestart("Task flow deleted");
      _orchFlow={name:"",description:"",steps:[]};
      _orchFlowLoadedFromServer=false;
      _orchFlowLoadedFor=null;
      // Re-render the orchestrator tab
      var db=Q("drawer-body");
      if(db&&drawerAgent&&drawerTab==="orchestrator"){
        db.innerHTML=renderOrchestrator(drawerAgent);
      }
      // Refresh agent data to reflect alsoAllow change
      api("agents/"+encodeURIComponent(agentId)).then(function(agentData){
        if(agentData&&!agentData.error){
          for(var i=0;i<D.agents.length;i++){
            if(D.agents[i].id===agentId){
              if(agentData.tools)D.agents[i].tools=agentData.tools;
              if(drawerAgent&&drawerAgent.id===agentId)drawerAgent=D.agents[i];
              break;
            }
          }
        }
      }).catch(function(){});
    })
    .catch(function(e){toast(e.message||"Failed to delete flow","err")});
}

// ── Setup Checklist (inline HTML renderer) ──
function _renderSetupChecklist(a,f){
  var also=getToolAlso(a||{});
  var hasRunTaskFlow=also.indexOf("run_task_flow")>-1;
  var subagentConfig=(a&&a.subagents)||{};
  var allowAgents=subagentConfig.allowAgents||[];
  var uniqueStepAgents=[];
  (f.steps||[]).forEach(function(s){if(s.agentId&&uniqueStepAgents.indexOf(s.agentId)<0)uniqueStepAgents.push(s.agentId)});
  var missingAgents=uniqueStepAgents.filter(function(sa){return allowAgents.indexOf("*")<0&&allowAgents.indexOf(sa)<0});
  var hasAllAgents=allowAgents.indexOf("*")>-1||missingAgents.length===0;
  var h='<div class="orch-setup-checklist">';
  h+='<div class="orch-setup-header">Setup Checklist</div>';
  h+='<div class="orch-setup-body">';
  h+='<div class="orch-setup-item '+(hasRunTaskFlow?"done":"")+'">'
    +'<span class="orch-setup-icon">'+(hasRunTaskFlow?"✅":"⚠️")+'</span>'
    +(hasRunTaskFlow
      ?'<span>The <code>run_task_flow</code> tool is enabled for this agent.</span>'
      :'<span>Add <code>run_task_flow</code> to this agent\'s <code>tools.alsoAllow</code>.</span>')
    +'</div>';
  h+='<div class="orch-setup-item '+(hasAllAgents?"done":"")+'">'
    +'<span class="orch-setup-icon">'+(hasAllAgents?"✅":"⚠️")+'</span>'
    +(hasAllAgents
      ?'<span>Subagent relationships are configured — this agent can delegate to the step agents.</span>'
      :'<span>Add these agents to <code>subagents.allowAgents</code>: <code>'+esc(missingAgents.join(", "))+'</code></span>')
    +'</div>';
  h+='<div class="orch-setup-item"><span class="orch-setup-icon">📝</span>'
    +'<span>Ensure this agent\'s <strong>AGENTS.md</strong> has workflow instructions to call <code>run_task_flow</code> with <code>flowName: '+esc(f.name)+'</code>.</span></div>';
  h+='<div class="orch-setup-snippet-section">'
    +'<button class="btn btn-accent btn-sm" onclick="_generateAndShowSnippet(\''+esc(a.id)+'\')">Generate AGENTS.md Snippet</button>'
    +'<div id="agentsmd-snippet-area"></div></div>';
  h+='</div></div>';
  return h;
}

function _generateAndShowSnippet(agentId){
  if(!_orchFlow)return;
  var snippet=_generateAgentsMdSnippetClient(_orchFlow);
  var area=Q("agentsmd-snippet-area");
  if(!area)return;
  area.innerHTML='<textarea id="agentsmd-snippet-text" class="orch-snippet-textarea" rows="16" readonly>'+esc(snippet)+'</textarea>'
    +'<button class="btn btn-sm" onclick="_copyAgentsMdSnippet()">📋 Copy</button>';
}

function _copyAgentsMdSnippet(){
  var ta=Q("agentsmd-snippet-text");
  if(!ta)return;
  if(navigator.clipboard&&navigator.clipboard.writeText){
    navigator.clipboard.writeText(ta.value).then(function(){
      toast("Snippet copied to clipboard","ok");
    }).catch(function(){
      toast("Failed to copy — please copy manually","err");
    });
  }else{
    ta.select();
    try{document.execCommand("copy");toast("Snippet copied to clipboard","ok")}
    catch(e){toast("Failed to copy — please copy manually","err")}
  }
}

function _generateAgentsMdSnippetClient(flow){
  var toolName="run_task_flow";
  var lines=[];
  lines.push("# Workflow policy");
  lines.push("");
  lines.push("You are a coordination agent, not an implementation agent.");
  lines.push("");
  lines.push("For requests that match this workflow:");
  lines.push("- Do not perform the work yourself.");
  lines.push("- Call the `"+toolName+"` tool.");
  lines.push("- Pass:");
  lines.push("  - flowName: `"+flow.name+"`");
  lines.push("  - task summary");
  lines.push("");
  lines.push("Execution policy:");
  for(var i=0;i<flow.steps.length;i++){
    var step=flow.steps[i];
    var num=i+1;
    var line=num+". "+step.id+" (agent: "+step.agentId+")";
    if(step.description)line+=" — "+step.description;
    if(step.humanIntervention)line+=" [requires human approval]";
    lines.push(line);
  }
  lines.push("");
  lines.push("Approval policy:");
  var humanSteps=flow.steps.filter(function(s){return s.humanIntervention});
  if(humanSteps.length>0){
    lines.push("- Steps requiring human approval: "+humanSteps.map(function(s){return s.id}).join(", ")+".");
    lines.push("- When approval is required, the workflow must pause and wait rather than proceeding.");
  }else{
    lines.push("- No steps currently require human approval.");
  }
  lines.push("- Any destructive change, production deployment, secret rotation, infrastructure mutation, or irreversible action requires explicit user approval.");
  lines.push("");
  lines.push("Your responsibilities:");
  lines.push("- classify the request");
  lines.push("- start the workflow");
  lines.push("- surface failures or approval requests");
  lines.push("- summarize final outputs");
  lines.push("");
  lines.push("You must not:");
  lines.push("- implement work directly when the workflow applies");
  lines.push("- skip any flow steps");
  lines.push("- bypass approval gates");
  return lines.join("\n");
}

// ── Danger Tab ──
function renderDanger(a){
  return'<div class="danger-zone">'
    +'<div class="danger-zone-title">Danger Zone</div>'
    +'<p class="danger-zone-desc">Removing an agent stages deletion until Apply &amp; Restart. Workspace files and active flows are cleaned up on apply.</p>'
    +'<button class="btn btn-danger" onclick="deleteAgent(\''+esc(a.id)+'\')">Delete Agent</button></div>';
}
function deleteAgent(id){
  if(!confirm("Delete agent "+id+"? This stages removal for Apply & Restart and restores on Discard."))return;
  api(_deferParam("agents/"+encodeURIComponent(id)),{method:"DELETE"})
    .then(function(r){
      closeDrawer();
      load({fast:true});
      var msg="Agent removed";
      if(r.warnings&&r.warnings.length>0){
        msg+="\n\n"+r.warnings.map(function(w){return "• "+w;}).join("\n");
        toast(msg,"warn");
      }else{
        toast(msg,"ok");
      }
      _deferRestart(null,true);
    }).catch(function(e){toast(e.message,"err")});
}

// ── Channels Page (top-level) ──
function showChannelsPage(){
  location.hash="channels";
  openPagePanel("📡 Channels",
    '<div id="channels-body"><div class="loading-center"><span class="spin"></span> Loading…</div></div>');
  _loadEffectiveConfig({_quiet:true}).then(function(){
    renderChannelsPage();
  }).catch(function(){
    renderChannelsPage();
  });
}

function renderChannelsPage(){
  var el=Q("channels-body");if(!el)return;
  var allCh=_getVisibleChannels();
  var chNames=Object.keys(allCh);
  var bindings=D.bindings||[];

  var h='';

  h+='<div class="flex-between mb-lg">';
  h+='<div class="section-desc">Manage channel accounts and bind agents to them.</div>';
  h+='<div class="flex-row">';
  h+='<button class="btn btn-sm" onclick="showAddAccountModal()">+ Add Account</button>';
  h+='<button class="btn btn-accent btn-sm" onclick="showAddBindingModal()">+ Add Binding</button>';
  h+='</div></div>';
  if(chNames.length===0){
    h+='<div class="empty">';
    h+='<div class="empty-icon">📡</div>';
    h+='No channel accounts configured yet.<br><br>';
    h+='<button class="btn btn-accent" onclick="showAddAccountModal()">+ Add your first account</button></div>';
    el.innerHTML=h;return;
  }

  // Build flat list of account cards across all channels
  var usedBindingIdx={};
  h+='<div class="ch-grid">';
  chNames.forEach(function(ch){
    var cfg=allCh[ch]||{};
    var chEnabled=cfg.enabled!==false;
    var accs=cfg.accounts?Object.keys(cfg.accounts).filter(function(a){return a!=="default"||Object.keys((cfg.accounts||{})[a]||{}).length>0}):[];
    var chBindings=bindings.filter(function(b){return b.match&&b.match.channel===ch});

    // If no accounts, show a single channel-level card
    if(accs.length===0){
      if(Object.keys((cfg.accounts||{})).length===0&&chBindings.length>0)return;
      h+='<div class="ch-card">';
      h+='<div class="ch-card-head">';
      h+='<span class="ch-card-icon">'+chIcon(ch)+'</span>';
      h+='<span class="ch-card-name">'+esc(ch)+'</span>';
      h+='<div class="ch-card-actions">';
      h+='<span class="badge channel-status-badge '+(chEnabled?"badge-green":"badge-red")+'" onclick="toggleChannelPage(\''+esc(ch)+'\','+(!chEnabled)+')">'+(chEnabled?"Online":"Offline")+'</span>';
      h+='<button class="btn btn-sm" onclick="editChannelSettings(\''+esc(ch)+'\')">Edit</button>';
      h+='<button class="btn btn-sm btn-danger" onclick="deleteChannelPage(\''+esc(ch)+'\')">Remove</button>';
      h+='</div></div>';
      h+='<div class="ch-card-body">';
      h+='<div class="ch-int-empty center">No accounts configured.<br><br><button class="btn btn-accent btn-sm" onclick="showAddAccountModal(\''+esc(ch)+'\')">+ Add Account</button></div>';
      h+='</div></div>';
      return;
    }

    // One card per account
    accs.forEach(function(accName){
      var accCfg=(cfg.accounts||{})[accName]||{};
      var accEnabled=accCfg.enabled!==false;
      // Bindings for this specific account (exact match or wildcard)
      var accBindings=chBindings.filter(function(b){
        var m=b.match||{};
        return m.accountId===accName||m.accountId==="*"||(!m.accountId&&!m.peer);
      });

      h+='<div class="ch-card">';

      // Header: channel icon + account name + status
      h+='<div class="ch-card-head">';
      h+='<span class="ch-card-icon">'+chIcon(ch)+'</span>';
      h+='<div class="ch-card-head-info">';
      h+='<span class="ch-card-name">'+esc(accName)+'</span>';
      h+='<span class="ch-card-channel-type">'+esc(ch)+'</span>';
      h+='</div>';
      h+='<div class="ch-card-actions">';
      h+='<span class="ch-card-acc-dot" style="background:'+(accEnabled?"var(--green)":"var(--red)")+'"></span>';
      h+='<span class="badge channel-status-badge compact '+(chEnabled?"badge-green":"badge-red")+'" onclick="toggleChannelPage(\''+esc(ch)+'\','+(!chEnabled)+')">'+(chEnabled?"Online":"Offline")+'</span>';
      h+='<button class="btn btn-sm" onclick="editAccountPage(\''+esc(ch)+'\',\''+esc(accName)+'\')">Edit</button>';
      h+='<button class="btn btn-sm btn-danger" onclick="deleteAccount(\''+esc(ch)+'\',\''+esc(accName)+'\')">Remove</button>';
      h+='</div></div>';

      // Body
      h+='<div class="ch-card-body">';

      // Account info row
      if(accCfg.groupPolicy){
        h+='<div class="ch-card-meta"><span class="ch-card-meta-label">Policy</span> '+esc(accCfg.groupPolicy)+'</div>';
      }

      // Bindings for this account
      if(accBindings.length>0){
        h+='<div>';
        h+='<div class="ch-card-section-title">Bindings</div>';
        h+='<div class="flex-col" style="gap:6px">';
        accBindings.forEach(function(b){
          var aid=b.agentId||"?";
          var col=agentColor(aid);
          var m=b.match||{};
          var route="";
          if(m.peer)route=m.peer.kind+": "+m.peer.id;
          else if(m.accountId==="*")route="wildcard";
          else if(m.accountId)route="channel: "+(m.channel_id||m.guildId||m.teamId||"");
          // Find global index
          var gi=-1;for(var j=0;j<bindings.length;j++){if(bindings[j]===b){gi=j;usedBindingIdx[gi]=true;break}}

          h+='<div class="ch-card-binding" onclick="showEditBindingModal('+gi+')" style="cursor:pointer">';
          h+='<span class="ch-card-binding-arrow">→</span>';
          h+='<span class="ch-card-binding-agent" style="color:'+col+'">'+esc(aid)+'</span>';
          h+='<span class="ch-card-binding-route">'+esc(route)+'</span>';
          h+='<span class="ch-card-binding-actions">';
          h+='<span onclick="event.stopPropagation();showEditBindingModal('+gi+')" title="Edit">Edit</span>';
          h+='<span onclick="event.stopPropagation();removeBindingGlobal('+gi+')" title="Remove">Remove</span>';
          h+='</span></div>';
        });
        h+='</div></div>';
      }else{
        h+='<div class="ch-int-empty">No bindings for this account.</div>';
      }

      h+='</div>'; // end body

      // Footer
      h+='<div class="ch-card-footer">';
      h+='<button class="btn btn-sm" onclick="showAddBindingModal(\''+esc(ch)+'\')">+ Binding</button>';
      h+='</div>';

      h+='</div>'; // end card
    });
  });
  h+='</div>'; // end grid

  el.innerHTML=h;
}

function toggleChannelPage(name,enabled){
  api(_deferParam("channels/"+encodeURIComponent(name)),{method:"PUT",body:JSON.stringify({enabled:enabled})}).then(function(){
    if(D.channels&&D.channels[name])D.channels[name].enabled=enabled;
    _deferRestart("Channel "+(enabled?"enabled":"disabled"));
    _refreshEffectiveUi();
  }).catch(function(e){toast(e.message,"err")});
}
function deleteChannelPage(name){
  if(!confirm("Remove channel "+name+" and all its bindings?"))return;
  // Also remove bindings for this channel
  var remaining=(D.bindings||[]).filter(function(b){return!(b.match&&b.match.channel===name)});
  api(_deferParam("channels/"+encodeURIComponent(name)),{method:"DELETE"}).then(function(){
    return api(_deferParam("bindings"),{method:"PUT",body:JSON.stringify({bindings:remaining})});
  }).then(function(){
    if(D.channels&&D.channels[name])delete D.channels[name];
    D.bindings=remaining;
    toast("Channel removed","ok");
    _deferRestart("Channel removed");
    _refreshEffectiveUi();
  }).catch(function(e){toast(e.message,"err")});
}
function removeBindingGlobal(gi){
  var all=(D.bindings||[]).slice();
  if(gi<0||gi>=all.length)return;
  all.splice(gi,1);
  api(_deferParam("bindings"),{method:"PUT",body:JSON.stringify({bindings:all})}).then(function(){toast("Rule removed","ok");_deferRestart("Binding removed");D.bindings=all;_refreshEffectiveUi()}).catch(function(e){toast(e.message,"err")});
}

// ── Channel Configure / Add / Routing (new implementation) ──
var _echAccCount=0;

// Render a single field input for a channel form
function renderFieldInput(prefix,f,val){
  var id=prefix+f.key;
  var v=val||"";
  if(f.type==="select"){
    var h='<div class="fg">'+tip(f.label,f.tip||"")+'<select id="'+id+'">';
    (f.options||[]).forEach(function(o){h+='<option value="'+esc(o)+'"'+(v===o?" selected":"")+'>'+esc(o)+'</option>'});
    h+='</select></div>';
    return h;
  }
  if(f.type==="checkbox"){
    return'<div class="fg"><label class="perm-item perm-item-auto"><input type="checkbox" id="'+id+'"'+(v?" checked":"")+' /> '+esc(f.label)+'</label></div>';
  }
  var inputType=f.secret?"password":"text";
  return'<div class="fg">'+tip(f.label,f.tip||"")+'<input id="'+id+'" type="'+inputType+'" placeholder="'+esc(f.placeholder||"")+'" value="'+esc(v)+'" /></div>';
}

// Render a collapsible account form inside editChannelPage
function renderAccountForm(chName,accName,accData,idx){
  var fields=CH_ACCOUNT_FIELDS[chName]||[];
  var prefix="ech-acc-"+idx+"-";
  var h='<div class="account-form-card" id="ech-acc-block-'+idx+'">';
  h+='<div class="account-form-head">';
  h+='<span class="account-form-title">'+esc(accName)+'</span>';
  h+='<input type="hidden" id="ech-acc-name-'+idx+'" value="'+esc(accName)+'" />';
  if(accName!=="default")h+='<button class="btn btn-sm btn-danger" onclick="document.getElementById(\'ech-acc-block-'+idx+'\').remove()">Remove</button>';
  h+='</div>';
  h+='<div class="account-form-body">';
  // Enabled checkbox
  var enabled=accData.enabled!==false;
  h+='<div class="fg"><label class="perm-item perm-item-auto"><input type="checkbox" id="'+prefix+'enabled"'+(enabled?" checked":"")+' /> Enabled</label></div>';
  // Type-specific fields
  fields.forEach(function(f){
    h+=renderFieldInput(prefix,f,accData[f.key]||"");
  });
  // Discord-specific: guilds config
  if(chName==="discord"){
    h+=renderDiscordGuilds(prefix,accData);
  }
  // Commands config (Discord)
  if(chName==="discord"){
    var cmds=accData.commands||{};
    h+='<div class="guild-section-title">Commands</div>';
    h+='<div class="fg-row">';
    h+='<div class="fg"><label class="perm-item perm-item-auto"><input type="checkbox" id="'+prefix+'cmd-native"'+(cmds.native?" checked":"")+' /> Native Commands</label></div>';
    h+='<div class="fg"><label class="perm-item perm-item-auto"><input type="checkbox" id="'+prefix+'cmd-nativeSkills"'+(cmds.nativeSkills?" checked":"")+' /> Native Skills</label></div>';
    h+='</div>';
  }
  // Thread bindings (Discord)
  if(chName==="discord"){
    var tb=accData.threadBindings||{};
    h+='<div class="guild-section-title">Thread Bindings</div>';
    h+='<div class="fg"><label class="perm-item perm-item-auto"><input type="checkbox" id="'+prefix+'tb-enabled"'+(tb.enabled?" checked":"")+' /> Enable Thread Bindings</label></div>';
    h+='<div class="fg-row3">';
    h+='<div class="fg">'+tip("Idle Hours","Hours before an idle thread is unbound.")+'<input id="'+prefix+'tb-idleHours" type="number" value="'+esc(String(tb.idleHours||12))+'" /></div>';
    h+='<div class="fg">'+tip("Max Age Hours","Maximum thread age before unbinding.")+'<input id="'+prefix+'tb-maxAgeHours" type="number" value="'+esc(String(tb.maxAgeHours||48))+'" /></div>';
    h+='<div class="fg"><label class="perm-item perm-item-auto mt-lg"><input type="checkbox" id="'+prefix+'tb-spawnSub"'+(tb.spawnSubagentSessions?" checked":"")+' /> Spawn Subagent Sessions</label></div>';
    h+='</div>';
  }
  h+='</div></div>';
  return h;
}

// Discord guilds sub-editor
function renderDiscordGuilds(prefix,accData){
  var guilds=accData.guilds||{};
  var guildIds=Object.keys(guilds);
  var h='<div id="'+prefix+'guilds">';
  if(guildIds.length===0){
    h+='<div class="guild-empty">No guilds configured.</div>';
  }else{
    guildIds.forEach(function(gid,gi){
      var g=guilds[gid]||{};
      var gp=prefix+"g-"+gi+"-";
      var chans=g.channels||{};
      var chanIds=Object.keys(chans);
      h+='<div class="guild-block" id="'+gp+'block">';
      // Row 1: Guild ID + require mention + remove
      h+='<div class="guild-head-row">';
      h+='<div class="fg fg-no-margin">'+tip("Guild ID","Discord server ID.")+'<input id="'+gp+'id" value="'+esc(gid)+'" placeholder="1234567890" class="fg-compact" /></div>';
      h+='<label class="perm-item perm-item-auto"><input type="checkbox" id="'+gp+'requireMention"'+(g.requireMention?" checked":"")+' /> @mention</label>';
      h+='<button class="btn btn-sm btn-danger" onclick="document.getElementById(\''+gp+'block\').remove()">Remove</button>';
      h+='</div>';
      // Row 2: Users + Channels side by side
      h+='<div class="guild-body-row">';
      h+='<div class="fg fg-no-margin">'+tip("Allowed Users","Comma-separated user IDs.")+'<input id="'+gp+'users" value="'+esc((g.users||[]).join(", "))+'" placeholder="user IDs" class="fg-compact" /></div>';
      h+='<div class="fg fg-no-margin">'+tip("Allowed Channels","Comma-separated channel IDs.")+'<input id="'+gp+'channels" value="'+esc(chanIds.join(", "))+'" placeholder="channel IDs" class="fg-compact" /></div>';
      h+='</div>';
      h+='</div>';
    });
  }
  h+='</div>';
  h+='<button class="btn btn-sm" onclick="addDiscordGuild(\''+esc(prefix)+'\')" class="mt-sm">+ Add Guild</button>';
  return h;
}

var _guildCounter=100;
function addDiscordGuild(prefix){
  var container=Q(prefix+"guilds");if(!container)return;
  var gi=_guildCounter++;
  var gp=prefix+"g-"+gi+"-";
  var h='<div class="guild-block" id="'+gp+'block">';
  h+='<div class="guild-head-row">';
  h+='<div class="fg fg-no-margin">'+tip("Guild ID","Discord server ID.")+'<input id="'+gp+'id" value="" placeholder="1234567890" class="fg-compact" /></div>';
  h+='<label class="perm-item perm-item-auto"><input type="checkbox" id="'+gp+'requireMention" /> @mention</label>';
   h+='<button class="btn btn-sm btn-danger" onclick="document.getElementById(\''+gp+'block\').remove()">Remove</button>';
  h+='</div>';
  h+='<div class="guild-body-row">';
  h+='<div class="fg fg-no-margin">'+tip("Allowed Users","Comma-separated user IDs.")+'<input id="'+gp+'users" value="" placeholder="user IDs" class="fg-compact" /></div>';
  h+='<div class="fg fg-no-margin">'+tip("Allowed Channels","Comma-separated channel IDs.")+'<input id="'+gp+'channels" value="" placeholder="channel IDs" class="fg-compact" /></div>';
  h+='</div>';
  h+='</div>';
  var div=document.createElement("div");div.innerHTML=h;
  container.appendChild(div.firstElementChild);
}

// Collect account data from a rendered account form
function collectAccountData(chName,idx){
  var prefix="ech-acc-"+idx+"-";
  var fields=CH_ACCOUNT_FIELDS[chName]||[];
  var obj={};
  // Enabled
  var enEl=Q(prefix+"enabled");
  if(enEl)obj.enabled=enEl.checked;
  // Type-specific fields
  fields.forEach(function(f){
    var el=Q(prefix+f.key);
    if(!el)return;
    var v=el.value.trim();
    if(f.type==="checkbox"){obj[f.key]=el.checked}
    else if(v)obj[f.key]=v;
  });
  // Discord-specific
  if(chName==="discord"){
    // Commands
    var cmdNative=Q(prefix+"cmd-native");
    var cmdSkills=Q(prefix+"cmd-nativeSkills");
    if(cmdNative||cmdSkills){
      obj.commands={};
      if(cmdNative)obj.commands.native=cmdNative.checked;
      if(cmdSkills)obj.commands.nativeSkills=cmdSkills.checked;
    }
    // Thread bindings
    var tbEn=Q(prefix+"tb-enabled");
    if(tbEn){
      obj.threadBindings={enabled:tbEn.checked};
      var tbIdle=Q(prefix+"tb-idleHours");if(tbIdle&&tbIdle.value)obj.threadBindings.idleHours=parseInt(tbIdle.value)||12;
      var tbMax=Q(prefix+"tb-maxAgeHours");if(tbMax&&tbMax.value)obj.threadBindings.maxAgeHours=parseInt(tbMax.value)||48;
      var tbSub=Q(prefix+"tb-spawnSub");if(tbSub)obj.threadBindings.spawnSubagentSessions=tbSub.checked;
    }
    // Guilds
    var guildsContainer=Q(prefix+"guilds");
    if(guildsContainer){
      var guildBlocks=guildsContainer.querySelectorAll("[id$='-block']");
      if(guildBlocks.length>0){
        obj.guilds={};
        guildBlocks.forEach(function(block){
          var bp=block.id.replace("block","");
          var gidEl=Q(bp+"id");if(!gidEl||!gidEl.value.trim())return;
          var gid=gidEl.value.trim();
          var gObj={};
          var rmEl=Q(bp+"requireMention");if(rmEl)gObj.requireMention=rmEl.checked;
          var usersEl=Q(bp+"users");if(usersEl&&usersEl.value.trim())gObj.users=usersEl.value.split(",").map(function(s){return s.trim()}).filter(Boolean);
          var chansEl=Q(bp+"channels");
          if(chansEl&&chansEl.value.trim()){
            gObj.channels={};
            chansEl.value.split(",").map(function(s){return s.trim()}).filter(Boolean).forEach(function(cid){
              gObj.channels[cid]={enabled:true};
            });
          }
          obj.guilds[gid]=gObj;
        });
      }
    }
  }
  return obj;
}

function editChannelSettings(chName){
  var cfg=JSON.parse(JSON.stringify((D.channels||{})[chName]||{}));
  var chFields=CH_CHANNEL_FIELDS[chName]||[];

  var h='<div class="modal-form">';
  h+='<div class="ch-settings-header">';
  h+='<span class="ch-settings-icon">'+chIcon(chName)+'</span>';
  h+='<div class="ch-settings-title">'+esc(chName)+' Settings</div></div>';

  h+='<div class="fg"><label class="perm-item perm-item-auto"><input type="checkbox" id="ech-enabled"'+(cfg.enabled!==false?" checked":"")+' /> Enabled</label></div>';
  chFields.forEach(function(f){
    h+=renderFieldInput("ech-ch-",f,cfg[f.key]||"");
  });

  h+='<div class="flex-row mt-lg">';
  h+='<button class="btn btn-accent" onclick="saveChannelSettings(\''+esc(chName)+'\')">Save</button>';
  h+='<button class="btn" onclick="closeModal()">Cancel</button></div>';
  h+='</div>';
  openModal("Channel Settings",h);
}

function saveChannelSettings(chName){
  var config=JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(D.config));
  if(!config.channels)config.channels={};
  if(!config.channels[chName])config.channels[chName]={};
  var ch=config.channels[chName];
  var enEl=Q("ech-enabled");
  ch.enabled=enEl?enEl.checked:true;
  var chFields=CH_CHANNEL_FIELDS[chName]||[];
  chFields.forEach(function(f){
    var el=Q("ech-ch-"+f.key);
    if(!el)return;
    var v=el.value.trim();
    if(f.type==="checkbox"){ch[f.key]=el.checked}
    else if(v)ch[f.key]=v;
    else delete ch[f.key];
  });
  api("config?defer=1",{method:"PUT",body:JSON.stringify({config:config})})
    .then(function(){toast("Settings saved","ok");_deferRestart("Channel settings saved");_setEffectiveConfig(config);closeModal();_refreshEffectiveUi()})
    .catch(function(e){toast(e.message,"err")});
}

// ── Edit a single account ──
function editAccountPage(chName,accName){
  var cfg=JSON.parse(JSON.stringify((D.channels||{})[chName]||{}));
  var accData=(cfg.accounts||{})[accName]||{};
  var prefix="ea-";

  var h='<div class="modal-medium">';
  // Header row
  h+='<div class="acc-edit-header">';
  h+='<span class="acc-edit-icon">'+chIcon(chName)+'</span>';
  h+='<div class="flex-1">';
  h+='<div class="acc-edit-name">'+esc(accName)+'</div>';
  h+='<div class="acc-edit-type">'+esc(chName)+' account</div>';
  h+='</div>';
  var accEnabled=accData.enabled!==false;
  h+='<label class="perm-item perm-item-auto"><input type="checkbox" id="'+prefix+'enabled"'+(accEnabled?" checked":"")+' /> Enabled</label>';
  h+='</div>';

  // ── Basic Settings (two-column grid) ──
  var fields=CH_ACCOUNT_FIELDS[chName]||[];
  if(fields.length>0){
    h+='<div class="fg-row" style="margin-bottom:16px">';
    fields.forEach(function(f){
      h+=renderFieldInput(prefix,f,accData[f.key]||"");
    });
    h+='</div>';
  }

  // ── Channel Settings (collapsible, merged from channel-level config) ──
  var chFields=(CH_CHANNEL_FIELDS[chName]||[]).filter(function(f){return f.key!=="defaultAccount"});
  if(chFields.length>0){
    h+='<div class="collapsible">';
    h+='<div class="collapsible-head" onclick="var b=this.nextElementSibling;b.style.display=b.style.display===\'none\'?\'block\':\'none\';this.querySelector(\'.ea-chev\').textContent=b.style.display===\'none\'?\'▸\':\'▾\'">';
    h+='<span class="ea-chev collapsible-chevron">▾</span>';
    h+='<span class="collapsible-label">Channel Settings</span>';
    h+='</div>';
    h+='<div style="padding:0 14px 12px">';
    h+='<div class="fg-row">';
    chFields.forEach(function(f){
      h+=renderFieldInput(prefix+"ch-",f,cfg[f.key]||"");
    });
    h+='</div>';
    h+='</div></div>';
  }

  // Discord-specific collapsible sections
  if(chName==="discord"){
    // ── Commands (inline, compact) ──
    var cmds=accData.commands||{};
    h+='<div class="collapsible">';
    h+='<div class="collapsible-head" onclick="var b=this.nextElementSibling;b.style.display=b.style.display===\'none\'?\'block\':\'none\';this.querySelector(\'.ea-chev\').textContent=b.style.display===\'none\'?\'▸\':\'▾\'">';
    h+='<span class="ea-chev collapsible-chevron">▾</span>';
    h+='<span class="collapsible-label">Commands</span>';
    h+='</div>';
    h+='<div style="padding:0 14px 12px;display:flex;gap:16px">';
    h+='<label class="perm-item perm-item-auto"><input type="checkbox" id="'+prefix+'cmd-native"'+(cmds.native?" checked":"")+' /> Native Commands</label>';
    h+='<label class="perm-item perm-item-auto"><input type="checkbox" id="'+prefix+'cmd-nativeSkills"'+(cmds.nativeSkills?" checked":"")+' /> Native Skills</label>';
    h+='</div></div>';

    // ── Thread Bindings (collapsible) ──
    var tb=accData.threadBindings||{};
    h+='<div class="collapsible">';
    h+='<div class="collapsible-head" onclick="var b=this.nextElementSibling;b.style.display=b.style.display===\'none\'?\'block\':\'none\';this.querySelector(\'.ea-chev\').textContent=b.style.display===\'none\'?\'▸\':\'▾\'">';
    h+='<span class="ea-chev collapsible-chevron">'+(tb.enabled?'▾':'▸')+'</span>';
    h+='<span class="collapsible-label">Thread Bindings</span>';
    h+='<span class="collapsible-meta">'+(tb.enabled?'enabled':'disabled')+'</span>';
    h+='</div>';
    h+='<div style="padding:0 14px 12px;display:'+(tb.enabled?'block':'none')+'">';
    h+='<div class="tb-row" style="display:grid;grid-template-columns:auto 1fr 1fr auto;gap:10px;align-items:center">';
    h+='<label class="perm-item perm-item-auto"><input type="checkbox" id="'+prefix+'tb-enabled"'+(tb.enabled?" checked":"")+' /> Enabled</label>';
    h+='<div class="fg fg-no-margin">'+tip("Idle Hours","Hours before idle thread unbound.")+'<input id="'+prefix+'tb-idleHours" type="number" value="'+esc(String(tb.idleHours||12))+'" /></div>';
    h+='<div class="fg fg-no-margin">'+tip("Max Age Hours","Max thread age.")+'<input id="'+prefix+'tb-maxAgeHours" type="number" value="'+esc(String(tb.maxAgeHours||48))+'" /></div>';
    h+='<label class="perm-item perm-item-auto"><input type="checkbox" id="'+prefix+'tb-spawnSub"'+(tb.spawnSubagentSessions?" checked":"")+' /> Spawn Sub</label>';
    h+='</div></div></div>';

    // ── Guilds (collapsible) ──
    h+='<div class="collapsible">';
    h+='<div class="collapsible-head" onclick="var b=this.nextElementSibling;b.style.display=b.style.display===\'none\'?\'block\':\'none\';this.querySelector(\'.ea-chev\').textContent=b.style.display===\'none\'?\'▸\':\'▾\'">';
    h+='<span class="ea-chev collapsible-chevron">▾</span>';
    h+='<span class="collapsible-label">Guilds</span>';
    var guildCount=Object.keys(accData.guilds||{}).length;
    h+='<span class="collapsible-meta">'+guildCount+' guild'+(guildCount!==1?'s':'')+'</span>';
    h+='</div>';
    h+='<div style="padding:0 14px 12px">';
    h+=renderDiscordGuilds(prefix,accData);
    h+='</div></div>';
  }

  // Actions
  h+='<div style="display:flex;gap:8px;margin-top:16px;align-items:center;padding-top:12px;border-top:1px solid var(--border)">';
  h+='<button class="btn btn-accent" onclick="saveAccountConfig(\''+esc(chName)+'\',\''+esc(accName)+'\')">Save</button>';
  h+='<button class="btn" onclick="closeModal()">Cancel</button>';
  if(accName!=="default"){
    h+='<button class="btn btn-danger" style="margin-left:auto" onclick="deleteAccount(\''+esc(chName)+'\',\''+esc(accName)+'\')">Delete Account</button>';
  }
  h+='</div>';
  h+='</div>';
  openModal("Edit Account",h);
}

// ── Add Binding modal: pick agent, account, optional peer channel ──
function showAddBindingModal(chName){
  var agents=D.agents||[];
  var allCh=D.channels||{};
  var chNames=Object.keys(allCh);

  var h='<div class="modal-form">';
  h+='<div class="fg">'+tip("Agent","Which agent should handle messages.")
    +'<select id="ab-agent"><option value="">Select agent…</option>';
  agents.forEach(function(a){h+='<option value="'+esc(a.id)+'">'+esc(a.name||a.id)+'</option>'});
  h+='</select></div>';

  // Channel type picker (if not pre-set)
  if(!chName){
    h+='<div class="fg">'+tip("Channel","Which channel type to bind to.")
      +'<select id="ab-ch" onchange="onBindingChChange()">';
    if(chNames.length>1)h+='<option value="">Select channel…</option>';
    chNames.forEach(function(c){h+='<option value="'+esc(c)+'"'+(chNames.length===1?' selected':'')+'>'+chIcon(c)+' '+esc(c)+'</option>'});
    h+='</select></div>';
  }

  // Account + peer sections (dynamic)
  h+='<div id="ab-dynamic">';
  var resolvedCh=chName||(chNames.length===1?chNames[0]:"");
  if(resolvedCh)h+=_buildBindingAccPeer(resolvedCh);
  h+='</div>';

  h+='<div class="file-actions-row mt-md">';
  h+='<button class="btn" onclick="closeModal()">Cancel</button>';
  h+='<button class="btn btn-accent" onclick="doAddBinding(\''+esc(chName||"")+'\')">'+'Add Binding</button></div>';
  h+='</div>';
  openModal("Add Binding"+(chName?" — "+chName:""),h);
  // Trigger initial known channels render
  if(resolvedCh)setTimeout(function(){onBindingAccChange(resolvedCh)},0);
}

function _buildBindingAccPeer(chName){
  var cfg=(D.channels||{})[chName]||{};
  var accs=cfg.accounts?Object.keys(cfg.accounts):[];
  var h='';
  h+='<div class="fg">'+tip("Account","Which account to bind.")
    +'<select id="ab-acc" onchange="onBindingAccChange(\''+esc(chName)+'\')">';
  if(accs.length>1)h+='<option value="">any (all accounts)</option>';
  accs.forEach(function(a){h+='<option value="'+esc(a)+'">'+esc(a)+'</option>'});
  h+='</select></div>';
  if(chName==="discord"){
    h+='<div class="fg" id="ab-peer-section">'+tip("Discord Channel (optional)","Specific Discord channel ID to route. Leave empty to route all.")
      +'<input id="ab-peer-id" placeholder="e.g. 1482374954996732127" />';
    h+='<div id="ab-known-channels" class="mt-sm"></div>';
    h+='</div>';
  }else{
    h+='<div class="fg">'+tip("Peer Filter (optional)","Format: kind:id. Leave empty to match all.")
      +'<input id="ab-peer-raw" placeholder="channel:123456" /></div>';
  }
  return h;
}

function onBindingChChange(){
  var chName=V("ab-ch");
  var container=Q("ab-dynamic");
  if(!container)return;
  if(!chName){container.innerHTML="";return}
  container.innerHTML=_buildBindingAccPeer(chName);
  setTimeout(function(){onBindingAccChange(chName)},0);
}

function onBindingAccChange(chName){
  var container=Q("ab-known-channels");
  if(!container)return;
  var accName=V("ab-acc").trim();
  var cfg=(D.channels||{})[chName]||{};

  var knownChannels=[];
  var accsToScan=accName?[accName]:Object.keys(cfg.accounts||{});
  accsToScan.forEach(function(an){
    var accCfg=(cfg.accounts||{})[an]||{};
    var guilds=accCfg.guilds||{};
    Object.keys(guilds).forEach(function(gid){
      var gChans=(guilds[gid]||{}).channels||{};
      Object.keys(gChans).forEach(function(cid){
        if(knownChannels.indexOf(cid)<0)knownChannels.push(cid);
      });
    });
  });

  if(knownChannels.length===0){
    container.innerHTML='<span class="section-desc">No configured channels for this account.</span>';
    return;
  }
  var h='<div class="flex-row-wrap">';
  h+='<span class="section-desc w-full mb-sm">Known channels (click to fill):</span>';
  knownChannels.forEach(function(cid){
    h+='<span style="padding:2px 8px;border-radius:4px;font-size:var(--fs-xs);font-family:monospace;background:var(--bg3);border:1px solid var(--border);cursor:pointer;color:var(--tx2)" onclick="Q(\'ab-peer-id\').value=\''+esc(cid)+'\'">'+esc(cid)+'</span>';
  });
  h+='</div>';
  container.innerHTML=h;
}

function doAddBinding(chName){
  if(!chName)chName=V("ab-ch");
  if(!chName){toast("Select a channel","err");return}
  var agentId=V("ab-agent");
  if(!agentId){toast("Select an agent","err");return}
  var acc=V("ab-acc").trim();
  var match={channel:chName};
  if(acc)match.accountId=acc;

  if(chName==="discord"){
    var peerId=V("ab-peer-id").trim();
    if(peerId)match.peer={kind:"channel",id:peerId};
  }else{
    var peerRaw=V("ab-peer-raw").trim();
    if(peerRaw&&peerRaw.indexOf(":")>-1){
      var parts=peerRaw.split(":");
      match.peer={kind:parts[0],id:parts.slice(1).join(":")};
    }
  }

  var all=(D.bindings||[]).concat([{agentId:agentId,match:match}]);
  api(_deferParam("bindings"),{method:"PUT",body:JSON.stringify({bindings:all})}).then(function(){
    toast("Binding added","ok");_deferRestart("Binding added");D.bindings=all;closeModal();_refreshEffectiveUi();
  }).catch(function(e){toast(e.message,"err")});
}

// ── Edit Binding modal: modify an existing binding in-place ──
function showEditBindingModal(gi){
  var bindings=D.bindings||[];
  if(gi<0||gi>=bindings.length)return;
  var b=bindings[gi];
  var m=b.match||{};
  var chName=m.channel||"";
  var agents=D.agents||[];
  var allCh=D.channels||{};
  var chNames=Object.keys(allCh);

  var h='<div class="modal-form">';
  h+='<div class="fg">'+tip("Agent","Which agent should handle messages.")
    +'<select id="eb-agent">';
  agents.forEach(function(a){h+='<option value="'+esc(a.id)+'"'+(a.id===b.agentId?' selected':'')+'>'+esc(a.name||a.id)+'</option>'});
  h+='</select></div>';

  h+='<div class="fg">'+tip("Channel","Which channel type to bind to.")
    +'<select id="eb-ch" onchange="onEditBindingChChange()">';
  chNames.forEach(function(c){h+='<option value="'+esc(c)+'"'+(c===chName?' selected':'')+'>'+chIcon(c)+' '+esc(c)+'</option>'});
  h+='</select></div>';

  h+='<div id="eb-dynamic">';
  if(chName)h+=_buildEditBindingAccPeer(chName,m);
  h+='</div>';

  h+='<div class="file-actions-row mt-md">';
  h+='<button class="btn" onclick="closeModal()">Cancel</button>';
  h+='<button class="btn btn-accent" onclick="doEditBinding('+gi+')">Save</button></div>';
  h+='</div>';
  openModal("Edit Binding",h);
  // Constrain modal width for this small form
  var modalEl=document.querySelector("#modal-bg .modal");if(modalEl)modalEl.style.maxWidth="520px";
  if(chName)setTimeout(function(){onEditBindingAccChange(chName)},0);
}

function _buildEditBindingAccPeer(chName,m){
  var cfg=(D.channels||{})[chName]||{};
  var accs=cfg.accounts?Object.keys(cfg.accounts):[];
  var curAcc=m.accountId||"";
  var h='';
  h+='<div class="fg">'+tip("Account","Which account to bind.")
    +'<select id="eb-acc" onchange="onEditBindingAccChange(\''+esc(chName)+'\')">';
  h+='<option value="">any (all accounts)</option>';
  accs.forEach(function(a){h+='<option value="'+esc(a)+'"'+(a===curAcc?' selected':'')+'>'+esc(a)+'</option>'});
  h+='</select></div>';
  if(chName==="discord"){
    var peerId=(m.peer&&m.peer.id)||"";
    h+='<div class="fg" id="eb-peer-section">'+tip("Discord Channel (optional)","Specific Discord channel ID to route. Leave empty to route all.")
      +'<input id="eb-peer-id" placeholder="e.g. 1482374954996732127" value="'+esc(peerId)+'" />';
    h+='<div id="eb-known-channels" class="mt-sm"></div>';
    h+='</div>';
  }else{
    var peerRaw=(m.peer?(m.peer.kind+":"+m.peer.id):"");
    h+='<div class="fg">'+tip("Peer Filter (optional)","Format: kind:id. Leave empty to match all.")
      +'<input id="eb-peer-raw" placeholder="channel:123456" value="'+esc(peerRaw)+'" /></div>';
  }
  return h;
}

function onEditBindingChChange(){
  var chName=V("eb-ch");
  var container=Q("eb-dynamic");
  if(!container)return;
  if(!chName){container.innerHTML="";return}
  container.innerHTML=_buildEditBindingAccPeer(chName,{});
  setTimeout(function(){onEditBindingAccChange(chName)},0);
}

function onEditBindingAccChange(chName){
  var container=Q("eb-known-channels");
  if(!container)return;
  var accName=V("eb-acc").trim();
  var cfg=(D.channels||{})[chName]||{};
  var knownChannels=[];
  var accsToScan=accName?[accName]:Object.keys(cfg.accounts||{});
  accsToScan.forEach(function(an){
    var accCfg=(cfg.accounts||{})[an]||{};
    var guilds=accCfg.guilds||{};
    Object.keys(guilds).forEach(function(gid){
      var gChans=(guilds[gid]||{}).channels||{};
      Object.keys(gChans).forEach(function(cid){
        if(knownChannels.indexOf(cid)<0)knownChannels.push(cid);
      });
    });
  });
  if(knownChannels.length===0){
    container.innerHTML='<span class="section-desc">No configured channels for this account.</span>';
    return;
  }
  var h='<div class="flex-row-wrap">';
  h+='<span class="section-desc w-full mb-sm">Known channels (click to fill):</span>';
  knownChannels.forEach(function(cid){
    h+='<span style="padding:2px 8px;border-radius:4px;font-size:var(--fs-xs);font-family:monospace;background:var(--bg3);border:1px solid var(--border);cursor:pointer;color:var(--tx2)" onclick="Q(\'eb-peer-id\').value=\''+esc(cid)+'\'">'+esc(cid)+'</span>';
  });
  h+='</div>';
  container.innerHTML=h;
}

function doEditBinding(gi){
  var chName=V("eb-ch");
  if(!chName){toast("Select a channel","err");return}
  var agentId=V("eb-agent");
  if(!agentId){toast("Select an agent","err");return}
  var acc=V("eb-acc").trim();
  var match={channel:chName};
  if(acc)match.accountId=acc;

  if(chName==="discord"){
    var peerId=V("eb-peer-id").trim();
    if(peerId)match.peer={kind:"channel",id:peerId};
  }else{
    var peerRaw=V("eb-peer-raw").trim();
    if(peerRaw&&peerRaw.indexOf(":")>-1){
      var parts=peerRaw.split(":");
      match.peer={kind:parts[0],id:parts.slice(1).join(":")};
    }
  }

  var all=(D.bindings||[]).slice();
  all[gi]={agentId:agentId,match:match};
  api(_deferParam("bindings"),{method:"PUT",body:JSON.stringify({bindings:all})}).then(function(){
    toast("Binding updated","ok");_deferRestart("Binding updated");D.bindings=all;closeModal();_refreshEffectiveUi();
  }).catch(function(e){toast(e.message,"err")});
}

function saveAccountConfig(chName,accName){
  var prefix="ea-";
  var config=JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(D.config));
  if(!config.channels)config.channels={};
  if(!config.channels[chName])config.channels[chName]={};
  if(!config.channels[chName].accounts)config.channels[chName].accounts={};

  var obj={};
  // Enabled
  var enEl=Q(prefix+"enabled");
  if(enEl)obj.enabled=enEl.checked;
  // Type-specific fields
  var fields=CH_ACCOUNT_FIELDS[chName]||[];
  fields.forEach(function(f){
    var el=Q(prefix+f.key);
    if(!el)return;
    var v=el.value.trim();
    if(f.type==="checkbox"){obj[f.key]=el.checked}
    else if(v)obj[f.key]=v;
  });
  // Discord-specific
  if(chName==="discord"){
    var cmdNative=Q(prefix+"cmd-native");
    var cmdSkills=Q(prefix+"cmd-nativeSkills");
    if(cmdNative||cmdSkills){
      obj.commands={};
      if(cmdNative)obj.commands.native=cmdNative.checked;
      if(cmdSkills)obj.commands.nativeSkills=cmdSkills.checked;
    }
    var tbEn=Q(prefix+"tb-enabled");
    if(tbEn){
      obj.threadBindings={enabled:tbEn.checked};
      var tbIdle=Q(prefix+"tb-idleHours");if(tbIdle&&tbIdle.value)obj.threadBindings.idleHours=parseInt(tbIdle.value)||12;
      var tbMax=Q(prefix+"tb-maxAgeHours");if(tbMax&&tbMax.value)obj.threadBindings.maxAgeHours=parseInt(tbMax.value)||48;
      var tbSub=Q(prefix+"tb-spawnSub");if(tbSub)obj.threadBindings.spawnSubagentSessions=tbSub.checked;
    }
    // Guilds
    var guildsContainer=Q(prefix+"guilds");
    if(guildsContainer){
      var guildBlocks=guildsContainer.querySelectorAll("[id$='-block']");
      if(guildBlocks.length>0){
        obj.guilds={};
        guildBlocks.forEach(function(block){
          var bp=block.id.replace("block","");
          var gidEl=Q(bp+"id");if(!gidEl||!gidEl.value.trim())return;
          var gid=gidEl.value.trim();
          var gObj={};
          var rmEl=Q(bp+"requireMention");if(rmEl)gObj.requireMention=rmEl.checked;
          var usersEl=Q(bp+"users");if(usersEl&&usersEl.value.trim())gObj.users=usersEl.value.split(",").map(function(s){return s.trim()}).filter(Boolean);
          var chansEl=Q(bp+"channels");
          if(chansEl&&chansEl.value.trim()){
            gObj.channels={};
            chansEl.value.split(",").map(function(s){return s.trim()}).filter(Boolean).forEach(function(cid){
              gObj.channels[cid]={enabled:true};
            });
          }
          obj.guilds[gid]=gObj;
        });
      }
    }
  }

  config.channels[chName].accounts[accName]=obj;
  // Also save channel-level fields if present
  var chFields=CH_CHANNEL_FIELDS[chName]||[];
  chFields.forEach(function(f){
    var el=Q("ea-ch-"+f.key);
    if(!el)return;
    var v=el.value.trim();
    if(f.type==="checkbox"){config.channels[chName][f.key]=el.checked}
    else if(v)config.channels[chName][f.key]=v;
    else delete config.channels[chName][f.key];
  });
  api("config?defer=1",{method:"PUT",body:JSON.stringify({config:config})})
    .then(function(){toast("Account saved","ok");_deferRestart("Account saved");_setEffectiveConfig(config);closeModal();_refreshEffectiveUi()})
    .catch(function(e){toast(e.message,"err")});
}

function deleteAccount(chName,accName){
  if(!confirm("Delete account "+accName+" from "+chName+"?"))return;
  var config=JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(D.config));
  if(config.channels&&config.channels[chName]&&config.channels[chName].accounts){
    delete config.channels[chName].accounts[accName];
  }
  api("config?defer=1",{method:"PUT",body:JSON.stringify({config:config})})
    .then(function(){toast("Account deleted","ok");_deferRestart("Account deleted");_setEffectiveConfig(config);closeModal();_refreshEffectiveUi()})
    .catch(function(e){toast(e.message,"err")});
}

function showAddAccountModal(chName){
  var h='<div class="modal-form">';
  // If no channel type passed, show type picker first
  if(!chName){
    h+='<div class="fg">'+tip("Channel Type","Select the messaging platform.")
      +'<select id="nac-type" onchange="onAddAccTypeChange()">';
    h+='<option value="">Select…</option>';
    CH_TYPES.forEach(function(c){h+='<option value="'+c+'">'+chIcon(c)+' '+c+'</option>'});
    h+='</select></div>';
  }
  h+='<div class="fg">'+tip("Account ID","A unique name for this account, e.g. my-discord-bot.")+'<input id="nac-name" placeholder="my-bot" /></div>';
  h+='<div id="nac-fields">';
  if(chName){
    var fields=CH_ACCOUNT_FIELDS[chName]||[];
    fields.forEach(function(f){
      h+=renderFieldInput("nac-",f,"");
    });
  }
  h+='</div>';
  h+='<div style="display:flex;gap:8px;margin-top:16px;justify-content:flex-end">';
  h+='<button class="btn" onclick="closeModal()">Cancel</button>';
  h+='<button class="btn btn-accent" onclick="doAddAccount(\''+esc(chName||"")+'\')">'+(chName?'Add Account':'Add Account')+'</button></div>';
  h+='</div>';
  openModal(chName?"Add Account — "+chName:"Add Account",h);
}

function onAddAccTypeChange(){
  var type=V("nac-type");
  var container=Q("nac-fields");if(!container)return;
  if(!type){container.innerHTML="";return}
  var fields=CH_ACCOUNT_FIELDS[type]||[];
  var fh='';
  fields.forEach(function(f){fh+=renderFieldInput("nac-",f,"")});
  container.innerHTML=fh;
}

function doAddAccount(chName){
  // If no chName passed, read from type picker
  if(!chName)chName=V("nac-type");
  if(!chName){toast("Select a channel type","err");return}
  var accName=V("nac-name").trim();
  if(!accName){toast("Account name required","err");return}
  var fields=CH_ACCOUNT_FIELDS[chName]||[];
  var obj={enabled:true};
  fields.forEach(function(f){
    var el=Q("nac-"+f.key);
    if(!el)return;
    var v=el.value.trim();
    if(f.type==="checkbox"){obj[f.key]=el.checked}
    else if(v)obj[f.key]=v;
  });
  var config=JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(D.config));
  if(!config.channels)config.channels={};
  if(!config.channels[chName])config.channels[chName]={enabled:true,accounts:{}};
  if(!config.channels[chName].accounts)config.channels[chName].accounts={};
  config.channels[chName].accounts[accName]=obj;
  config.channels[chName].enabled=true;
  api("config?defer=1",{method:"PUT",body:JSON.stringify({config:config})})
    .then(function(){toast("Account added","ok");_deferRestart("Account added");_setEffectiveConfig(config);closeModal();_refreshEffectiveUi()})
    .catch(function(e){toast(e.message,"err")});
}

// ── Models Manager ──
var _modelsApiTab="aliases"; // "aliases" or "status"
function showModelsAndApi(tab){
  location.hash="models";
  _modelsApiTab=tab||"aliases";
  var h='<div class="models-tabs">';
  h+='<div class="dtab clickable'+(_modelsApiTab==="aliases"?" active":"")+'" onclick="showModelsAndApi(\'aliases\')">Model Aliases</div>';
  h+='<div class="dtab clickable'+(_modelsApiTab==="status"?" active":"")+'" onclick="showModelsAndApi(\'status\')">API Status</div>';
  h+='</div>';
  h+='<div id="models-api-body"></div>';
  openPagePanel("🧠 Models & API",h);
  if(_modelsApiTab==="aliases")_renderAliasesTab();
  else _renderApiStatusTab();
}
// Keep old names working
function showModels(){showModelsAndApi("aliases")}
function showProviderStatus(){showModelsAndApi("status")}

function _renderAliasesTab(){
  var el=Q("models-api-body");if(!el)return;
  var aliasMap=getModelAliasMap();
  var aliases=Object.keys(aliasMap);
  var h='<div>';
  h+='<div class="alias-help-text">Map short alias names to <code class="code-hint">provider/model</code> pairs. Agents reference aliases instead of full model IDs. Multiple aliases can point to the same model.</div>';
  h+='<div class="model-header">';
  h+='<span>Alias</span><span>Provider</span><span>Model</span><span></span></div>';
  h+='<div id="models-list" class="alias-list">';
  aliases.forEach(function(alias,i){
    h+=modelRow(i,alias,aliasMap[alias]);
  });
  h+='</div>';
  h+='<button class="btn btn-sm alias-add-btn" onclick="addModelRow()">+ Add Alias</button>';
  h+='<div class="flex-row mt-lg">';
  h+='<button class="btn btn-accent" onclick="saveModels()">Save</button>';
  h+='<button class="btn" onclick="closePagePanel()">Cancel</button></div>';
  h+='</div>';
  el.innerHTML=h;
  // Populate dropdowns after render
  setTimeout(function(){_populateAllModelDropdowns()},0);
}

function _renderApiStatusTab(){
  var el=Q("models-api-body");if(!el)return;
  el.innerHTML='<div class="loading-center"><span class="spin"></span> Checking providers…</div>';
  _loadApiStatusInto(el);
}

function _forceRefreshApiStatus(){
  var el=Q("models-api-body");
  if(el)el.innerHTML='<div class="loading-center"><span class="spin"></span> Refreshing providers…</div>';
  api("models/status/refresh",{method:"POST"}).then(function(d){
    if(el){
      // Re-render with fresh data
      _renderApiStatusTab();
    }
  }).catch(function(e){
    if(el)el.innerHTML='<div class="health-err" style="padding:20px">Refresh failed: '+esc(e.message)+'</div>';
  });
}

function modelRow(i,alias,providerModel){
  var parts=(providerModel||"").split("/");
  var provider=parts[0]||"";
  var modelId=parts.slice(1).join("/")||"";
  return'<div class="model-row model-row-grid" id="mrow-'+i+'">'
    +'<div><input id="ma-'+i+'" value="'+esc(alias)+'" placeholder="e.g. the-brain" class="model-row-alias" /><label class="model-row-label accent">Alias</label></div>'
    +'<div><select id="mp-'+i+'" onchange="_onProviderDropdown('+i+')" class="model-row-select"><option value="'+esc(provider)+'">'+esc(provider||"— provider —")+'</option></select><label class="model-row-label">Provider</label></div>'
    +'<div><select id="mm-'+i+'" onchange="_onModelDropdown('+i+')" class="model-row-select"><option value="'+esc(modelId)+'">'+esc(modelId||"— model —")+'</option></select>'
    +'<input id="mmc-'+i+'" placeholder="enter custom model ID" value="" class="model-row-custom" style="display:none" /><label class="model-row-label">Model</label></div>'
    +'<button class="btn btn-sm btn-danger model-row-remove" onclick="removeModelRow('+i+')">✕</button>'
    +'</div>';
}

function _populateAllModelDropdowns(){
  fetchProviderModels(function(pm){
    var rows=document.querySelectorAll(".model-row");
    rows.forEach(function(row){
      var id=row.id.replace("mrow-","");
      _populateProviderDropdown(id,pm);
    });
  });
}

function _populateProviderDropdown(id,pm){
  var provSel=Q("mp-"+id);if(!provSel)return;
  var curProv=provSel.value;
  var providers=Object.keys(pm||{}).sort();
  var h='<option value="">— provider —</option>';
  providers.forEach(function(p){
    h+='<option value="'+esc(p)+'"'+(curProv===p?" selected":"")+'>'+esc(p)+'</option>';
  });
  // Keep current value if not in list
  if(curProv&&providers.indexOf(curProv)<0){
    h+='<option value="'+esc(curProv)+'" selected>'+esc(curProv)+'</option>';
  }
  h+='<option value="__custom__">✏ custom…</option>';
  provSel.innerHTML=h;
  // Populate model dropdown for current provider
  _onProviderDropdown(id);
}

function _onProviderDropdown(id){
  var provSel=Q("mp-"+id);var modSel=Q("mm-"+id);
  if(!provSel||!modSel)return;
  var prov=provSel.value;
  var customInp=Q("mmc-"+id);
  if(prov==="__custom__"){
    // Replace select with input
    var inp=document.createElement("input");
    inp.id="mp-"+id;inp.placeholder="provider name";inp.className="prov-input-full";
    provSel.parentNode.replaceChild(inp,provSel);
    modSel.innerHTML='<option value="">type model ID below</option>';
    if(customInp){customInp.style.display="";customInp.placeholder="enter custom model ID"}
    return;
  }
  var pm=_providerModels||{};
  var models=(pm[prov]||[]).slice();
  // Include models already used by other aliases for this provider so duplicates are always selectable
  var aliasMap=getModelAliasMap();
  Object.keys(aliasMap).forEach(function(a){
    var parts=aliasMap[a].split("/");
    if(parts[0]===prov){
      var m=parts.slice(1).join("/");
      if(m&&models.indexOf(m)<0)models.push(m);
    }
  });
  var curMod=modSel.value;
  var h='<option value="">— model —</option>';
  models.forEach(function(m){
    h+='<option value="'+esc(m)+'"'+(curMod===m?" selected":"")+'>'+esc(m)+'</option>';
  });
  if(curMod&&models.indexOf(curMod)<0){
    h+='<option value="'+esc(curMod)+'" selected>'+esc(curMod)+'</option>';
  }
  h+='<option value="__custom__">✏ other…</option>';
  modSel.innerHTML=h;
  if(customInp){customInp.style.display="none";customInp.value=""}
}
function _onModelDropdown(id){
  var modSel=Q("mm-"+id);var customInp=Q("mmc-"+id);
  if(!modSel||!customInp)return;
  if(modSel.value==="__custom__"){
    customInp.style.display="";
    customInp.focus();
  }else{
    customInp.style.display="none";
    customInp.value="";
  }
}
var _modelRowCount=0;
function addModelRow(){
  var list=Q("models-list");if(!list)return;
  var existing=document.querySelectorAll(".model-row").length;
  var i=existing+_modelRowCount;_modelRowCount++;
  var div=document.createElement("div");
  div.innerHTML=modelRow(i,"","");
  list.appendChild(div.firstChild);
  // Populate dropdowns for the new row
  fetchProviderModels(function(pm){_populateProviderDropdown(i,pm)});
}
function removeModelRow(i){
  var row=Q("mrow-"+i);if(row)row.remove();
}
function saveModels(){
  var oldAliasMap=getModelAliasMap();
  var models={};
  var rows=document.querySelectorAll(".model-row");
  rows.forEach(function(row){
    var id=row.id.replace("mrow-","");
    var aliasEl=Q("ma-"+id),provEl=Q("mp-"+id),modSel=Q("mm-"+id),modCustom=Q("mmc-"+id);
    if(!aliasEl||!provEl)return;
    var alias=aliasEl.value.trim();
    var prov=provEl.value.trim();
    if(prov==="__custom__")prov="";
    // Model: prefer select value, fall back to custom input
    var mod="";
    if(modSel)mod=modSel.value.trim();
    if(mod==="__custom__")mod="";
    if(!mod&&modCustom)mod=modCustom.value.trim();
    if(!alias||!prov||!mod)return;
    // Use alias as key to allow multiple aliases for the same provider/model
    // Note: config keys are provider/model, so last alias wins if duplicated
    models[prov+"/"+mod]={alias:alias};
  });

  // Build new alias map: new alias -> "provider/modelId"
  var newAliasMap={};
  Object.keys(models).forEach(function(k){if(models[k].alias)newAliasMap[models[k].alias]=k});

  // Detect renames: old alias -> new alias (same provider/model key)
  var renames={}; // oldAlias -> newAlias
  Object.keys(oldAliasMap).forEach(function(oldAlias){
    var provModel=oldAliasMap[oldAlias];
    if(!newAliasMap[oldAlias]&&models[provModel]&&models[provModel].alias!==oldAlias){
      renames[oldAlias]=models[provModel].alias;
    }
  });

  var config=JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(D.config));
  if(!config.agents)config.agents={};
  if(!config.agents.defaults)config.agents.defaults={};
  config.agents.defaults.models=models;

  // Apply renames across the config
  if(Object.keys(renames).length>0){
    // Update agents.defaults.model
    var dm=config.agents.defaults.model;
    if(dm){
      if(typeof dm==="string"&&renames[dm]){
        config.agents.defaults.model=renames[dm];
      }else if(typeof dm==="object"){
        if(dm.primary&&renames[dm.primary])dm.primary=renames[dm.primary];
        if(dm.fallbacks&&Array.isArray(dm.fallbacks)){
          dm.fallbacks=dm.fallbacks.map(function(f){return renames[f]||f});
        }
      }
    }
    // Update agents.defaults.heartbeat.model
    var dhb=config.agents.defaults.heartbeat;
    if(dhb&&dhb.model&&renames[dhb.model])dhb.model=renames[dhb.model];

    // Update each agent
    var list=config.agents.list||[];
    list.forEach(function(agent){
      // model.primary / model.fallbacks
      var m=agent.model;
      if(m){
        if(typeof m==="string"&&renames[m]){
          agent.model=renames[m];
        }else if(typeof m==="object"){
          if(m.primary&&renames[m.primary])m.primary=renames[m.primary];
          if(m.fallbacks&&Array.isArray(m.fallbacks)){
            m.fallbacks=m.fallbacks.map(function(f){return renames[f]||f});
          }
        }
      }
      // heartbeat.model
      if(agent.heartbeat&&agent.heartbeat.model&&renames[agent.heartbeat.model]){
        agent.heartbeat.model=renames[agent.heartbeat.model];
      }
    });

    var renameList=Object.keys(renames).map(function(old){return old+" → "+renames[old]});
    toast("Renamed: "+renameList.join(", "),"info");
  }

  // Detect removed aliases and clean up dangling references
  var removedAliases=[];
  Object.keys(oldAliasMap).forEach(function(oldAlias){
    if(!newAliasMap[oldAlias]&&!renames[oldAlias])removedAliases.push(oldAlias);
  });
  if(removedAliases.length>0){
    var removedSet={};removedAliases.forEach(function(a){removedSet[a]=true});
    // Clean agents.defaults.model
    var dm2=config.agents.defaults.model;
    if(dm2){
      if(typeof dm2==="string"&&removedSet[dm2]){
        config.agents.defaults.model="";
      }else if(typeof dm2==="object"){
        if(dm2.primary&&removedSet[dm2.primary])dm2.primary="";
        if(dm2.fallbacks&&Array.isArray(dm2.fallbacks)){
          dm2.fallbacks=dm2.fallbacks.filter(function(f){return!removedSet[f]});
        }
      }
    }
    // Clean agents.defaults.heartbeat.model
    var dhb2=config.agents.defaults.heartbeat;
    if(dhb2&&dhb2.model&&removedSet[dhb2.model])dhb2.model="";
    // Clean each agent
    var list2=config.agents.list||[];
    list2.forEach(function(agent){
      var m=agent.model;
      if(m){
        if(typeof m==="string"&&removedSet[m]){agent.model=""}
        else if(typeof m==="object"){
          if(m.primary&&removedSet[m.primary])m.primary="";
          if(m.fallbacks&&Array.isArray(m.fallbacks)){
            m.fallbacks=m.fallbacks.filter(function(f){return!removedSet[f]});
          }
        }
      }
      if(agent.heartbeat&&agent.heartbeat.model&&removedSet[agent.heartbeat.model]){
        agent.heartbeat.model="";
      }
    });
    toast("Removed aliases: "+removedAliases.join(", "),"info");
  }

  api("config?defer=1",{method:"PUT",body:JSON.stringify({config:config})})
    .then(function(){_setEffectiveConfig(config);toast("Models saved","ok");_deferRestart("Models saved");closePagePanel();_refreshEffectiveUi()}).catch(function(e){toast(e.message,"err")});
}

// ── Global actions ──
function showCreateAgent(){
  var aliases=getModelAliases();
  var modelInput=aliases.length>0
    ?('<select id="na-model"><option value="">— select model —</option>'+aliases.map(function(a){return'<option value="'+esc(a)+'">'+esc(a)+'</option>'}).join("")+'</select>')
    :'<input id="na-model" placeholder="the-brain" />';
  openPagePanel("Create New Agent",
    '<div style="max-width:600px">'
    +'<div class="fg">'+tip("Agent ID","Unique identifier, lowercase with hyphens. Cannot be changed after creation.")+'<input id="na-id" placeholder="my-agent" /></div>'
    +'<div class="fg">'+tip("Display Name","Human-readable name shown in the dashboard.")+'<input id="na-name" placeholder="My Agent" /></div>'
    +'<div class="fg">'+tip("Model","Model alias to use. Define aliases in the Models panel.")+modelInput+'</div>'
    +'<div class="fg">'+tip("Workspace","Path to the directory containing this agent\'s MD files.")+'<input id="na-ws" placeholder="~/.openclaw/workspace-my-agent" /></div>'
    +'<div class="fg"><label class="perm-item perm-item-auto"><input type="checkbox" id="na-default" /> Default agent</label></div>'
    +'<div style="display:flex;gap:8px;margin-top:14px">'
    +'<button class="btn btn-accent" onclick="createAgent()">Create</button>'
    +'<button class="btn" onclick="closePagePanel()">Cancel</button></div>'
    +'</div>');
}
function createAgent(){
  var id=V("na-id").trim(),name=V("na-name").trim(),model=V("na-model").trim(),ws=V("na-ws").trim(),isDef=CK("na-default");
  if(!id){toast("Agent ID required","err");return}
  var body={id:id,name:name||id};
  if(model)body.model=model;if(ws)body.workspace=ws;if(isDef)body["default"]=true;
  api(_deferParam("agents"),{method:"POST",body:JSON.stringify(body)})
    .then(function(r){
      toast("Agent created","ok");_deferRestart("Agent created");closePagePanel();
      // Add to local data without reloading from gateway
      var newAgent=r.agent||body;
      if(!D.agents)D.agents=[];
      D.agents.push(newAgent);
      _invalidateAndRedraw();
    }).catch(function(e){toast(e.message,"err")});
}
function showRawConfig(){
  location.hash="config";
  // Show panel immediately with loading state
  openPagePanel("⚙ Configuration Editor",
    '<div style="display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;padding:60px;color:var(--tx3)"><span class="spin"></span><span style="margin-left:10px">Loading configuration…</span></div>');
  // Fetch fresh config from disk
  api("config/raw").then(function(d){
    var raw=d.raw||"{}";
    var config;
    try{config=JSON.parse(raw)}catch(e){config=D.config||{}}
    _setEffectiveConfig(config);
    _showRawConfigUI(config,d.hasPending);
  }).catch(function(){
    // Fallback to in-memory
    _showRawConfigUI(D.config||{});
  });
}

      {key:"interruptOnSpeech",type:"boolean",req:false,desc:"Interrupt on user speech. Default: true."}
    ]}

  var SECTION_ICONS={
    meta:"📋",wizard:"🧙",logging:"📝",browser:"🌐",secrets:"🔐",auth:"🔑",
    models:"🧠",agents:"🤖",tools:"🔧",bindings:"🔗",messages:"💬",commands:"⌨️",
    session:"📂",channels:"📡",gateway:"🚪",skills:"⚡",plugins:"🧩",env:"🌍",
    cron:"⏰",hooks:"🪝",canvasHost:"🎨",discovery:"📡",ui:"🎭",talk:"🎙️"
  };
