  var h='<div class="cfg-layout">';

  // Left: section list + editors
  h+='<div id="cfg-editor-main" class="flex-1">';

  // Pending changes notice
  if(hasPending){
    h+='<div class="cfg-pending-notice">⏳ You are editing staged changes that haven\'t been applied yet. Save here to update the staged config, then use "Apply &amp; Restart" to push to the gateway.</div>';
  }

  // Toolbar
  h+='<div class="cfg-toolbar">';
  h+='<button class="btn btn-sm" onclick="cfgExpandAll()" title="Expand all">▼ Expand All</button>';
  h+='<button class="btn btn-sm" onclick="cfgCollapseAll()" title="Collapse all">▶ Collapse All</button>';
  h+='<span class="flex-1"></span>';
  h+='<span id="cfg-status" class="section-desc"></span>';
  h+='</div>';
  // Action bar — validate + save grouped together
  h+='<div class="cfg-actions">';
  h+='<button class="btn btn-sm" onclick="cfgViewRawFullscreen()" class="nowrap">⛶ Raw</button>';
  h+='<button class="btn btn-sm" onclick="closePagePanel()" class="nowrap">Cancel</button>';
  h+='<button class="btn btn-sm" onclick="cfgValidate()" class="nowrap">✓ Validate</button>';
  h+='<button class="btn btn-accent btn-sm" onclick="cfgSave()" class="nowrap">Save</button>';
  h+='</div>';

  // Validation banner
  h+='<div id="cfg-validation" class="cfg-validation"></div>';

  // Sections
  sections.forEach(function(key){
    var icon=SECTION_ICONS[key]||"📄";
    var val=config[key];
    var jsonStr=JSON.stringify(val,null,2);
    var lineCount=jsonStr.split("\n").length;
    var taHeight=Math.min(Math.max(lineCount*20+20,120),500);

    h+='<div class="cfg-section" data-section="'+esc(key)+'">';
    // Header — clickable to toggle
    h+='<div class="cfg-section-head" onclick="cfgToggle(this)">';
    h+='<span class="cfg-arrow">▶</span>';
    h+='<span class="cfg-section-icon">'+icon+'</span>';
    h+='<span class="cfg-section-name">'+esc(key)+'</span>';
    h+='<span class="cfg-section-keys">'+Object.keys(val||{}).length+' keys</span>';
    h+='</div>';
    // Body — collapsed by default
    h+='<div class="cfg-section-body">';
    h+=mdToolbar("cfg-ta-"+key,{json:true});
    h+='<div class="json-editor edge-top-flat">';
    h+='<pre class="json-highlight" id="jh-'+esc(key)+'" aria-hidden="true">'+highlightJSON(jsonStr)+'</pre>';
    h+='<textarea class="code-ed cfg-ta json-ta" id="cfg-ta-'+esc(key)+'" data-key="'+esc(key)+'" data-fs-title="'+esc(key)+' (JSON)" style="min-height:'+taHeight+'px;border-top-left-radius:0;border-top-right-radius:0" spellcheck="false" oninput="cfgMarkDirty();syncHighlight(this)" onfocus="cfgShowDocs(\''+esc(key)+'\')" onscroll="syncScroll(this)">'+esc(jsonStr)+'</textarea>';
    h+='</div>';
    h+='<div class="cfg-section-err"></div>';
    h+='</div>';
    h+='</div>';
  });

  // Add new section
  h+='<div class="cfg-add-section">';
  h+='<input id="cfg-new-key" placeholder="New section key…" class="cfg-add-input" />';
  h+='<button class="btn btn-sm" onclick="cfgAddSection()">+ Add Section</button>';
  h+='</div>';

  h+='</div>'; // end main

  // Right: documentation panel (desktop only)
  h+='<div id="cfg-docs-panel" class="cfg-docs-panel">';
  h+='<div class="cfg-docs-box">';
  h+='<div class="cfg-docs-label">Documentation</div>';
  h+='<div id="cfg-docs-content" class="cfg-docs-content">Click on a section to view its documentation.</div>';
  h+='</div></div>';

  h+='</div>'; // end flex container

  // Update the already-open page panel body (don't re-call openPagePanel to avoid flicker)
  var pb=document.getElementById("page-panel-body");
  if(pb)pb.innerHTML=h;

  // Store docs reference for later
  window._cfgSectionDocs=SECTION_DOCS;
}

// ── Config editor helpers ──
function cfgToggle(headEl){
  var body=headEl.nextElementSibling;
  var arrow=headEl.querySelector(".cfg-arrow");
  if(body.style.display==="none"){
    body.style.display="block";
    if(arrow)arrow.style.transform="rotate(90deg)";
    headEl.style.borderRadius="var(--radius) var(--radius) 0 0";
    // Auto-focus textarea
    var ta=body.querySelector("textarea");
    if(ta){var key=ta.getAttribute("data-key");if(key)cfgShowDocs(key)}
  }else{
    body.style.display="none";
    if(arrow)arrow.style.transform="";
    headEl.style.borderRadius="var(--radius)";
  }
}
function cfgExpandAll(){
  document.querySelectorAll(".cfg-section-body").forEach(function(b){b.style.display="block"});
  document.querySelectorAll(".cfg-arrow").forEach(function(a){a.style.transform="rotate(90deg)"});
  document.querySelectorAll(".cfg-section-head").forEach(function(h){h.style.borderRadius="var(--radius) var(--radius) 0 0"});
}
function cfgCollapseAll(){
  document.querySelectorAll(".cfg-section-body").forEach(function(b){b.style.display="none"});
  document.querySelectorAll(".cfg-arrow").forEach(function(a){a.style.transform=""});
  document.querySelectorAll(".cfg-section-head").forEach(function(h){h.style.borderRadius="var(--radius)"});
}
function cfgShowDocs(key){
  var el=document.getElementById("cfg-docs-content");
  if(!el)return;
  var doc=(window._cfgSectionDocs||{})[key];
  if(!doc){el.innerHTML='<span class="section-desc">No documentation available for \' '+esc(key)+'\'.</span>';return}
  var h='';
  h+='<div class="cfg-doc-desc">'+esc(doc.desc)+'</div>';
  h+='<div class="mb-md">';
  if(doc.required){
    h+='<span class="cfg-doc-badge required">REQUIRED SECTION</span>';
  }else{
    h+='<span class="cfg-doc-badge optional">OPTIONAL SECTION</span>';
  }
  h+='</div>';
  if(doc.matchOrder){
    h+='<div class="cfg-doc-note">'+esc(doc.matchOrder)+'</div>';
  }
  if(doc.fields&&doc.fields.length>0){
    h+='<div class="cfg-doc-props-title">Properties</div>';
    doc.fields.forEach(function(f){
      var reqColor=f.req?'var(--red)':'var(--tx3)';
      var reqLabel=f.req?'required':'optional';
      h+='<div class="cfg-doc-prop">';
      h+='<div class="cfg-doc-prop-head">';
      h+='<code class="cfg-doc-prop-key">'+esc(f.key)+'</code>';
      h+='<span class="cfg-doc-prop-type">'+esc(f.type)+'</span>';
      h+='<span class="cfg-doc-prop-req" style="color:'+reqColor+';border:1px solid '+reqColor+'">'+reqLabel+'</span>';
      h+='</div>';
      h+='<div class="cfg-doc-prop-desc">'+esc(f.desc)+'</div>';
      h+='</div>';
    });
  }
  el.innerHTML=h;
}
// ── JSON syntax highlighting ──
function highlightJSON(str){
  // Escape HTML first, then apply token coloring
  var h=str.replace(/&/g,"&amp;").replace(/</g,"&lt;").replace(/>/g,"&gt;");
  // Strings (keys and values)
  h=h.replace(/"(?:[^"\\]|\\.)*"/g,function(m){
    // Check if it's a key (followed by :) — we'll handle that in a second pass
    return '<span class="jh-str">'+m+'</span>';
  });
  // Numbers
  h=h.replace(/\b(-?\d+\.?\d*(?:[eE][+-]?\d+)?)\b/g,'<span class="jh-num">$1</span>');
  // Booleans and null
  h=h.replace(/\b(true|false|null)\b/g,'<span class="jh-bool">$1</span>');
  // Now distinguish keys from string values: a key is a string followed by whitespace and colon
  h=h.replace(/<span class="jh-str">("(?:[^"\\]|\\.)*")<\/span>(\s*:)/g,'<span class="jh-key">$1</span>$2');
  // Braces and brackets
  h=h.replace(/([{}\[\]])/g,'<span class="jh-brace">$1</span>');
  return h;
}
function syncHighlight(ta){}
function syncScroll(ta){}

// ── Markdown / code toolbar ──
function isMobileView(){return window.innerWidth<=900}
function mdToolbar(targetId,opts){
  opts=opts||{};
  var json=opts.json;
  var h='<div class="md-toolbar">';
  if(!json){
    h+='<button class="md-tb-btn" data-tip="Bold" onclick="mdAction(\'bold\',\''+targetId+'\')"><b>B</b></button>';
    h+='<button class="md-tb-btn" data-tip="Italic" onclick="mdAction(\'italic\',\''+targetId+'\')"><i>I</i></button>';
    h+='<button class="md-tb-btn" data-tip="Code" onclick="mdAction(\'code\',\''+targetId+'\')"><code>`</code></button>';
    h+='<button class="md-tb-btn" data-tip="Code block" onclick="mdAction(\'codeblock\',\''+targetId+'\')">```</button>';
    h+='<span class="md-tb-sep"></span>';
    h+='<button class="md-tb-btn" data-tip="Heading" onclick="mdAction(\'heading\',\''+targetId+'\')">H</button>';
    h+='<button class="md-tb-btn" data-tip="List" onclick="mdAction(\'list\',\''+targetId+'\')">•</button>';
    h+='<button class="md-tb-btn" data-tip="Link" onclick="mdAction(\'link\',\''+targetId+'\')">🔗</button>';
    h+='<span class="md-tb-sep"></span>';
  }else{
    h+='<button class="md-tb-btn" data-tip="Format JSON" onclick="mdAction(\'jsonformat\',\''+targetId+'\')">{ }</button>';
    h+='<span class="md-tb-sep"></span>';
  }
  // Fullscreen toggle (always present)
  h+='<button class="md-tb-btn" data-tip="Fullscreen" onclick="openFsEditorFrom(\''+targetId+'\','+(json?'true':'false')+')">⛶</button>';
  h+='</div>';
  return h;
}
function mdAction(action,targetId){
  var ta=Q(targetId);if(!ta)return;
  var s=ta.selectionStart,e=ta.selectionEnd;
  var val=ta.value,sel=val.substring(s,e);
  var before=val.substring(0,s),after=val.substring(e);
  var ins="",cursorOff=0;
  switch(action){
    case"bold":ins="**"+(sel||"text")+"**";cursorOff=sel?ins.length:2;break;
    case"italic":ins="_"+(sel||"text")+"_";cursorOff=sel?ins.length:1;break;
    case"code":ins="`"+(sel||"code")+"`";cursorOff=sel?ins.length:1;break;
    case"codeblock":ins="\n```\n"+(sel||"code")+"\n```\n";cursorOff=sel?ins.length:5;break;
    case"heading":ins="## "+(sel||"Heading");cursorOff=ins.length;break;
    case"list":
      if(sel){ins=sel.split("\n").map(function(l){return"- "+l}).join("\n");cursorOff=ins.length}
      else{ins="- item";cursorOff=ins.length}
      break;
    case"link":ins="["+(sel||"text")+"](url)";cursorOff=sel?ins.length-1:1;break;
    case"jsonformat":
      try{var parsed=JSON.parse(ta.value);ta.value=JSON.stringify(parsed,null,2);if(ta.oninput)ta.oninput()}catch(ex){toast("Invalid JSON — cannot format","err")}
      return;
    default:return;
  }
  ta.value=before+ins+after;
  ta.focus();
  ta.selectionStart=s+cursorOff;ta.selectionEnd=s+cursorOff;
  // Trigger input event for any listeners (e.g. syncHighlight)
  if(ta.oninput)ta.oninput();
}

// ── Fullscreen editor overlay ──
var _fsEditorCtx=null;
var _fsDirectCb=null;
function openFsEditorFrom(targetId,isJson){
  var src=Q(targetId);if(!src)return;
  var title=src.getAttribute("data-fs-title")||src.getAttribute("placeholder")||"Editor";
  _fsEditorCtx={srcId:targetId,isJson:!!isJson};
  _fsDirectCb=null;
  _buildFsOverlay(title,src.value,!!isJson);
}
function openFsEditorDirect(title,content,isJson,onSave){
  _fsEditorCtx=null;
  _fsDirectCb=onSave||null;
  _buildFsOverlay(title,content,!!isJson);
}
function _buildFsOverlay(title,content,isJson){
  var ov=document.createElement("div");
  ov.className="fs-editor-overlay";ov.id="fs-editor-overlay";
  var h='<div class="fs-editor-head"><h3>'+esc(title)+'</h3><div class="flex-row">';
  h+='<button class="btn btn-sm" onclick="closeFsEditor(false)">Cancel</button>';
  h+='<button class="btn btn-sm btn-accent" onclick="closeFsEditor(true)">✓ Done</button>';
  h+='</div></div>';
  h+='<div class="fs-editor-body">';
  if(isJson){
    h+=mdToolbar("fs-editor-ta",{json:true});
    h+='<div class="json-editor edge-top-flat fill-grid">';
    h+='<pre class="json-highlight" id="fs-editor-jh" aria-hidden="true">'+highlightJSON(content)+'</pre>';
    h+='<textarea class="json-ta" id="fs-editor-ta" data-key="fs-editor" spellcheck="false" oninput="syncHighlight(this)" onscroll="syncScroll(this)">'+esc(content)+'</textarea>';
    h+='</div>';
  }else{
    h+=mdToolbar("fs-editor-ta");
    h+='<textarea id="fs-editor-ta" spellcheck="false" style="font-family:\'SF Mono\',\'Fira Code\',monospace;font-size:var(--fs-mono);line-height:1.7;padding:16px;border-top-left-radius:0;border-top-right-radius:0">'+esc(content)+'</textarea>';
  }
  h+='</div>';
  ov.innerHTML=h;
  document.body.appendChild(ov);
  var ta=Q("fs-editor-ta");
  if(ta)setTimeout(function(){ta.focus()},50);
}
function closeFsEditor(save){
  var ov=Q("fs-editor-overlay");if(!ov)return;
  if(save){
    var doneBtn=ov.querySelector(".btn-accent");
    if(doneBtn){doneBtn.disabled=true;doneBtn.textContent="⏳ Saving…"}
  }
  if(save&&_fsEditorCtx){
    var src=Q(_fsEditorCtx.srcId);
    var fsTa=Q("fs-editor-ta");
    if(src&&fsTa){
      src.value=fsTa.value;
      var ev=new Event("input",{bubbles:true});
      src.dispatchEvent(ev);
    }
  }
  if(save&&_fsDirectCb){
    var fsTa2=Q("fs-editor-ta");
    if(fsTa2){
      // Don't remove overlay yet — let the callback handle it after save completes
      var cb=_fsDirectCb;
      _fsDirectCb=null;
      _fsEditorCtx=null;
      cb(fsTa2.value);
      return; // overlay stays open until callback's API call finishes
    }
  }
  ov.remove();
  _fsEditorCtx=null;
  _fsDirectCb=null;
}
function _closeFsOverlay(){
  var ov=Q("fs-editor-overlay");if(ov)ov.remove();
}

// ── Pinch-zoom prevention (skip map canvas — it handles its own pinch) ──
document.addEventListener("gesturestart",function(e){
  if(e.target&&e.target.closest&&e.target.closest(".map-canvas"))return;
  e.preventDefault();
},{passive:false});
document.addEventListener("gesturechange",function(e){
  if(e.target&&e.target.closest&&e.target.closest(".map-canvas"))return;
  e.preventDefault();
},{passive:false});
document.addEventListener("gestureend",function(e){
  if(e.target&&e.target.closest&&e.target.closest(".map-canvas"))return;
  e.preventDefault();
},{passive:false});
// Prevent two-finger zoom on touch devices (except on map canvas)
var _lastTouchEnd=0;
document.addEventListener("touchend",function(e){
  var now=Date.now();
  if(now-_lastTouchEnd<=300&&e.target&&e.target.tagName!=="TEXTAREA"&&e.target.tagName!=="INPUT"){e.preventDefault()}
  _lastTouchEnd=now;
},{passive:false});
document.addEventListener("touchstart",function(e){
  if(e.touches.length>1){
    if(e.target&&e.target.closest&&e.target.closest(".map-canvas"))return;
    e.preventDefault();
  }
},{passive:false});

// Auto-fullscreen textareas on mobile when they have data-fs-title
document.addEventListener("focus",function(e){
  if(!isMobileView())return;
  var t=e.target;
  if(!t||t.tagName!=="TEXTAREA")return;
  if(!t.getAttribute("data-fs-title"))return;
  // Don't re-open if already in fullscreen
  if(Q("fs-editor-overlay"))return;
  // Small delay to let the modal finish rendering
  setTimeout(function(){openFsEditorFrom(t.id,t.classList.contains("json-ta"))},120);
},true);
function cfgMarkDirty(){
  var el=document.getElementById("cfg-status");
  if(el)el.innerHTML='<span class="health-warn">● Unsaved changes</span>';
  // Live JSON syntax check on the focused textarea
  var active=document.activeElement;
  if(active&&active.classList.contains("cfg-ta")){
    var sectionBody=active.closest(".cfg-section-body");
    var errEl=sectionBody?sectionBody.querySelector(".cfg-section-err"):null;
    try{JSON.parse(active.value);if(errEl){errEl.style.display="none";errEl.textContent=""}}
    catch(e){if(errEl){errEl.style.display="block";errEl.textContent="JSON syntax error: "+e.message}}
  }
}
function cfgAddSection(){
  var keyEl=Q("cfg-new-key");if(!keyEl)return;
  var key=keyEl.value.trim();
  if(!key){toast("Enter a section key","err");return}
  if(document.querySelector('.cfg-ta[data-key="'+key+'"]')){toast("Section '"+key+"' already exists","err");return}
  // Rebuild with new section
  var config=cfgAssemble();
  if(!config)return;
  config[key]={};
  _setEffectiveConfig(config);
  showRawConfig();
  toast("Section '"+key+"' added","ok");
}
function cfgAssemble(){
  var config={};
  var tas=document.querySelectorAll(".cfg-ta");
  var hasError=false;
  tas.forEach(function(ta){
    var key=ta.getAttribute("data-key");
    // Error element is a sibling of .json-editor, inside .cfg-section-body
    var sectionBody=ta.closest(".cfg-section-body");
    var errEl=sectionBody?sectionBody.querySelector(".cfg-section-err"):null;
    try{
      config[key]=JSON.parse(ta.value);
      if(errEl){errEl.style.display="none";errEl.textContent=""}
    }catch(e){
      hasError=true;
      if(errEl){errEl.style.display="block";errEl.textContent="JSON syntax error in \""+key+"\": "+e.message}
      // Expand the section so user can see the error
      if(sectionBody)sectionBody.style.display="block";
      var head=sectionBody?sectionBody.previousElementSibling:null;
      if(head){var arrow=head.querySelector(".cfg-arrow");if(arrow)arrow.style.transform="rotate(90deg)";head.style.borderRadius="var(--radius) var(--radius) 0 0"}
    }
  });
  if(hasError){toast("Fix JSON errors before proceeding","err");return null}
  return config;
}
function cfgViewRawFullscreen(){
  var config=cfgAssemble();
  if(!config)return;
  var raw=JSON.stringify(config,null,2);
  openFsEditorDirect("Raw Configuration (Full JSON)",raw,true,function(newVal){
    try{
      var parsed=JSON.parse(newVal);
      api("config?defer=1",{method:"PUT",body:JSON.stringify({raw:newVal})}).then(function(r){
        _closeFsOverlay();
        if(r.error){toast(r.error,"err");return}
        _setEffectiveConfig(parsed);
        showRawConfig();
        _refreshEffectiveUi();
        toast("Config saved","ok");
        _deferRestart("Config saved");
      }).catch(function(e){_closeFsOverlay();toast("Save failed: "+e.message,"err")});
    }catch(e){_closeFsOverlay();toast("Invalid JSON: "+e.message,"err")}
  });
}
function cfgValidate(){
  var config=cfgAssemble();
  if(!config)return;
  var banner=document.getElementById("cfg-validation");
  if(banner){banner.style.display="block";banner.innerHTML='<div class="cfg-validation-box validating section-desc"><span class="spin"></span> Validating…</div>'}
  api("config/validate",{method:"POST",body:JSON.stringify({config:config})}).then(function(r){
    if(!banner)return;
    var h='';
    if(r.errors&&r.errors.length>0){
      h+='<div class="cfg-validation-box errors">';
      h+='<div class="oc-banner-title limit">ERRORS</div>';
      r.errors.forEach(function(e){h+='<div class="val-err">• '+esc(e)+'</div>'});
      h+='</div>';
    }
    if(r.warnings&&r.warnings.length>0){
      h+='<div class="cfg-validation-box warnings">';
      h+='<div class="cfg-validation-title warnings">WARNINGS</div>';
      r.warnings.forEach(function(w){h+='<div class="cfg-validation-item warning">• '+esc(w)+'</div>'});
      h+='</div>';
    }
    if(r.cliValidation){
      h+='<div class="cfg-validation-box cli">';
      h+='<div class="cfg-validation-title cli">CLI CHECK</div>';
      h+='<pre class="cfg-validation-pre">'+esc(r.cliValidation)+'</pre>';
      h+='</div>';
    }
    if(r.valid&&(!r.warnings||r.warnings.length===0)){
      h='<div class="cfg-validation-box success">✓ Configuration is valid</div>';
    }
    banner.innerHTML=h;
  }).catch(function(e){
    if(banner)banner.innerHTML='<div class="cfg-validation-box error-single health-err">Validation failed: '+esc(e.message)+'</div>';
  });
}
function cfgSave(){
  var config=cfgAssemble();
  if(!config)return;
  var banner=document.getElementById("cfg-validation");
  var statusEl=document.getElementById("cfg-status");
  if(statusEl)statusEl.textContent="";
  _lockProgress();

  function done(){_unlockProgress()}

  function doSaveOnly(){
    api("config?defer=1",{method:"PUT",body:JSON.stringify({config:config}),_quiet:true}).then(function(){
      _setEffectiveConfig(config);
      _refreshEffectiveUi();
      _refreshToolRegistry();
      done();
      toast("Config saved","ok");
      _deferRestart("Config saved");
      if(statusEl)statusEl.innerHTML='<span class="cfg-status-saved">✓ Saved</span>';
      load();
    }).catch(function(e){
      done();
      toast("Save failed: "+e.message,"err");
    });
  }

  api("config/validate",{method:"POST",body:JSON.stringify({config:config}),_quiet:true}).then(function(r){
    if(r.errors&&r.errors.length>0){
      done();
      if(banner){
        banner.style.display="block";
        var h='<div class="cfg-validation-box errors">';
        h+='<div class="oc-banner-title limit">Cannot save — fix these errors first:</div>';
        r.errors.forEach(function(e){h+='<div class="val-err">• '+esc(e)+'</div>'});
        h+='</div>';
        banner.innerHTML=h;
      }
      toast("Fix validation errors before saving","err");
      return;
    }
    doSaveOnly();
  }).catch(function(){
    doSaveOnly();
  });
}
function restartGateway(){
  if(!confirm("Restart the OpenClaw gateway?"))return;
  _doRestart();
}
function _doRestart(){
  _lockProgress();
  _hideRestartBanner();
  _showRestartOverlay();
  // The restart API call will likely fail (gateway goes down) — that's expected
  api("config/restart",{method:"POST",_quiet:true}).catch(function(){});
  // Always wait for gateway to come back regardless of API response
  _waitForGateway(function(){
    _unlockProgress();
    _hideRestartOverlay();
    toast("Gateway restarted","ok");
    _refreshToolRegistry();
    load();
  });
}
var _restartCooldownMs=5000; // 5 second initial cooldown before polling
function _showRestartOverlay(){
  if(Q("restart-overlay"))return;
  var ov=document.createElement("div");ov.id="restart-overlay";
  ov.className="restart-overlay";
  ov.innerHTML='<div class="restart-overlay-inner">' 
    +'<div class="restart-overlay-icon">⚙</div>'
    +'<div class="restart-overlay-title">Restarting Gateway</div>'
    +'<div class="restart-overlay-desc">The gateway is restarting. Please wait while it comes back online. This usually takes a few seconds.</div>'
    +'<div id="restart-status" class="restart-overlay-status">⏳ Shutting down…</div>'
    +'<div id="restart-countdown" class="restart-overlay-countdown"></div>'
    +'</div>';
  document.body.appendChild(ov);
}
function _hideRestartOverlay(){
  var ov=Q("restart-overlay");if(ov)ov.remove();
}
function _updateRestartStatus(msg,color){
  var el=Q("restart-status");if(el){el.textContent=msg;if(color)el.style.color=color}
}
function _waitForGateway(cb){
  var attempts=0,maxAttempts=30;
  var badge=Q("gw-status");
  if(badge){badge.className="gw-badge";badge.textContent="⏳ Reconnecting…"}
  // Initial cooldown — wait before starting to poll
  var cooldown=Math.ceil(_restartCooldownMs/1000);
  var cdEl=Q("restart-countdown");
  var cdInterval=setInterval(function(){
    cooldown--;
    if(cdEl)cdEl.textContent="Starting reconnect in "+cooldown+"s…";
    if(cooldown<=0)clearInterval(cdInterval);
  },1000);
  if(cdEl)cdEl.textContent="Starting reconnect in "+cooldown+"s…";
  setTimeout(function(){
    clearInterval(cdInterval);
    if(cdEl)cdEl.textContent="";
    _updateRestartStatus("⏳ Reconnecting…","#ffaa00");
    var poll=setInterval(function(){
      attempts++;
      if(Q("restart-status")){
        _updateRestartStatus("⏳ Reconnecting… (attempt "+attempts+"/"+maxAttempts+")","#ffaa00");
      }
      api("overview",{_quiet:true}).then(function(d){
        clearInterval(poll);
        D=d;
        _updateRestartStatus("✓ Gateway is back online!","#00d68f");
        if(badge){badge.className="gw-badge ok";badge.textContent="● Gateway Online"}
        setTimeout(function(){if(cb)cb()},600);
      }).catch(function(){
        if(attempts>=maxAttempts){
          clearInterval(poll);
          _updateRestartStatus("✗ Gateway did not come back","#ff4757");
          if(badge){badge.className="gw-badge err";badge.textContent="○ Gateway Unreachable"}
          toast("Gateway did not come back after restart","err");
          setTimeout(function(){_hideRestartOverlay()},2000);
        }
      });
    },1500);
  },_restartCooldownMs);
}
var _progressLocked=false;
function _showProgress(){var el=Q("progress-bar");if(el)el.classList.add("active")}
function _hideProgress(){if(_progressLocked)return;var el=Q("progress-bar");if(el)el.classList.remove("active")}
function _lockProgress(){_progressLocked=true;_showProgress()}
function _unlockProgress(){_progressLocked=false;_hideProgress()}

// ── Deferred restart system ──
// Instead of triggering a gateway restart after every config change,
// changes are staged server-side and the user can apply them all at once.
var _pendingChangeCount=0;

function _deferRestart(description,suppressToast){
  _pendingChangeCount++;
  _showPendingBanner();
  if(!suppressToast)toast(description||"Change staged","ok");
}

function _showPendingBanner(){
  var existing=Q("pending-changes-banner");
  if(existing){
    // Update the count
    var countEl=existing.querySelector(".pending-count");
    if(countEl)countEl.textContent=_pendingChangeCount;
    return;
  }
  var b=document.createElement("div");b.id="pending-changes-banner";
  b.className="oc-banner bottom pending-bg";
  b.innerHTML='<div class="oc-banner-body">'
    +'<span class="pending-icon">⏳</span> '
    +'<span class="pending-count">'+_pendingChangeCount+'</span> pending change(s) — gateway restart required to apply'
    +'</div>'
    +'<div class="oc-banner-actions">'
    +'<button class="btn-banner primary" onclick="_commitAndRestart()">Apply &amp; Restart</button>'
    +'<button class="btn-banner ghost" onclick="_discardPending()">Discard</button>'
    +'</div>';
  document.body.appendChild(b);
}

function _hidePendingBanner(){
  var el=Q("pending-changes-banner");if(el)el.remove();
  _pendingChangeCount=0;
}

function _commitAndRestart(){
  _hidePendingBanner();
  _lockProgress();
  _showRestartOverlay();
  api("config/commit",{method:"POST"}).then(function(r){
    if(r.ok){
      _waitForGateway(function(){
        _unlockProgress();
        _hideRestartOverlay();
        load();
      });
    }else{
      _unlockProgress();
      _hideRestartOverlay();
      toast(r.error||"Nothing to commit","err");
    }
  }).catch(function(e){
    // Commit wrote to disk → gateway is restarting → API call may fail
    _waitForGateway(function(){
      _unlockProgress();
      _hideRestartOverlay();
      load();
    });
  });
}

function _discardPending(){
  api("config/pending",{method:"DELETE",_quiet:true}).then(function(){
    _hidePendingBanner();
    _pluginsCache=null;
    _skillsCache={};
    _globalSkillsCache=null;
    toast("Pending changes discarded","ok");
    api("overview?fast=1",{_quiet:true}).then(function(d){
      D.agents=d.agents||D.agents;
      D.bindings=d.bindings||[];
      if(d.config)_setEffectiveConfig(d.config);
      else if(d.channels)D.channels=d.channels;
      _refreshEffectiveUi();
      if(Q("channels-body"))renderChannelsPage();
      if(Q("plugins-body"))renderPluginsPage();
      if(Q("global-skills-body"))renderGlobalSkillsPage();
      if(drawerAgent&&drawerTab==="tools")renderDrawer();
    }).catch(function(){});
    load();
  }).catch(function(){
    _hidePendingBanner();
  });
}

// Check for pending changes on load (e.g. after page refresh)
function _checkPendingOnLoad(){
  api("config/pending",{_quiet:true}).then(function(r){
    if(r.hasPending){
      _pendingChangeCount=r.changeCount;
      _showPendingBanner();
    }
  }).catch(function(){});
}

// Helper: append ?defer=1 to an API path
function _deferParam(path){
  return path+(path.indexOf("?")>-1?"&":"?")+"defer=1";
}

function _showRestartBanner(){
  // Legacy: immediate restart (used only for explicit restart button)
  _lockProgress();
  _hideRestartBanner();
  _showRestartOverlay();
  _waitForGateway(function(){
    _unlockProgress();
    _hideRestartOverlay();
    load();
  });
}
function _hideRestartBanner(){var el=Q("restart-banner");if(el)el.remove()}

// ── Model limit detection and banner ──
var _modelLimitActive=false;
var _modelLimitExpiry=null;

function _isRateLimitError(msg){
  if(!msg)return false;
  var lower=msg.toLowerCase();
  return lower.indexOf("usage limit")>-1
    ||lower.indexOf("rate limit")>-1
    ||lower.indexOf("rate_limit")>-1
    ||lower.indexOf("quota exceeded")>-1
    ||lower.indexOf("too many requests")>-1
    ||lower.indexOf("429")>-1
    ||lower.indexOf("try again in")>-1
    ||lower.indexOf("failovererror")>-1
    ||lower.indexOf("invalid api key")>-1
    ||lower.indexOf("invalid.*key")>-1
    ||lower.indexOf("unauthorized")>-1
    ||lower.indexOf("authentication")>-1;
}

function _parseRetryMinutes(msg){
  var m=msg.match(/try again in\s*~?(\d+)\s*min/i);
  if(m)return parseInt(m[1],10);
  m=msg.match(/retry.after.*?(\d+)/i);
  if(m)return Math.ceil(parseInt(m[1],10)/60);
  return null;
}

function _showModelLimitBanner(errMsg){
  _modelLimitActive=true;
  var mins=_parseRetryMinutes(errMsg);
  if(mins)_modelLimitExpiry=Date.now()+mins*60000;
  else _modelLimitExpiry=null;

  // Update gateway status badge
  var badge=Q("gw-status");
  if(badge){badge.className="gw-badge err";badge.textContent="⚠ Model Limit Hit"}

  // Show persistent banner
  var existing=Q("model-limit-banner");
  if(existing)existing.remove();
  var b=document.createElement("div");b.id="model-limit-banner";
  b.className="oc-banner top limit-bg";
  var timeStr=mins?("Try again in ~"+mins+" minutes."):"Try again later or switch models.";
  b.innerHTML='<div style="flex:1;min-width:200px">'
    +'<div class="oc-banner-title limit">⚠ Model Usage Limit Reached</div>'
    +'<div class="oc-banner-subtitle">'+esc(errMsg.replace(/^FailoverError:\s*/i,""))+'</div>'
    +'<div class="oc-banner-hint">'+timeStr+' Sessions are blocked until the limit resets.</div>'
    +'</div>'
    +'<div class="oc-banner-actions">'
    +'<button class="btn-banner limit-primary" onclick="showModels()">Switch Models</button>'
    +'<button class="btn-banner limit-ghost" onclick="showLogs()">View Logs</button>'
    +'<button class="btn-banner ghost" onclick="_hideModelLimitBanner()">Dismiss</button>'
    +'</div>';
  document.body.prepend(b);

  // Auto-dismiss when expiry passes
  if(mins){
    setTimeout(function(){_hideModelLimitBanner()},mins*60000+5000);
  }
}

function _hideModelLimitBanner(){
  _modelLimitActive=false;
  _modelLimitExpiry=null;
  var el=Q("model-limit-banner");if(el)el.remove();
  // Restore gateway badge
  var badge=Q("gw-status");
  if(badge&&badge.textContent.indexOf("Limit")>-1){
    badge.className="gw-badge ok";badge.textContent="● Gateway Online";
  }
}

// ── Tooltip wiring ──
(function(){
  var tf=document.getElementById("tip-float");
  if(!tf)return;
  document.addEventListener("mouseover",function(e){
    var el=e.target.closest?e.target.closest("[data-tip]"):null;
    if(!el){tf.style.display="none";return}
    tf.textContent=el.getAttribute("data-tip");
    tf.style.display="block";
    var z=parseFloat(getComputedStyle(document.body).zoom)||1;
    var r=el.getBoundingClientRect();
    var top=(r.top/z)-tf.offsetHeight-8;
    if(top<8)top=(r.bottom/z)+8;
    var left=r.left/z;
    if(left+220>window.innerWidth/z-8)left=window.innerWidth/z-228;
    tf.style.top=top+"px";tf.style.left=left+"px";
  });
  document.addEventListener("mouseout",function(e){
    var el=e.target.closest?e.target.closest("[data-tip]"):null;
    if(el)tf.style.display="none";
  });
  document.addEventListener("scroll",function(){tf.style.display="none"},{passive:true,capture:true});
})();

// ── Tasks Page ──
var _tasksCache=[];
var _calView="list"; // list only — calendar views removed
var _calAnchor=null;
var _tasksSection="flows"; // "scheduled" | "flows" — top-level tab

// Parse cron expression to human-readable string
function cronToHuman(expr){
  if(!expr)return"";
  var parts=expr.trim().split(/\s+/);
  if(parts.length<5)return expr;
  var m=parts[0],h=parts[1],dom=parts[2],mon=parts[3],dow=parts[4];
  var DNAMES=["Sun","Mon","Tue","Wed","Thu","Fri","Sat"];
  // Common patterns
  if(m==="*"&&h==="*"&&dom==="*"&&mon==="*"&&dow==="*")return"Every minute";
  if(m.match(/^\*\/\d+$/)&&h==="*"&&dom==="*"&&mon==="*"&&dow==="*")return"Every "+m.split("/")[1]+" minutes";
  if(m==="0"&&h==="*"&&dom==="*"&&mon==="*"&&dow==="*")return"Every hour (on the hour)";
  if(h.match(/^\*\/\d+$/)&&m==="0"&&dom==="*"&&mon==="*"&&dow==="*")return"Every "+h.split("/")[1]+" hours";
  if(dom==="*"&&mon==="*"&&dow==="*"&&m!=="*"&&h!=="*")return"Daily at "+h.padStart(2,"0")+":"+m.padStart(2,"0");
  if(dom==="*"&&mon==="*"&&dow!=="*"&&m!=="*"&&h!=="*"){
    var days=dow.split(",").map(function(d){
      if(d.indexOf("-")>-1){
        var range=d.split("-");
        var from=DNAMES[parseInt(range[0])]||range[0];
        var to=DNAMES[parseInt(range[1])]||range[1];
        return from+"-"+to;
      }
      return DNAMES[parseInt(d)]||d;
    }).join(", ");
    return days+" at "+h.padStart(2,"0")+":"+m.padStart(2,"0");
  }
  if(dom!=="*"&&mon==="*"&&dow==="*"&&m!=="*"&&h!=="*")return"Monthly on day "+dom+" at "+h.padStart(2,"0")+":"+m.padStart(2,"0");
  return expr;
}

var MONTHS=["Jan","Feb","Mar","Apr","May","Jun","Jul","Aug","Sep","Oct","Nov","Dec"];
var DAYS=["Sun","Mon","Tue","Wed","Thu","Fri","Sat"];

var _workflowExecsCache=[];
var _pendingFlowsCache=[];
var _flowHistoryCache=[];
var _expandedFlowId=null;

function showTasksPage(){
  location.hash="tasks";
  if(!_calAnchor)_calAnchor=new Date();
  _registeredFlowsCache=[]; // reset so it re-fetches
  _tasksLoading=true;
  openPagePanel("📋 Tasks",
    '<div id="tasks-body"><div class="loading-center"><span class="spin"></span> Loading…</div></div>');

  // Render progressively — re-render whenever any data source completes
  var loaded={tasks:false,flows:false,pending:false,history:false};
  var _rendered=false;
  function tryRender(){
    // First render as soon as pending loads (for flows tab)
    // Re-render when tasks load too (for scheduled tab)
    if(loaded.pending||loaded.tasks){
      renderTasksPanel();
      _rendered=true;
    }
  }

  api("tasks/flows/pending",{_quiet:true}).then(function(d){
    _pendingFlowsCache=d.pending||[];
    if(!Array.isArray(_pendingFlowsCache))_pendingFlowsCache=[];
    loaded.pending=true;tryRender();
  }).catch(function(){
    _pendingFlowsCache=[];
    loaded.pending=true;tryRender();
  });
  api("tasks/flows/history",{_quiet:true}).then(function(d){
    _flowHistoryCache=d.history||[];
    if(!Array.isArray(_flowHistoryCache))_flowHistoryCache=[];
    loaded.history=true;tryRender();
  }).catch(function(){
    _flowHistoryCache=[];
    loaded.history=true;tryRender();
  });
  api("tasks",{_quiet:true}).then(function(d){
    _tasksCache=d.tasks||[];
    _heartbeatsCache=d.heartbeats||[];
    _tasksLoading=false;
    loaded.tasks=true;tryRender();
  }).catch(function(){
    _tasksCache=[];_heartbeatsCache=[];
    _tasksLoading=false;
    loaded.tasks=true;tryRender();
  });
  api("tasks/flows",{_quiet:true}).then(function(d){
    _workflowExecsCache=d.flows||d.executions||[];
    if(!Array.isArray(_workflowExecsCache))_workflowExecsCache=[];
    loaded.flows=true;tryRender();
  }).catch(function(){
    _workflowExecsCache=[];
    loaded.flows=true;tryRender();
  });
}

var _heartbeatsCache=[];

function renderTasksPanel(){
  var tasks=_tasksCache;
  var el=Q("tasks-body");if(!el)return;

  // ── Top-level section tabs: Flows | Scheduled ──
  var h='<div class="tasks-section-tabs">';
  h+='<div class="tasks-section-tab'+(_tasksSection==="flows"?" active":"")+'" onclick="switchTasksSection(\'flows\')">🔄 Flows</div>';
  h+='<div class="tasks-section-tab'+(_tasksSection==="scheduled"?" active":"")+'" onclick="switchTasksSection(\'scheduled\')">📅 Scheduled</div>';
  h+='</div>';

  if(_tasksSection==="flows"){
    h+=renderFlowsSection();
  }else{
    h+=renderScheduledSection(tasks);
  }

  el.innerHTML=h;
}

function switchTasksSection(s){
  _tasksSection=s;
  renderTasksPanel();
  // If switching to scheduled and tasks haven't loaded yet, fetch them
  if(s==="scheduled"&&_tasksCache.length===0){
    api("tasks",{_quiet:true}).then(function(d){
      _tasksCache=d.tasks||[];
      _heartbeatsCache=d.heartbeats||[];
      renderTasksPanel();
    }).catch(function(){});
  }
}

// ── Flows Section ──
var _registeredFlowsCache=[];
function renderFlowsSection(){
  var h='';

  // ── Section 0: Registered Flow Definitions ──
  h+='<div class="tasks-subsection">';
  h+='<div class="tasks-subsection-header">Registered Flows</div>';
  if(_registeredFlowsCache.length===0){
    h+='<div class="section-desc">Loading…</div>';
    // Fetch flow definitions
    api("tasks/flows/definitions",{_quiet:true}).then(function(d){
      _registeredFlowsCache=d.flows||[];
      renderTasksPanel();
    }).catch(function(){_registeredFlowsCache=[];});
  }else{
    h+='<div class="tasks-list">';
    _registeredFlowsCache.forEach(function(f){
      h+=_renderRegisteredFlowCard(f);
    });
    h+='</div>';
  }
  h+='</div>';

  // Split active flows into running vs waiting
  var running=_pendingFlowsCache.filter(function(p){return p.status==="running"});
  var waiting=_pendingFlowsCache.filter(function(p){return p.status==="waiting_for_approval"});

  // ── Section 1: Active Flows (running + waiting — real-time tracking) ──
  if(_pendingFlowsCache.length>0){
    h+='<div class="tasks-subsection">';
    h+='<div class="tasks-subsection-head"><div class="tasks-subsection-header">Active Flows</div>';
    h+='<button class="btn btn-sm btn-danger" onclick="clearActiveFlows()">Clear All</button>';
    h+='</div>';
    h+='<div class="tasks-list">';
    // Show all active flows with step progress
    _pendingFlowsCache.forEach(function(p){
      h+=_renderFlowCard(p);
    });
    h+='</div></div>';
  }

  // ── Section 2: Execution History (7-day retention) ──
  h+='<div class="tasks-subsection">';
  h+='<div class="tasks-subsection-head"><div class="tasks-subsection-header">Execution History</div>';
  if(_flowHistoryCache.length>0){
    h+='<button class="btn btn-sm btn-danger" onclick="clearFlowHistory()">Clear History</button>';
  }
  h+='</div>';
  if(!_flowHistoryCache||_flowHistoryCache.length===0){
    if(running.length===0&&waiting.length===0){
      h+='<div class="empty"><div class="empty-icon">📋</div>No flows yet.<br><span class="section-desc">Define a flow in the Orchestrator tab to get started.</span></div>';
    }else{
      h+='<div class="empty"><div class="empty-icon">📋</div>No completed flows in the last 7 days</div>';
    }
  }else{
    h+='<div class="tasks-list">';
    _flowHistoryCache.forEach(function(rec){
      var badge=rec.status==="completed"?'<span class="badge badge-green">✓ Completed</span>':'<span class="badge badge-red">✗ Cancelled</span>';
      h+='<div class="task-card">';
      // Header
      h+='<div class="task-card-title-group mb-sm">';
      h+='<span class="task-card-title">'+esc(rec.flowName)+'</span>';
      h+=badge;
      h+='</div>';
      // Task description
      h+='<div class="task-card-copy">'+esc(rec.task||"")+'</div>';
      // Step pipeline
      var steps=rec.completedStepIds||[];
      if(steps.length>0){
        h+='<div class="task-flow-pipeline">';
        steps.forEach(function(sid,i){
          if(i>0)h+='<div class="task-flow-connector done"></div>';
          h+='<div class="task-flow-chip done">';
          h+='<span>✓</span><span class="task-flow-chip-label">'+esc(sid)+'</span></div>';
        });
        h+='</div>';
      }
      // Timestamps
      h+='<div class="task-meta-row">';
      h+='<span>Started: <strong>'+esc(fmtDate(rec.createdAt))+'</strong></span>';
      if(rec.completedAt)h+='<span>Finished: <strong>'+esc(fmtDate(rec.completedAt))+'</strong></span>';
      h+='</div>';
      h+='</div>';
    });
    h+='</div>';
  }
  h+='</div>';
  return h;
}

/** Render a registered flow definition card */
function _renderRegisteredFlowCard(f){
  var ownerTone=agentToneClass(f.agentId||"");
  var isOrphan=!!f.orphaned;
  var h='<div class="cron-card">';
  // Header: name+badges left, edit button right
  h+='<div class="cron-card-header">';
  h+='<div class="cron-card-left">';
  h+='<div class="cron-card-name">'+esc(f.name)+'</div>';
  h+='<div class="cron-card-badges">';
  h+='<span class="badge task-status-badge">'+f.stepCount+' steps</span>';
  var hasGate=f.steps&&f.steps.some(function(s){return s.humanIntervention});
  if(hasGate)h+='<span class="badge badge-orange">⏸ approval gate</span>';
  if(isOrphan)h+='<span class="badge badge-red">⚠ orphaned</span>';
  h+='</div>';
  h+='</div>';
  h+='<div class="cron-card-actions">';
  if(isOrphan){
    h+='<button class="btn btn-sm btn-danger" onclick="deleteOrchFlow(\''+esc(f.agentId)+'\',\''+esc(f.name)+'\')">Delete</button>';
  }else{
    h+='<button class="btn btn-sm" onclick="editFlowForAgent(\''+esc(f.agentId)+'\')">✎ Edit</button>';
  }
  h+='</div>';
  h+='</div>';
  if(f.description){
    h+='<div class="cron-card-msg">'+esc(f.description.substring(0,150))+'</div>';
  }
  // Step pipeline
  h+='<div class="task-flow-pipeline">';
  (f.steps||[]).forEach(function(s,i){
    if(i>0)h+='<div class="task-flow-connector"></div>';
    h+='<div class="task-flow-chip">';
    if(s.humanIntervention)h+='<span class="health-warn">⏸</span>';
    h+='<span class="task-flow-chip-label">'+esc(s.id)+'</span>';
    h+='<span class="task-flow-chip-agent '+agentToneClass(s.agentId||'')+'">'+esc(s.agentId)+'</span>';
    h+='</div>';
  });
  h+='</div>';
  h+='<div class="task-card-owner">Owner: <span class="'+ownerTone+'">'+esc(f.agentId)+'</span></div>';
  h+='</div>';
  return h;
}
function editFlowForAgent(agentId){
  // Close the tasks panel and open the agent drawer on the orchestrator tab
  closePagePanel();
  var agent=null;
  for(var i=0;i<D.agents.length;i++){if(D.agents[i].id===agentId){agent=D.agents[i];break}}
  if(!agent){toast("Agent not found: "+agentId,"err");return}
  openDrawer(agent,"orchestrator");
}

/** Render a single active flow card with step progress pipeline */
function _renderFlowCard(p){
  var isWaiting=p.status==="waiting_for_approval";
  var isOrphan=!!p.orphaned;
  var statusBadge=isWaiting
    ?'<span class="badge badge-orange">⏸ Awaiting Approval</span>'
    :'<span class="badge badge-blue"><span class="spin task-running-dot"></span> Running</span>';
  if(isOrphan)statusBadge='<span class="badge badge-red">⚠ Orphaned</span>';

  var h='<div class="task-card">';

  // Header: flow name + status + actions
  h+='<div class="task-card-header">';
  h+='<div class="task-card-title-group">';
  h+='<span class="task-card-title">'+esc(p.flowName)+'</span>';
  h+=statusBadge;
  h+='</div>';
  if(isWaiting){
    h+='<div class="task-card-actions">';
    h+='<button class="btn btn-sm btn-accent" onclick="dashboardApproveFlow(\''+esc(p.token||p.resumeToken)+'\',true)">✓ Approve</button>';
    h+='<button class="btn btn-sm btn-danger" onclick="dashboardApproveFlow(\''+esc(p.token||p.resumeToken)+'\',false)">Deny</button>';
    h+='</div>';
  }else{
    h+='<div class="task-card-actions">';
    var actionLabel=isOrphan?'Clear':'Cancel';
    h+='<button class="btn btn-sm btn-danger" onclick="cancelActiveFlow(\''+esc(p.token)+'\')">'+actionLabel+'</button>';
    h+='</div>';
  }
  h+='</div>';

  // Task description
  h+='<div class="task-card-copy">'+esc(p.task||"")+'</div>';

  // Step progress pipeline — visual step indicators
  var allSteps=p.allStepIds||[];
  var completed=p.completedStepIds||[];
  var waitingAt=p.waitingAtStepId||"";
  var nextIdx=p.nextStepIndex||0;

  if(allSteps.length>0){
    h+='<div class="task-flow-pipeline">';
    allSteps.forEach(function(stepId,i){
      var isDone=completed.indexOf(stepId)>-1;
      var isCurrent=i===nextIdx;
      var isWaitingHere=stepId===waitingAt&&isWaiting;
      var stateClass='';
      var icon='○';
      if(isDone){stateClass=' done';icon='✓';}
      else if(isWaitingHere){stateClass=' waiting';icon='⏸';}
      else if(isCurrent){stateClass=' active';icon='▶';}
      if(i>0)h+='<div class="task-flow-connector'+(isDone?' done':'')+'"></div>';
      h+='<div class="task-flow-chip'+stateClass+'">';
      h+='<span>'+icon+'</span><span class="task-flow-chip-label">'+esc(stepId)+'</span>';
      h+='</div>';
    });
    h+='</div>';
  }

  // Meta info with bold timestamps
  h+='<div class="task-meta-row">';
  h+='<span>Started: <strong>'+esc(fmtDate(p.createdAt))+'</strong></span>';
  h+='<span>Agent: <strong>'+esc(p.agentId)+'</strong></span>';
  if(allSteps.length>0)h+='<span>Progress: <strong>'+completed.length+'/'+allSteps.length+' steps</strong></span>';
  h+='</div>';

  h+='</div>';
  return h;
}

function dashboardApproveFlow(token,approve){
  if(!approve){
    if(!confirm("Deny this flow?"))return;
  }
  if(approve) toast("Approving…","info");
  api("tasks/flows/resume",{method:"POST",body:JSON.stringify({flowToken:token,approve:approve})})
    .then(function(r){
      if(r.error){toast(r.error,"err");return}
      if(!approve){
        toast("Flow denied","ok");
        _pendingFlowsCache=_pendingFlowsCache.filter(function(p){return(p.token||p.resumeToken)!==token});
        renderTasksPanel();
        return;
      }
      // Find the pending flow to get the session key
      var pending=_pendingFlowsCache.find(function(p){return(p.token||p.resumeToken)===token});
      var sk=pending&&pending.sessionKey;
      var agentId=pending&&pending.agentId;
      _pendingFlowsCache=_pendingFlowsCache.filter(function(p){return(p.token||p.resumeToken)!==token});
      renderTasksPanel();
      // If we have a session key, send the approval through the dashboard session API
      // This ensures the message appears in the user's chat and the agent processes it in-context
      if(sk&&agentId){
        var stepName=pending&&pending.waitingAtStepId?pending.waitingAtStepId:"the current step";
        var flowName=pending&&pending.flowName?pending.flowName:"the flow";
        var msg='[Approved from dashboard] Step "'+stepName+'" in flow "'+flowName+'" has been approved. Call run_task_flow with action="resume", flowToken="'+token+'", approve=true to continue the flow.';
        api("sessions/"+encodeURIComponent(sk)+"/message",{method:"POST",body:JSON.stringify({message:msg,agentId:agentId}),_quiet:true})
          .then(function(){toast("Flow approved — agent is executing "+stepName,"ok")})
          .catch(function(){toast("Flow approved — tell the agent to continue in chat","ok")});
      }else{
        toast("Flow approved — tell the agent to continue in chat","ok");
      }
    })
    .catch(function(e){toast(e.message||"Failed","err")});
}

function clearAllPendingFlows(){
  if(_pendingFlowsCache.length===0){toast("No pending flows","info");return}
  if(!confirm("Deny and clear all "+_pendingFlowsCache.length+" pending flow(s)?"))return;
  var tokens=_pendingFlowsCache.map(function(p){return p.token||p.resumeToken});
  var done=0,errs=0;
  tokens.forEach(function(tk){
    api("tasks/flows/resume",{method:"POST",body:JSON.stringify({flowToken:tk,approve:false}),_quiet:true})
      .then(function(){done++;checkDone()})
      .catch(function(){errs++;checkDone()});
  });
  function checkDone(){
    if(done+errs<tokens.length)return;
    _pendingFlowsCache=[];
    renderTasksPanel();
    if(errs>0)toast("Cleared "+done+", "+errs+" failed","err");
    else toast("All pending flows cleared","ok");
  }
}

function deleteAllStuckExecs(){
  var stuck=_workflowExecsCache.filter(function(ex){return ex.state==="waiting"||ex.state==="failed"});
  if(stuck.length===0){toast("No stuck or failed executions","info");return}
  if(!confirm("Delete all "+stuck.length+" stuck/failed execution(s)? This cannot be undone."))return;
  var ids=stuck.map(function(ex){return ex.flowId});
  var done=0,errs=0;
  ids.forEach(function(fid){
    api("tasks/flows/"+encodeURIComponent(fid),{method:"DELETE",_quiet:true})
      .then(function(){done++;checkDone()})
      .catch(function(){errs++;checkDone()});
  });
  function checkDone(){
    if(done+errs<ids.length)return;
    _workflowExecsCache=_workflowExecsCache.filter(function(ex){return ex.state!=="waiting"&&ex.state!=="failed"});
    renderTasksPanel();
    if(errs>0)toast("Deleted "+done+", "+errs+" failed","err");
    else toast("All stuck/failed executions deleted","ok");
  }
}

function clearFlowHistory(){
  if(_flowHistoryCache.length===0){toast("No history to clear","info");return}
  if(!confirm("Clear all execution history? This cannot be undone."))return;
  api("tasks/flows/history",{method:"DELETE"})
    .then(function(r){
      if(r.error){toast(r.error,"err");return}
      _flowHistoryCache=[];
      renderTasksPanel();
      toast("History cleared","ok");
    })
    .catch(function(e){toast(e.message||"Failed","err")});
}

function clearActiveFlows(){
  if(_pendingFlowsCache.length===0){toast("No active flows","info");return}
  if(!confirm("Clear all active flows? This will remove "+_pendingFlowsCache.length+" flow(s). Running flows will be abandoned."))return;
  api("tasks/flows/active",{method:"DELETE"})
    .then(function(r){
      if(r.error){toast(r.error,"err");return}
      _pendingFlowsCache=[];
      renderTasksPanel();
      toast("Active flows cleared","ok");
    })
    .catch(function(e){toast(e.message||"Failed","err")});
}

function cancelActiveFlow(token){
  if(!confirm("Cancel this flow? It will be moved to execution history as cancelled."))return;
  api("tasks/flows/cancel",{method:"POST",body:JSON.stringify({flowToken:token})})
    .then(function(r){
      if(r.error){toast(r.error,"err");return}
      _pendingFlowsCache=_pendingFlowsCache.filter(function(p){return p.token!==token});
      toast("Flow cancelled","ok");
      // Refresh history
      api("tasks/flows/history",{_quiet:true}).then(function(d){
        _flowHistoryCache=d.history||[];
        renderTasksPanel();
      }).catch(function(){renderTasksPanel()});
    })
    .catch(function(e){toast(e.message||"Failed","err")});
}

// ── Scheduled Section (Cron Jobs) ──
var _tasksLoading=true;
function renderScheduledSection(tasks){
  var h='';
  h+='<div class="scheduled-head">';
  h+='<div class="scheduled-title">Cron Jobs</div>';
  h+='<button class="btn btn-sm btn-accent" onclick="showCreateCronJob()">+ New Cron Job</button>';
  h+='</div>';
  if(_tasksLoading&&(!tasks||tasks.length===0)){
    h+='<div class="loading-center"><span class="spin"></span> Loading cron jobs…</div>';
  }else if(!tasks||tasks.length===0){
    h+='<div class="empty"><div class="empty-icon">⏰</div>';
    h+='No cron jobs configured.<br>';
    h+='<span class="section-desc">Cron jobs run as agent turns on a schedule via <code>openclaw cron</code>.</span><br><br>';
    h+='<button class="btn btn-accent" onclick="showCreateCronJob()">+ Create your first cron job</button></div>';
  }else{
    h+='<div class="tasks-list">';
    tasks.forEach(function(t){ h+=renderCronJobCard(t); });
    h+='</div>';
  }
  if(_heartbeatsCache.length>0){
    h+='<div class="tasks-subsection heartbeat-section">';
    h+='<div class="tasks-subsection-header">Agent Heartbeats</div>';
    h+='<div class="heartbeat-list">';
    _heartbeatsCache.forEach(function(hb){
      var enabled=hb.enabled!==false;
      var tone=agentToneClass(hb.agentId||"");
      h+='<div class="heartbeat-row'+(enabled?'':' disabled')+'">';
      h+='<div class="flex-1">';
      h+='<div class="heartbeat-name '+tone+'">'+esc(hb.agentName||hb.agentId)+'</div>';
      h+='<div class="heartbeat-meta">⏰ every '+esc(hb.interval)+(hb.model?' · 🧠 '+esc(hb.model):'')+'</div>';
      h+='</div>';
      h+='<span class="badge '+(enabled?"badge-green":"badge-red")+'">'+(enabled?"active":"disabled")+'</span>';
      h+='</div>';
    });
    h+='</div></div>';
  }
  return h;
}
function renderCronJobCard(t){
  var sched=t.schedule||{};
  var schedKind=sched.kind||(t.cron?"cron":(t.every?"interval":(t.at?"one-shot":"unknown")));
  var isOneShot=schedKind==="at";
  var scheduleLabel="";
  if(schedKind==="cron"&&(sched.expr||t.cron))scheduleLabel=cronToHuman(sched.expr||t.cron);
  else if(schedKind==="every"&&(sched.interval||t.every))scheduleLabel="every "+(sched.interval||t.every);
  else if(schedKind==="at"&&(sched.at||t.at))scheduleLabel="at "+(sched.at||t.at);
  else if(sched.expr)scheduleLabel=sched.expr;
  var sessionLabel=t.sessionTarget||t.session||"isolated";
  var payload=t.payload||{};
  var msg=payload.message||t.message||payload.systemEvent||t.systemEvent||"";
  var agentId=t.agentId||t.agent||"";
  var delivery=t.delivery||{};
  var nextRun=t.state&&t.state.nextRunAtMs?new Date(t.state.nextRunAtMs).toISOString():t.nextRun;
  var lastRun=t.state&&t.state.lastRunAtMs?new Date(t.state.lastRunAtMs).toISOString():t.lastRun;
  var tz=sched.tz||t.tz||"";
  var h='<div class="cron-card">';
  // Header row: name+badges left, buttons right (desktop), stacked (mobile)
  h+='<div class="cron-card-header">';
  h+='<div class="cron-card-left">';
  h+='<div class="cron-card-name">'+esc(t.name||t.id)+'</div>';
  h+='<div class="cron-card-badges">';
  h+='<span class="badge '+(t.enabled===false?"badge-red":"badge-green")+'">'+(t.enabled===false?"disabled":"active")+'</span>';
  if(isOneShot)h+='<span class="badge badge-muted">one-shot</span>';
  else h+='<span class="badge badge-muted">'+esc(schedKind)+'</span>';
  h+='</div>';
  h+='</div>';
  h+='<div class="cron-card-actions">';
  h+='<button class="btn btn-sm" onclick="runCronJobNow(\''+esc(t.id)+'\')">▶ Run</button>';
  h+='<button class="btn btn-sm" onclick="showEditCronJob(\''+esc(t.id)+'\')">✎ Edit</button>';
  h+='<button class="btn btn-sm" onclick="showCronJobRuns(\''+esc(t.id)+'\',\''+esc(t.name||t.id)+'\')">📋 Runs</button>';
    h+='<button class="btn btn-sm btn-danger" onclick="deleteCronJob(\''+esc(t.id)+'\',\''+esc(t.name||t.id)+'\')">Delete</button>';
  h+='</div>';
  h+='</div>';
  // Meta row
  h+='<div class="cron-card-meta">';
  if(scheduleLabel)h+='<span>⏰ '+esc(scheduleLabel)+'</span>';
  if(tz)h+='<span>🌍 '+esc(tz)+'</span>';
  h+='<span>📂 '+esc(sessionLabel)+'</span>';
  if(agentId)h+='<span>🤖 '+esc(agentId)+'</span>';
  h+='</div>';
  if(msg){
    h+='<div class="cron-card-msg">';
    h+='💬 '+esc(msg.substring(0,120));
    if(msg.length>120)h+='…';
    h+='</div>';
  }
  if(lastRun||nextRun){
    h+='<div class="cron-card-times">';
    if(lastRun)h+='<span>Last: '+esc(fmtDate(lastRun))+'</span>';
    if(nextRun)h+='<span>Next: '+esc(fmtDate(nextRun))+'</span>';
    h+='</div>';
  }
  if(delivery.mode&&delivery.mode!=="none"){
    h+='<div class="cron-card-delivery">';
    h+='<span class="cron-delivery-label">📤 Delivery</span>';
    h+='<span class="cron-delivery-sep">→</span>';
    h+='<span class="cron-delivery-value">'+esc(delivery.mode);
    if(delivery.channel)h+=' / '+esc(delivery.channel);
    h+='</span>';
    h+='</div>';
  }
  h+='</div>';
  return h;
}
